Eorlund Gray-Mane

**Eorlund Gray-Mane** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in charge of forging weapons and armor for the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") at the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge"), located behind [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"). He is married to [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane"), with whom he has three children: [Avulstein](/wiki/Skyrim:Avulstein_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Avulstein Gray-Mane"), [Olfina](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane"), and [Thorald](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane"). He is also the brother of [Vignar Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vignar_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Vignar Gray-Mane"). Though Eorlund works closely with the Companions, he does not consider himself one of them, as his main concern is continuing his family's tradition of working the Skyforge. Nevertheless, he is very knowledgeable about their traditions and customs, and provides advice and master [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") training to new members and veterans alike. During the initiation quest [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms"), Eorlund will ask you for a favor, he will reward you after [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor"), and his expertise will prove invaluable during [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead").

Like the majority of Whiterun citizens, Eorlund has an opinion on the ongoing [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), and like his family, he supports the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), though not as much as the other members of [clan Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Gray-Mane").

Eorlund works the Skyforge every day from 8am to 9pm, either forging or using the grindstone. He spends the rest of his time inside [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") with his family, either wandering around, eating, relaxing or sleeping in his room on the second floor.

Eorlund wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor") with a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He is equipped with a [Skyforge steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Sword"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Key to House Gray-Mane") to House Gray-Mane, as well as a selection of [upper-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms")**: Prove you are worthy to join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
- **[Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor")**: Claim a [Fragment of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragment_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragment of Wuuthrad") from [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn").
- **[Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead")**: Cure [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit and become Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"Got of*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *lot of steel to shape."*
:   *"Hmm?"*
:   *"I ain't much for talkin'."*
:   *"Whiterun belongs to the true sons of Skyrim now, just as it should."* **(If Stormcloaks control Whiterun)**
:   *"We Gray-Manes got just as much to be proud of as them Battle-Borns, but you won't see us with our noses in the air."*
:   *"My poor Fralia thinks Thorald's still alive, but I know better."*

Topics:

:   **Quite a forge you've got here.**
:   *"The Skyforge? Aye, my clan-fathers have worked it since the first Gray-Manes came to Whiterun. Skyforge Steel is all the Companions will use, for good reason."*

:   **Tell me about yourself.**
:   *"You blind, boy/girl? I'm a blacksmith. Any half-wit could see that."*

:   **Who are the Companions?**
:   *"By Ysmir, are you thick, or just too new to know better? The Companions are the oldest, most honored band of warriors in Skyrim. Whiterun was built around their hall, Jorrvaskr. Don't reckon they can use you. But stranger things have happened."*

    :   **Are you a Companion?**
    :   *"Why? Who says I have to be? Skyforge Steel is my art and honor. The Companions need the best, so they come to me."*

If the Stormcloaks manage to [conquer](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") Whiterun:

:   **Are you glad the Stormcloaks are in charge?**
:   *"I'm sure my brother Vignar is, since they made him Jarl after throwing Balgruuf out. Comes the end of the day, Imperials and Stormcloaks ain't much different. Both sides want to tell you how you should live your life. Guess I'd rather hear it from a real Nord than some Emperor down south."*

His goodbyes:

:   *"Hm hmm."*
:   *"We done?"*

### Conversations

*"Hrm."*

When Eorlund bumps into his wife Fralia in the evening, they will engage in conversation, although Eorlund will use fewer words than ever before:

**Fralia**: *"Eorlund, dearest, are you hungry? Would you like me to fix you something?"*
**Eorlund**: *"Hrm."*
**Fralia**: *"A venison pie, maybe? With a nice cup of mulled mead?"*
**Eorlund**: *"Hrm."*

**Fralia**: *"When will you be makin' some more jewelry, love? Some silver lockets and amulets would fetch a nice price at the stand."*
**Eorlund**: *"Hrm."*
**Fralia**: *"Wonderful, dear. Thank you."*
**Eorlund**: *"Hrm."*

### Take Up Arms

*"My name is Eorlund Gray-Mane. I work the Skyforge."*

During the quest [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms"), you will find yourself as an errand runner for the Companions. When you locate Eorlund, he will ask:

:   *"What brings you here?"*
:   **Vilkas sent me with his sword.**
:   *"I'm guessing you're the newcomer then?"*

:   :   **Does Vilkas always send newcomers on errands?**
    :   *"Oh, don't worry too much about it. They were all whelps once. They just might not like to talk about it. And don't always just do what you're told. Nobody rules anybody in the Companions."*

:   :   **I'm just doing what I'm asked.**
    :   *"That attitude would get you far, if you were some stuffy merchant or a Jarl's footstool. Around here, you'll want to learn to live your own life. Remember, nobody rules anybody in the Companions."*

Either will lead to:

:   **Someone has to be in charge, though.**
:   *"Well, I'm not sure how they've managed it, but they have. No leaders since Ysgramor. Kodlak is the Harbinger, and he's a sort of advisor for the whole group, but every man is his own. Every woman, her own."*
:   **Are you a Companion?**
:   *"Not actually a Companion myself, but none of them know how to work a forge properly, and I'm honored to serve them. My name is Eorlund Gray-Mane. I work the Skyforge. Best steel in all of Skyrim. All of Tamriel."*

Lastly, he will grab the opportunity and use your low rank to his benefit:

:   *"I have a favor to ask."*
:   **What is it?**
:   *"I've been working on a shield for Aela. My wife is in mourning and I need to get back to her soon. I'd be much obliged if you could take this to Aela for me."*

:   :   **Didn't you just tell me not to be a servant?**
    :   *"This isn't a command. Just decency. Help out an old blacksmith. I've got to get back to my work."*

:   :   **I'm happy to lend a hand.**
    :   *"That's a good man."*

He will then return to his duties. Once the quest is completed, Eorlund will offer master training in [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") with the words:

:   *"It's an honorable craft. I'll show you what I can."*

You can ask him again about the Companions, although he will be a bit insulted:

:   *"By Ysmir's beard, I ain't one for humor. You know who the Companions are. So quit your asking."*

### Proving Honor

During the quest [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor"), when you are officially initiated into the Companions, [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane") will encourage you to visit Eorlund for a better weapon. When you visit Eorlund with the request of a new weapon:

:   **I was told you would have a weapon for me.**
:   *"Yes, lad, you've been raised into the Companions, I hear. I can fashion whatever kind of weapon you want. Finest forge in Skyrim, right here before you."*

You can then choose between five weapon types:

| Weapon Type | Comment |
| --- | --- |
| [Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Sword") | *"A blade! It will be as sharp as Fralia's tongue!"* |
| [Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Dagger") | *"Ah, the sneaky type, eh? I think we can fix you right up."* |
| [Battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Battleaxe") | *"Just like Ysgramor himself."* |
| [Greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Greatsword") | *"Sure you can handle that? Ha! Of course you can."* |
| [War Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel War Axe") | *"Now that's a smart weapon. Light, strong, useful. Crack some skulls for me."* |

### Glory of the Dead

*"We take our leave."*

When you have started [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead") and returned to Whiterun, you'll find several citizens gathered around the Skyforge to pay their respects to deceased Harbinger [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane"). Naturally, Eorlund is present as well, standing next to Kodlak's body on top of the forge itself. When you arrive, you'll witness the ritual, with Eorlund asking the first question:

:   **Eorlund:** *"Who will start?"*
:   **Aela:** *"I'll do it. Before the ancient flame..."*
:   **Everyone:** *"We grieve."*
:   **Eorlund:** *"At this loss..."*
:   **Everyone:** *"We weep."*
:   **Vilkas:** *"For the fallen..."*
:   **Everyone:** *"We shout."*
:   **Farkas:** *"And for ourselves..."*
:   **Everyone:** *"We take our leave."*

After the ritual, Eorlund will watch as Aela ignites the fire under Kodlak, and people will then start to go their separate ways. Aela will gather what is left of [The Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle"), while Eorlund will seek you out and ask:

:   *"Do you have the fragments of Wuuthrad, still? I'll need to prepare them for mounting again."*

:   :   **I return them with honor. (Give fragments)**
    :   *"Don't get too flowery on me, lad/lass."*

:   :   **Here, take them. (Give fragments)**
    :   *"Careful with those. Don't want even more fragments, do we?"*

He will then make a special request:

:   *"Of course, I have a small favor to ask of you. There's another piece, that Kodlak always kept close to himself. Would you go to his chambers and bring it back for me? I'm not sure I'm the best one to go through his things."*

    :   *"Thank you. I'll be here."*
    :   *"I appreciate it."*

He will then return to his daily routines while you go through Kodlak's end table for the fragment. When you return to Eorlund, he will say:

:   *"You're back."*
:   *"Thank you. Your Shield-Siblings have withdrawn to the Underforge. I think they're waiting for you."*

He will then get to work, regardless of the hour, and keep his plans secret for the time being.

*"Just because something is, doesn't mean it must be."*

In the Underforge, the members of the Circle will be gathered around the fountain, all of them frustrated and discouraged. They all know that Kodlak died without being granted his only wish, namely to be freed of his lycanthropy so he could spend his afterlife in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Lore:Sovngarde "Lore:Sovngarde"). While they know of a way to cleanse his soul, it requires them to enter the [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb") and perform a ceremony:

**Vilkas**: *"The old man had one wish before he died. And he didn't get it. It's as simple as that."*
**Aela**: *"Being moon-born is not so much of a curse as you might think, Vilkas."*
**Vilkas**: *"That's fine for you. But he wanted to be clean. He wanted to meet Ysgramor and know the glories of Sovngarde. But all that was taken from him."*
**Aela**: *"And you avenged him."*
**Farkas**: *"Kodlak did not care for vengeance."*
**Vilkas**: *"No, Farkas, he didn't. And that's not what this is about. We should be honoring Kodlak, no matter our own thoughts on the blood."*
**Aela**: *"You're right. It's what he wanted, and he deserved to have it."*
**Vilkas**: *"Kodlak used to speak of a way to cleanse his soul, even in death. You know the legends of the Tomb of Ysgramor."*
**Aela**: *"There the souls of the Harbingers will heed the call of northern steel. We can't even enter the tomb without Wuuthrad, and it's in pieces, like it has been for a thousand years."*

At this point, Eorlund Gray-Mane will enter and say:

**Eorlund**: *"And dragons were just stories. And the elves once ruled Skyrim. Just because something is, doesn't mean it must be. The blade is a weapon. A tool. Tools are meant to be broken. And repaired."*
**Vilkas**: *"Is that? Did you repair the blade?"*
**Eorlund**: *"This is the first time I've had all the pieces, thanks to our Shield-Brother/Shield-Sister here. "The flames of a hero can reforge the shattered." The flames of Kodlak shall fuel the rebirth of Wuuthrad. And now it will take you to meet him once more."*

He will then address you personally:

:   *"As the one who bore the fragments, I think you should be the one to carry Wuuthrad into battle."*

He will then hand you the weapon and speak to the other members:

:   *"The rest of you, prepare to journey to the Tomb of Ysgramor. For Kodlak."*

He will then turn around and leave the Underforge.

When you have completed Glory of the Dead and Kodlak enjoys his afterlife in Sovngarde, a trip up to the Skyforge and Eorlund will make him tell about a strange change he has observed with the forge:

:   *"You know, since Kodlak's funeral the Skyforge feels more... awake. It's always been said that the souls of the heroes of old are what give Skyforge steel its strength. But I think the forge knows the greatness of Kodlak's soul. I can't really explain, but it feels like it's... young. I'll wager it could now forge metal the likes of which hasn't been seen since eras long forgotten. I'm eager to try."*

After completing the full Companions questline, standard "Ancient Nord" weapons from draugr can be converted into "Nord Hero" weapons by speaking to Eorlund at the Skyforge.

## Rumors

Eorlund's smithing skills are known all over Skyrim, although you will hear Whiterun citizens talk about them the most. At the local weaponry shop, [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's"), [Adrianne Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adrianne_Avenicci "Skyrim:Adrianne Avenicci") will tell you: *"I don't claim to be the best blacksmith in Whiterun. Eorlund Gray-Mane's got that honor. Man's steel is legendary. All I ask is a fair chance."* When giving you her [favor quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword_for_a_Great_Man "Skyrim:Greatsword for a Great Man"), she will mention Eorlund once again: *"Aye, that I do. I've got to, if I hope to be as good as Eorlund Gray-Mane some day. In fact, I just finished my best piece of work."* Naturally, Fralia Gray-Mane thinks highly of her husband and will tell you: *"My husband Eorlund tends the Skyforge up at Jorrvaskr, the Companions mead hall. There's no finer smith in the nine holds. You should ask him about his work. It's the only subject that'll get him talking. Well, that and maybe those stuck-up, dung-sniffing Battle-Borns."* When trying to sell her wares at the market, she will shout: *"Shiny trinkets for your good lady! All crafted by the great Eorlund Gray-Mane himself!"* She can also be seen telling [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") why she doesn't need to trade with the caravans: *"Plenty of people here that need Eorlund's craftsmanship, my dear. We've never had any reason to deal with those caravans of theirs."* She will also tell [Lillith Maiden-Loom](/wiki/Skyrim:Lillith_Maiden-Loom "Skyrim:Lillith Maiden-Loom") that Eorlund will craft a new locket in polished silver: *"Ahhh, I see. I think I know just what you need. I don't have anything like that here now, but my Eorlund - he can make you one right quick. When I get home, I'll have him start on it right away."* In Jorrvaskr, [Njada Stonearm](/wiki/Skyrim:Njada_Stonearm "Skyrim:Njada Stonearm") will tell [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor") how to hold his shield: *"If Eorlund made it, it's more likely you're gripping it wrong. Find me tomorrow and we can go over it."*

When you first enter Whiterun you can overhear Adrianne Avenicci trying to convince [Idolaf Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born") about asking Eorlund for help: *"Why don't you swallow that stubborn pride of yours and ask Eorlund Gray-Mane for help?"*, to which Idolaf will hatefully reply: *"Ha! I'd sooner bend my knee to Ulfric Stormcloak."* Due to the feud between the two clans, another Battle-Born, namely [Olfrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born") will say: *"Eorlund Gray-Mane's a stubborn fool. Our friendship ended when he turned his back on the Emperor."* However, most people outside Whiterun recognize Eorlund's skills, even young [Dorthe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dorthe "Skyrim:Dorthe") from [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), who will ask her [father](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor"): *"You really think I can be a blacksmith someday, papa? As good as Eorlund Gray-Mane?"* In [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), local blacksmith [Oengul War-Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oengul_War-Anvil "Skyrim:Oengul War-Anvil") will prove more bitter, saying: *"Everyone says Eorlund Gray-Mane is the best smith in Skyrim. I plan to change a few minds about that."* and add: *"I respect Eorlund, but he has the good fortune to work the Skyforge. Something about the fires... their steel just holds tighter."* The most prominent rumor about Eorlund occurs during the [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") quest, when most of Skyrim's upper class is gathered for a party inside the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"). At that occasion, the party guests will discuss Eorlund. One guest will comment: *"I'm not sure that it's news, but lately it seems like every blacksmith in Skyrim is out to prove that he's the equal of Eorlund Gray-Mane."* The other guest will then reply: *"It's not really a fair comparison, if you ask me. After all, Eorlund works the Skyforge. How is any smith going to compete with that?"*

## Bugs

- Two lines of dialogue were recorded for Eorlund for use during the quest [Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action"). Unfortunately, they were mistakenly attached to stage 1000 of [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"), so they can never be heard in-game:
  *"We Gray-Manes got just as much to be proud of as them Battle-Borns, but you won't see us with our noses in the air."*
  *"My poor Fralia thinks Thorald's still alive, but I know better."*
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Eorlund refers to female Companions as "lad" instead of "lass" when asking him for a weapon.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Eorlund has no sleep package, making it impossible for him to do so.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Eorlund's merchant chest is accessible via a [glitch](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Eorlund_Gray-Mane#Merchant_Chest "Skyrim talk:Eorlund Gray-Mane").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
  - Although it is accessible via a glitch, there are certain conditions on the chest: it won't contain Skyforge Steel or Wolf Armor unless you are a part of the Companions and progressed a certain length into the quest chain; and if you take everything and wait two days for it to replenish, you have to talk to Eorlund and enter his merchant menu before his stock is shown in said chest, otherwise it will stay empty.
- If in combat with him, the quest [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead") may not start properly.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Eorlund may not open at 8 in the morning, but rather 9 or 10.

# Skyrim:Erandur

Erandur

**Erandur**, once known as **Casimir**, is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") of [Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara") investigating the nightmares plaguing [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). While investigating, you will be directed to Erandur, who is also looking into the problem. This will start the quest [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare").

He wears a set of [hooded monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Monk Robes") with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") of the best possible quality and two leveled [potions of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). He also carries a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple_Key "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple Key") to [Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple"). He relies on three spells, specifically [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward"), [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), and [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"), though he also uses his mace.

## Related Quests

- **[Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare")**: Relieve the people of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") from [Vaermina](/wiki/Lore:Vaermina "Lore:Vaermina")'s curse.
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

### Waking Nightmare

Erandur can be found in the taproom of [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn"), busily reassuring the town's residents to trust in Mara:

**[Irgnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir "Skyrim:Irgnir")**: *"It's a curse! It has to be! I've got to get out of this town."*
**[Fruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Fruki "Skyrim:Fruki")**: *"Irgnir, get a hold of yourself. They're just dreams. Please tell her, Erandur."*
**Erandur**: *"Listen to your friend, Fruki. They are just dreams, my dear. I assure you that it is quite normal."*
**Irgnir**: *"It's the same dream over and over again. You think that's normal? It's evil I tell you!"*
**Fruki**: *"Erandur, she has a point. You keep telling us no harm will follow these dreams, but they must be an omen."*
**Thoring**: *"Give him a chance to speak. He's trying to help us."*
**Erandur**: *"Everyone, please. I'm doing what I can to end these nightmares. In the meantime all I ask is you remain strong and put your trust in Lady Mara."*
**Irgnir**: *"I... I will. Thank you..."*

When spoken to directly:

:   *"What troubles you, my son/daughter?"*
:   **What's wrong with everyone around here?**
:   *"The entire town is being plagued by horrible nightmares. They're in serious danger but I'm afraid there's little I can do about it."*

You then have three options to pick from:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **What could you do, anyway? Dreams aren't real.** | *"These dreams are manifestations created by the Daedric Lord Vaermina. She has an awful hunger for our memories. In return, she leaves behind nightmares, not unlike a cough marks a serious illness. I must end her terrible influence over these people before the damage becomes permanent."* |
| **Don't be ridiculous. Dreams are harmless.** | *"In any other circumstance, I'd agree with you. However, these aren't normal dreams. The Daedric Lord Vaermina's voracious hunger for memories is responsible for these visions. The nightmares are an echo of her presence as she feeds."* |
| **Then leave. This isn't your problem.** | *"Turn my back on these people when their lives could be at stake? I should say not. Those dreams are not just visions, they're a footprint left by the Daedric Lord Vaermina as she drains these people of their memories!"* |

Any option leads to:

:   **What's your plan?**
:   *"I need to return to the source of the problem, to [Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple"). Perhaps you'd be willing to assist me in that regard?"*
:   **What do you mean, "return"? You've been there?**
:   *"I've already said too much. If anyone overhears what we're saying, it could start a panic. I would simply ask that you trust me and help me end Dawnstar's nightmares."*

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **I trust you. How can I help? / I've decided to help you end the nightmares.** | *"Wonderful! My lady Mara will be quite pleased! Nightcaller Temple is only a short walk from Dawnstar. Come, we must hurry."* |
| **I can't trust you. You're hiding something.** | *"Your concerns are understandable; trust is a very difficult commodity to come by these days. I can only give you my word as a priest of Mara that my intentions are honorable."* |

If you reject helping him:

:   **Sorry, I can't.**
:   *"I understand. If you should change your mind, I'll be here."*

Once you accept the quest you can ask him about Vaermina:

:   **Who is the Daedric Lord Vaermina?**
:   *"Vaermina resides in a strange realm known as [Quagmire](/wiki/Lore:Quagmire "Lore:Quagmire")... a nightmarish land where reality shifts upon itself in seemingly impossible ways. From her citadel at the center, she reaches forth to collect our memories, leaving nothing in return apart from visions of horror and despair."*
:   **What does she do with the memories?**
:   *"Who can say? Perhaps she collects them for display like works of art in a nonsensical art gallery. Whatever the case may be, her intentions are far from benevolent."*

### Walking to the Temple

Erandur warns you of the dangers before entering

While walking towards Nightcaller Temple, Erandur will talk about the temple and the priests who lived there:

:   *"Follow me, it's this way. It feels good to finally have a chance to help these people. Helplessly watching them suffer's been difficult. The tower on that hill is our destination. People around here call it the Tower of the Dawn. I'm not familiar with the tower's history, but it was deserted for quite a long time before Nightcaller Temple was established inside. When the temple was active the priests would rarely be seen in Dawnstar. They preferred to live a solitary existence. The temple's been abandoned for decades now. Ironic isn't it... a ruin within a ruin? There's a small shrine to Mara I established inside the tower's entry hall. I was hoping to seek spiritual guidance from Her. Perhaps my prayers were answered and your reason for stumbling across Dawnstar is more than a mere coincidence."*

Before entering, he will inform you of the dangers you are about to face:

:   *"Before we enter, I must warn you about the dangers that could be lurking within. Years ago, this temple was raided by an orc war party seeking revenge... they were being plagued by nightmares just like the people of Dawnstar."*
:   **Were they successful?**
:   *"No. Knowing they could never defeat the orcs, the priests of Vaermina released what they call "The Miasma," putting everyone to sleep."*
:   **Why is it dangerous if they're asleep?**
:   *"I'm concerned that when this place is unsealed, the Miasma will dissipate and they'll awaken; both orcs and priests alike."*
:   **What does the Miasma do?**
:   *"The Miasma was created by the priests of Vaermina for their rituals. It's a gas that places the affected in a deep sleep. Because the rituals would last for months or even years, the Miasma was designed to slow down the aging process."*
:   **Is the gas dangerous?**
:   *"Sadly, yes. The longer an individual is exposed to the Miasma, the more the mind can become damaged. Those who've been under the effect of it for extended periods of time have been known to lose their minds entirely. In some cases, a few never awoke at all."*

### Nightcaller Temple

Erandur opens the way

When you enter Nightcaller Temple Erandur will walk to the back of the room and cast a spell on the back wall:

:   *"Give me just a moment, and I'll have this open."*

Once inside, he will say:

:   *"Now I can show you the source of the nightmares. Over here.
    Behold the Skull of Corruption, the source of Dawnstar's woes. We must reach the inner sanctum and destroy it. Come, there's no time to lose."*

When you reach a doorway blocked with a barrier, he will say:

:   *"Damn it. The priests must have activated this barrier when the Miasma was released."*
:   **Looks difficult to breach.**
:   *"Impossible actually. Hmm, I wonder... There may be a way to bypass the barrier, but I must check their library and confirm it can be done."*
:   **You seem to know an awful lot about this place.**
:   *"I suppose there's no point in concealing the truth any longer. My knowledge of this temple comes from personal experience. I was a priest of Vaermina."*

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **Why keep it a secret?** | *"When the orcs invaded the temple, I fled. I left my brothers and sisters here to die."* |
| **You should have told me the truth.** | *"Yes, you're right. I should have, but I didn't know what to say. When the orcs raided the temple, I fled. I left my brothers and sisters behind to die."* |
| **I knew it! You're a liar!** | *"And what would you have me say? Sorry for following the misguided teachings of a mad Divine? Sorry for stealing memories from children? Do you realize when the orcs attacked, I was only concerned with myself? I fled... and left my brothers and sisters behind to die."* |

:   *"I've spent the last few decades living in regret and seeking redemption from Mara. And by Her Benevolence, I will right my wrongs."*
:   **How can the Skull be affecting Dawnstar?**
:   *"Lore holds that the Skull of Corruption holds a constant hunger for the memories of others. The Skull has been out of touch for so long, I fear it's gained the ability to reach out on its own and try to feed. What it does with these memories is just conjecture and an argument for scholars and historians to this very day."*
:   *"I still have my key to the library. Whenever you're ready, let's move on."*
:   **All right. I'm ready.**
:   *"This way... the library isn't far."*

Erandur checks [The Dreamstride](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dreamstride "Skyrim:The Dreamstride") for a way past the barrier

Entering the library, [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Invader "Skyrim:Orcish Invader") and [devotees](/wiki/Skyrim:Vaermina_Devotee "Skyrim:Vaermina Devotee") begin to reawaken. Once they have been dealt with, Erandur will say:

:   *"Barring any more interruptions, perhaps we can locate the information I need."*
:   **What am I looking for?**
:   *"We're looking for a book of alchemical recipes called "The Dreamstride." The tome bears the likeness of Vaermina on the cover. It should be here somewhere. If you check around the shelves around the balcony, I'll check around the lower level."*

As you search for the book, he will comment:

:   *"This library used to be filled with arcane volumes. Now look at it; almost everything's been burned. I hope the tome we need is still intact."*

Once you have found the book:

:   **Found it.**
:   *"Let me take a look... Mara be praised! There is a way past the barrier to the inner sanctum. It involves a recipe for a liquid known as Vaermina's Torpor."*
:   **Is that some type of potion?**
:   *"Yes. The Torpor grants an ability the priests of Vaermina called "The Dreamstride"; using dreams to travel distances in the real world."*

:   **That's impossible.**

    :   *"I assure you, the Dreamstride is well known in Vaerminian Lore."*

:   **That's amazing!**

    :   *"Quite amazing, yes. Alchemy and the blessings of a Divine distilled down into a ingestible liquid."*

Either option will have him end with:

:   *"Sadly, I have yet to see it function in person."*
:   **I'm going to be your test subject, then?**
:   *"As a sworn priest of Mara, the elixir won't work for me. The Torpor will only work for Priests of Vaermina, or the unaffiliated."*
:   **Sounds dangerous. How can you be certain?**
:   *"I will not lie to you, there is some risk involved. The last time the Torpor was imbibed could have been decades ago. But I swear upon Lady Mara that I will do everything within my power to prevent any harm from befalling you."*
:   **Forget it! It could kill me!**
:   *"No, all my research points in the opposite direction. This is the exact liquid the priests would drink. The only question in my mind is whether you will be granted The Dreamstride. Otherwise, the worst that could happen is a bad aftertaste. I swear upon Lady Mara that I would never let any harm befall you."*
:   **Do you know where we can find the Torpor?**
:   *"I believe there is a laboratory in the east wing. If we proceed there, we should be able to locate a sample."*
:   **What will The Dreamstride feel like?**
:   *"You'll be viewing the memory of another through your own eyes and with your own body. Those around you will perceive you as normal and you will find the words you utter may not be your own. Thanks to all of these odd principles, there is quite a lot of debate as to whether this is really a dream or just the machinations of Vaermina."*

Following Erandur to the laboratory, more Orcs and Devotees begin to awaken. Once you have fought your way past them, Erandur will say:

:   *"Now that they've been dealt with, we need to find the Torpor."*
:   **How will I know what it looks like?**
:   *"It should be in a small bottle, very similar to a potion. I'll begin searching up here."*

Once you find the Torpor:

:   *"I'm relieved you discovered a bottle intact; this place looks as though it was ransacked by the orcs. So... I've taken us this far, but you need to guide us the rest of the way. Drink."*
:   **Here? Now?**
:   *"Dawnstar's fate rests in that tiny bottle. The longer we wait, the more damage Vaermina could be doing to those poor people. I understand your hesitation, but I promise you that it works."*
:   **How will I know when to awaken?**
:   *"I will watch over you as you slumber to ensure your safety. If I deduce anything is amiss, I will use my arts to bring you back. Otherwise, I am uncertain what will end your Dreamstride. Perhaps when Vaermina's curious appetite has been filled."*

After drinking the Torpor, you will see what happened when the Orcs attacked Nightcaller Temple through the eyes of Erandur.

### Release the Miasma

Dreamstrider

**Thorek**: *"The orcs have breached the inner sanctum, Brother Veren."*
**Veren**: *"We must hold. We can't allow the Skull to fall into their hands."*
**Thorek**: *"But... no more than a handful of us remain, brother."*
**Veren**: *"Then we have no choice. The Miasma must be released."*
**Thorek**: *"The Miasma? But, brother..."*
**Veren**: *"We have no alternative. It's the will of Vaermina. And what about you, Brother Casimir? Are you prepared to serve the will of Vaermina?"*
**Casimir**: *"I've made my peace. I'm ready."*
**Veren**: *"Then it's decided. Brother Casimir, you must activate the barrier and release the Miasma. Let nothing stop you. Brother Thorek, we must remain here and guard this Skull with our lives if necessary."*
**Thorek**: *"Agreed. To the death."*
**Veren**: *"Then let it be done. Farewell, my brothers!"*

Once you exit the dreamstride and deactivate the barrier, Erandur will be amazed:

:   *"It... it worked. Mara be praised! You vanished after drinking the Torpor and materialized on the other side. I have never seen anything quite like it."*

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **It was remarkable... As if I were really there.** | *"How I envy you. I can only imagine the excitement of seeing history through the eyes of another! Sadly, I am resigned to just reading of its wonders through my research of the Skull."* |
| **It served a purpose.** | *"After what you just experienced, you are not amazed? I am at a loss for words."* |
| **Are you mad? I could have died!** | *"I thought I was clear regarding the dangers that awaited you within the Dreamstride. However, this hardly matters any longer as you appear to have exited unscathed."* |

:   **We can discuss it later. We need to proceed.**
:   *"Indeed. My reverence for Vaermina's machinations should not take precedence over our mission. My apologies. The inner sanctum lies ahead. We must reach the Skull and put an end to Dawnstar's troubles. Lead on, my friend."*

Old friends, [Veren](/wiki/Skyrim:Veren_Duleri "Skyrim:Veren Duleri") and [Thorek](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorek "Skyrim:Thorek")

As you walk through the temple towards the Skull of Corruption, you meet Erandur's old friends [Veren](/wiki/Skyrim:Veren_Duleri "Skyrim:Veren Duleri") and [Thorek](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorek "Skyrim:Thorek"):

**Erandur**: *"Wait... Veren... Thorek... you're alive!"*
**Veren**: *"No thanks to you, Casimir."*
**Erandur**: *"I no longer use that name. I'm Erandur, Priest of Mara."*
**Veren**: *"You're a traitor. You left us to die and then ran before the Miasma took you."*
**Erandur**: *"No. I... I was scared. I wasn't ready to sleep."*
**Veren**: *"Enough of your lies! I can't allow you to destroy the Skull, Priest of Mara."*
**Erandur**: *"Then you leave me no choice!"*

After defeating Veren and Thorek, Erandur will say:

:   *"I... knew Veren and Thorek. They were my friends. Is this punishment for my past? Is it Mara's will to torment me so?"*

You can say:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **We had no choice.** | *"Yes. You're right. If they needed to die so that Dawnstar could live, then it was worth the price."* |
| **They were trying to kill us.** | *"And had they succeeded, Dawnstar's fate would be sealed. You have a unique way of looking at things, my friend."* |
| **Maybe they were right. Don't destroy the staff.** | *"No! You mustn't listen to them. They speak only lies and deception. Had we aided them in releasing the Skull, they would use it to wreak havoc across Skyrim. They... they had to die."* |

Erandur calls upon the power of Mara

He will then continue:

:   *"It's time. The Skull must be destroyed. If you'll stand back, I'll perform the ritual granted to me by Lady Mara."*

As he approaches the Skull of Corruption he will seek the help of Mara, chanting:

:   *"I call upon you, Lady Mara! The Skull hungers. It yearns for memories and leaves nightmares in its wake. Grant me the power to break through this barrier and to send the Skull to the depths of Oblivion!"*

As he is calling for help from Mara, Vaermina will speak into your mind, trying to persuade you to kill Erandur before he destroys the Skull of Corruption. If you let Erandur live and destroy the Skull of Corruption, he will remark:

:   *"Forgive me if I don't appear relieved... this temple has taken its toll on me."*

You can reply:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **Are you going to be all right?** | *"In time, I believe I will."* |
| **So, we're done, then?** | *"Yes. The Skull has been destroyed and Dawnstar is safe."* |
| **How about some compensation?** | *"Being a humble servant of Mara, I have little in the way of gold or coin, but perhaps I can offer you something better... companionship."* |

When approached again, he will reveal Nightcaller Temple to be his new home and offer his assistance as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") as a reward:

:   *"I'd constructed a meager shrine to Mara in the antechamber where we entered. My intention was to spend the rest of my years here, burying the past and praying for forgiveness. But instead, I wish to offer my services to you. If you ever wish to journey with me, I'll be here."* Your only dialogue option is to thank him, and he'll reply *"There's no need to thank me. What you did was for the people of Dawnstar. If anyone should be thanked, it should be you."*

## Follower Dialogue

## Rumors

[Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja") in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") will mention being healed by a priest who might very well be Erandur, although this is never explicitly stated:

:   *"I had a bad fall in the mine when I was bringing some food to the men. I was pretty bad off for a while, but a priest of Mara was passing through on his way to Dawnstar and healed me to the best of his abilities."*

## Notes

- The Skull of Corruption is part of the [Oblivion Walker](/wiki/Skyrim:Oblivion_Walker "Skyrim:Oblivion Walker") achievement. Allowing Erandur to destroy it will make you unable to achieve this, unless you obtain two Daedric Artifacts from the quest [Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight").
- Erandur is one of the few followers with fully unique comments about the area you are in at the moment.
- [Sylgia](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja") in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") mentions that a "priest of Mara on his way to Dawnstar" was the one who healed her, which could refer to Erandur.
- Despite being a self-proclaimed priest of Mara, Erandur will still invoke [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura")'s name in combat like any other Dunmer. This is just inherent to his voicetype, as the generic combat lines aren't conditioned to *not* be used by Erandur.
  - Additionally, Erandur does have unique combat lines referencing Mara ("For Lady Mara!", etc.), but these lines are only heard during the Waking Nightmare quest. He also has lines referring to Dawnstar, but these are also only heard during the quest.
- Due to his robes taking up both his head and body slots, he will not equip body armor except when given a helmet or circlet (such as the [Diadem of the Savant](/wiki/Skyrim:Diadem_of_the_Savant "Skyrim:Diadem of the Savant")), or if he is inducted to be a Blade.
  - Erandur will not wear [vampire robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Equipment "Skyrim:Vampire Equipment")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") if they are given to him, even if he is given a helmet or the Diadem so he can wear chest armor. He can wear other vampire equipment, however.
- Although Erandur prefers casting spells, his Magicka pool is very small, and doesn't improve when he levels up.
- If you spare Erandur, he won't mention anything related to the quest once you finish the latter, you cannot ask him about them any longer, and he will switch to standard Dunmer combat dialogue instead.
- If you spare Erandur and ask to check his inventory, 8 torches will be present. They aren't marked as owned by him, allowing you to take them for free.
- Erandur will refer to Vaermina's Torpor in 3 sizes: a "small bottle" when you ask him what it looks like, a "tall bottle" at the end of the conversation, and a "tiny bottle" when he asks you to drink it. The Torpor itself resembles a Philter of Fortify Health.

## Bugs

:   *See also [Skyrim:Waking Nightmare#Bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare#Bugs "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare")*

- If dismissed, he will return to Nightcaller Temple; however, if you wish to get him again as a follower, he may not reappear and seems to disappear from the game entirely.
  - A good way to avoid this from happening is to dismiss him at the Temple.
- Erandur's 11 general idle comments were all erroneously set to only run in caves (and also never in the Tamriel worldspace), so they aren't used anywhere else, often resulting in him repeating the same generic lines over and over again.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

Eranya

**Eranya** is a dead [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") (see bugs below) [mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental") who can be found at the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah"). She wears [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes") and carries [Eranya's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eranya%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eranya's Journal").

## Related Quests

- **[A Matter of Pride](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Matter_of_Pride "Skyrim:A Matter of Pride")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand"): Obtain the legendary katana [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)").

## Bugs

- Despite being described as an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") in her journal, she uses a Breton character model. **?**

## Overview

Erden Relvel

**Erden Relvel** is an antagonist in the questline of [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"). He aims to continue spreading the destructive influence of [Dagoth Ur](/wiki/Lore:Dagoth_Ur "Lore:Dagoth Ur") as a puppet of the [Mask of Dagoth Ur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Dagoth_Ur "Skyrim:Mask of Dagoth Ur"), and must be stopped.

He will appear at Tel Mithryn graveyard after the completion of [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)") is complete, and once you have solved the [puzzle of the armory](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest_Arthamis%27_Note "Skyrim:Priest Arthamis' Note") in [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear") and read Erden's [challenge to you](/wiki/Skyrim:Erden_Relvel%27s_Note "Skyrim:Erden Relvel's Note"). He summons several [Ash Zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Zombie "Skyrim:Ash Zombie") to aid him in combat.

He wears the Mask of Dagoth Ur and the [Robe of the Lich](/wiki/Skyrim:Robe_of_the_Lich "Skyrim:Robe of the Lich"). In his inventory is the final Fahlbtharz Forge Gem.

## Related Quests

- **[Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find out who attacked the temple and retrieve their [unique mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Dagoth_Ur "Skyrim:Mask of Dagoth Ur").[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

## Overview

Erdi

**Erdi** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") maid living in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). She is involved in the quest [The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness"), where she provides you with the key to the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing") of the palace.

Erdi wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1da "Skyrim:Clothes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") along with a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

## Dialogue

When approached, she will greet you with:

:   *"Oh, hello! Just tidying up."*
:   *"So exciting when new folk come into town. I bet you've had plenty of adventures."*

If your character is female, Erdi will talk idly about her aspirations:

:   *"Maybe you need a partner? Hmm? Just picture it. Two women, the dusty road, strapping men at every tavern, a fortune in gold to be claimed..."*
:   *"Someday, I'll be a gallant heroine. You make it look so.. appealing."*

If your character is male, she will keep talking about her dream for a chivalrous hero to arrive and take her away:

:   *"Are you my gallant hero? Have you come to whisk me away, to a life of adventure and romance?"*
:   *"I made a wish in the town well that a golden knight came to take me to his castle. Oh, does it spoil the wish if I tell?"*
:   *"Someday, a gallant hero will ride up and take me away. Someday..."*

Despite this misleading dialogue, she cannot be [married](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") or become a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

### Conversations

In the Winking Skeever:

:   **Jawanan:** *"So, um, mind if I buy you a drink?"*
:   **Erdi:** *"Aw, that's so sweet of you! Thanks!"*

### The Mind of Madness

Telling her that you need to get into the Pelagius Wing:

:   **I need to get into the Pelagius Wing.**
:   *"Oh, I'd get in trouble for that. It's not allowed. Besides, it's scary in there!"*
:   **Falk asked me to check it out.**
:   *"Well... I suppose in that case, it's okay to let you in. But only briefly. Be careful, and come right back!"*

She will then give you the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing_Key "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing Key") to the wing.

| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 70-246 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, **[Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed")**, [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [DA05HunterStallFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DA05HunterStallFaction "Skyrim:DA05HunterStallFaction"); [DA05HuntersOfHircineFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DA05HuntersOfHircineFaction "Skyrim:DA05HuntersOfHircineFaction") | | |

Eriana

**Eriana**, a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"), is one of the hunters who shows up in [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto") hunting [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding"). If you choose to side with Sinding, you will have to kill her.

Eriana wears a set of [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor") along with [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers") and a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). For close ranged combat, she relies on a leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") that can be up to [Elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality and a leveled [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") that can be up to [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel") in quality. For long ranged combat, she relies on a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and twenty [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), both of which can be up to Elven in quality.

## Related Quests

- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.

## Quest-Related Dialogue

She will only say:

:   *"Greetings, fellow hunter."*
:   *"Lead on."*

## Notes

- Eriana is one of two NPCs in the game, with the other being [Sabine Nytte](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabine_Nytte "Skyrim:Sabine Nytte"), who has a race-specific voice type (in her case this is "FemaleNord") that doesn't match their race.

# Skyrim:Erik the Slayer (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik") become an adventurer.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik") |
| Location(s): | [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") |
| Reward: | A potential [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") |
| ID: | RoriksteadFreeform |

Erik lamenting over his situation

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik_the_Slayer "Skyrim:Erik the Slayer") in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").
2. Convince [Mralki](/wiki/Skyrim:Mralki "Skyrim:Mralki") to allow Erik to become an adventurer.
3. Return to Erik.

### Erik the Farmer

[Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik") can be found staying in the [Frostfruit Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn") in the evening or working as a farmer for [Lemkil](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil "Skyrim:Lemkil") in the small settlement of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). He will be glad to see you, another adventurer: *"You look like you've seen your share of adventure. I envy you that."* In fact, he wants to be an adventurer like you, but his father [Mralki](/wiki/Skyrim:Mralki "Skyrim:Mralki") doesn't agree. Not only does the farm need him, but his family couldn't afford to buy armor even if he did let Erik pursue his dream. Erik hopes you can talk to his father and change his mind.

Mralki is the innkeeper of Frostfruit Inn and you can find him there. Obviously, he worries about his son a lot. *"My son? Erik? What about him? Did something happen? Is he alright?"* You may talk to him in two ways:

| Option | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| You should let your son choose the life he wants. | But the world is a dangerous place. Erik has no idea what he's getting himself into. What's more, he's got no armor. I'll have to save up the money for it. |
| Your days of exploiting your son are over. | Exploiting? What's that supposed to mean? Erik works the farm because he's a good lad! I'm not forcing him to stay here. I know that he wants a life of adventure, but I've told him before that I can't afford to buy him armor. |

Then you can attempt to persuade or intimidate Mralki. You must pass an easy [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade him. You can also give him some gold for the cost of armor.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Here, use this to buy some armor.  **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: You would give your own coin to help my son? I'm moved by your compassion. Your kind deed will not go unrewarded, my friend. Tell Erik I've changed my mind, and we'll visit Whiterun soon to fit him for armor. **Failed**: I appreciate the gesture, but I'd rather not be in debt to a stranger. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Erik **Failed**: Nothing |
| You'd prefer your son to grow bitter and resent you?  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: I... I cannot deny the truth of what you say. Erik is all the family that I have left, but it's wrong to hold him back as I have. Go and tell Erik that I've changed my mind. I'll see about borrowing some money in Whiterun for his armor. **Failed**: Perhaps you should let a father decide what is best for his own son. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Erik **Failed**: Nothing |
| Find the money, or you'll have me to deal with.  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Ah, I see. I've just remembered that I saved a few septims in case of an emergency. This is starting to feel like one. Tell Erik that I've changed my mind, and we'll visit Whiterun soon to fit him for armor. And please don't hurt me! **Failed**: Go ahead, hit me as often as you want. It's not going to change anything, other than to make me and the town guard angry. | | | | **Passed**: Return to Erik **Failed**: Nothing |
| On second thought, let's talk about this another time. | Another time, or not at all. It's really none of your business, after all. | | | | Nothing |

### Erik the Slayer

Bring the good news to Erik and he will be very excited. *"I'll hope you'll come back to Rorikstead soon and pay me a visit. Maybe we can swap stories about our adventures over a mug of ale at the inn!"* The next time you see him, he will be equipped with a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor") and you can also ask him to be your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

## Bugs

- If you complete the quest, then rent a room and stay at the inn overnight, Erik the Slayer may be enabled while you are in bed, and will be frozen and impossible to interact with when you get up. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Erik the Slayer (RoriksteadFreeform) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Talk to Mralki about Erik |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Erik |
| 30 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage RoriksteadFreeform stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest RoriksteadFreeform`.

# Skyrim:Erik the Slayer

## Overview

| Erik the Slayer (RefID: 000350B8, 000656E2) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000350B8 000656E2 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000350A7 00065657 |
| Other Information | | | |

Erik at Frostfruit Inn

Erik sitting for a drink

**Erik** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [barbarian](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbarian "Skyrim:Barbarian") living in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). He is the son of [Mralki](/wiki/Skyrim:Mralki "Skyrim:Mralki"), innkeeper of the [Frostfruit Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn"). Erik's mother died when he was little. Erik is bored of his life as a farmer and yearns to leave the town and taste adventure. However, Mralki, a caring and overprotective father, won't let his son do anything even remotely dangerous. Erik asks you to [convince his father](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik_the_Slayer_(quest) "Skyrim:Erik the Slayer (quest)") to change his mind. If successful, he will change his name to **Erik the Slayer**.

After completing his quest it is possible to [hire](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") Erik the Slayer for 500 gold when returning at a later date. Erik is a melee/bow class that favors two-handed weapons and light armor (he has semi-decent Block skill). He has a cheerful disposition and comments about how little regret he has about becoming an adventurer. He can also be [recruited](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") into the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

He sleeps from 10pm to 6am, waking up to head outside and tend the crops. He ends his workday at 6pm and returns to Frostfruit Inn for a one-hour evening meal. He then spends the rest of the day inside the inn until his bedtime. When he becomes a mercenary, however, he will quit his job as a farmer and instead will just stay at the inn.

He wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1d9 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"), and wields an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). He carries a spare [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and [a selection of middle-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). As a mercenary, he will be clad in a more appropriate apparel: a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), and a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). He will keep his iron sword, but will discard his other items.

## Related Quests

- **[Erik the Slayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik_the_Slayer_(quest) "Skyrim:Erik the Slayer (quest)")**: Help [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik") become an adventurer.
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

### Erik the Slayer

When you approach him, he may tell you about his father:

:   *"My father, Mralki, manages the inn. He used to be a soldier, but he left that life behind."*

If you have not solved his problem, he may also remark:

:   *"You look like you've seen your share of adventure. I envy you that. In fact, maybe you can help me with something."*

Similarly, if you have refused to help him earlier, talking to him again will prompt him to ask you:

:   *"Did you reconsider? Will you talk to my father?"*

You may mention that his crops seem to be thriving, and Erik will agree:

:   **Your crops seem to be thriving**
:   *"It's true. For as long as I can remember our crops have always done well. I'm not sure whether it's the soil, the climate or the favor of the Divines, but we've never had a poor harvest."*
:   **Have you lived here all your life?**
:   *"Born and raised right here in Rorikstead. My father was a soldier. He fought in the great war and when it was over, he retired here to raise a family. My mother passed away when I was just a babe, so he did his best to raise me on his own. It's not the most exciting place in the world, but the people here work hard and don't cause trouble for anyone."*
:   **What is it that you need?**
:   *"I want to be an adventurer like you, but my father says I can't. He says that he needs me to stay here and work the farm, and even if he did let me be an adventurer, we couldn't afford to buy armor. His name's Mralki, and he's the innkeeper here. I hope you can change his mind."*
:   **I'll see what I can do.**

    :   *"Thank you. I can't stand the thought of being trapped in this village for the rest of my days."*
:   **You should probably stick to farming.**

    :   *"Well, if you change your mind, I'd still like your help."*

If you agree to help him, he may leave you with these words as you bid him farewell:

:   *"I hope you can change my father's mind. He can be a little stubborn."*

Mralki insists on protecting Erik, as is evident in his dialogue:

:   *"That fool son of mine, Erik, wants to be an adventurer. He*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *a good-natured lad, but he's got no idea how dangerous the world really is."*
:   *"Some folk here will tell you I'm sheltering my boy too much, but I ask you, isn't it a father's duty to keep his children safe?"*

Talk to him about his son, and he will again show concern:

:   *"My son? Erik? What about him? Did something happen? Is he alright?"*

When you tell him that Erik wants to be an adventurer, Mralki will reason that he does not have enough septims to buy his son some armor. To solve this, you can either bribe, persuade, or intimidate him.

When you return to Erik, he may ask you:

:   *"Did you have any luck talking to my father?"*
:   **I haven't spoken to him yet.**

    :   *"Can't blame you for having better things to do than help some farmer you don't know."*
:   **Your father changed his mind.**

    :   *"I can't thank you enough, friend. I'll hope you'll come back to Rorikstead soon and pay me a visit. Maybe we can swap stories about our adventures over a mug of ale at the inn!"*

## Dialogue

After some time, visit Rorikstead and Erik will don his new set of armor and adopt a new schedule. His dialogue will also change: you cannot ask him about his life in Rorikstead anymore. He will greet you cheerfully:

:   *"Good to see you again! How would you like to hire a brave, if untested, mercenary?"*

He may comment on his new life:

:   *"It just feels right somehow, having this new life as an adventurer. It's what I was meant to do."*
:   *"At first I thought I'd miss farming. I guess I've had my fill of it, because I don't miss it at all."*
:   *"This new armor fits me like a glove."*

He may also tell you about his plans for the future:

:   *"If I can make enough money here in Skyrim, I think I'll travel to Hammerfell and see what work I can get there."*

If you have previously hired him, he may also say:

:   *"You're back! Great! Are we going on another adventure?"*

:   *"It's great to see you again! It's been too quiet without you around."*
:   **Erik the Slayer, huh? Sounds fearsome.**

    :   *"Father says I should pick a name that describes what I really am, but nobody's going to hire Erik Greenthumb or Erik Hoe-pusher. No, I need a name that will put some fear in the hearts of my enemies. When I have some enemies, that is."*
:   **You decided to become a mercenary?**

    :   *"Seemed like the best way to see the world and make some coin. Sure I'm a little green, but what I lack in experience, I make up for in courage."*

Upon hiring him, he will enthusiastically say:

:   *"Lead the way!"*

When you say that you need him to do something, he will ask:

:   *"What do you need?"*

Tell him to wait and he will reply:

:   *"I'll be right here. Be careful now!"*

When you ask him to follow you again, Erik will exclaim:

:   *"Great! Let's go!"*

If asked to trade items, he will say:

:   *"No problem! How can I help?"*

Dismissing him will have him tell you:

:   *"Well, it's been fun. I guess I'll head back to Rorikstead."*

If you have hired Erik the Slayer before, he will say the following as you approach:

:   *"I could really use some more experience in the field. I'd be happy to join you again, and it won't cost a thing."*

Accepting his offer and he'll respond:

:   *"I'm ready to go!"*

## Conversations

Before Erik becomes a mercenary, he can be seen conversing with other residents of Rorikstead. [Jouane Manette](/wiki/Skyrim:Jouane_Manette "Skyrim:Jouane Manette") asks Erik if he needs anything from the merchants in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"):

:   **Jouane Manette:** *"Anything I can pick up for you on my next trip into the city, Erik?"*
:   **Erik:** *"Thanks for the offer, Jouane, but I'm saving up for a new sword."*

Erik asks [Lemkil](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil "Skyrim:Lemkil") about his daughters:

:   **Erik:** *"I'm not saying it's my business, but I have to ask. Why are you so cruel to your little girls?"*
:   **Lemkil:** *"You're right, it's none of your business. How about you keep your nose out of it?"*
:   **Erik:** *"You keep on like you are, you'll end up with two daughters who hate you."*
:   **Lemkil:** *"Hah! And what would a witless oaf like you know about raising children?"*

Erik also engages in small talk with [Rorik](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik "Skyrim:Rorik"):

:   **Rorik:** *"Ah, there's nothing like fresh air and honest labor to bolster the spirit."*
:   **Erik:** *"True enough, but there's nothing wrong with a little adventure now and then. Not much excitement in working the soil every day."*

Erik can have two conversations with his father:

:   **Erik:** *"Father, how old were you when you left home?"*
:   **Mralki:** *"I know where this is going, son. As I've said many a time. the world is a dangerous place. You're much safer here at the farm, with me."*
:   **Erik:** *"But I don't want to be safe! I'm not afraid of the dangers out there. The only thing I'm afraid of is wasting my life on this farm."*
:   **Mralki:** *"Yes, that's your mother's side of the family talking. Just stay on for one more season, that's all I ask."*

:   **Mralki:** *"I heard you sneaking around downstairs last night. Were you trying to break into my chest again, son? I've told you to leave it alone."*
:   **Erik:** *"I just wanted to try on your old armor, from back when you were a soldier. I thought I might be old enough to wear it."*
:   **Mralki:** *"I've told you a hundred times, I lock that chest for a reason. I don't want you getting a head full of ideas about adventure and glory."*
:   **Erik:** *"I'm old enough to decide how to live my life, and I'd be honored to wear your armor, if you'd just let me. I'm strong enough to handle it."*
:   **Mralki:** *"Strong, yes, but how clever are you? I'll tell you what, if you can open the lock on my chest, you can have everything in it."*
:   **Erik:** *"I'll take your challenge, but if I win I get to start a new life as an adventurer, and with no objections from you."*

## Notes

.jpg)

Erik West aka "Immok the Slayer", whom Erik the Slayer was named after

- He is [based on](/wiki/Skyrim:Easter_Eggs#Erik_the_Slayer "Skyrim:Easter Eggs") [Erik West](/wiki/General:Erik_West "General:Erik West"), who was known as "ImmoktheSlayer" on the forums and was given an opportunity to play Skyrim at Bethesda’s studio during its development thanks to the Make-a-Wish foundation. He died of cancer in May 2011, six months before Skyrim’s official release.
- Before changing his name to Erik the Slayer, his RefID is `000350B8` and his BaseID is `000350A7`.
- He should put on his new armor immediately after your fast travel away and back. If that doesn't happen, try entering `setstage RoriksteadFreeform 20` and talking to Erik again. Then move away and come back.
- Although his default gear is governed by the Heavy Armor skill, Erik is actually more proficient in Light Armor. Additionally, he is by default equipped with a one-handed weapon and shield, though he is more proficient in Two-Handed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. His class was changed to [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H").
- He has unused lines for when you tell him to wait (*"You sure? All right. I'll keep guard here."*) and when you tell him to follow you (*"Good. I'm ready for anything."*), but due to a scripting oversight, you cannot normally hear them.

## Bugs

- Erik may occasionally be found beside the road close to [Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument") for unknown reasons.
  - Hiring and dismissing Erik on these occasions will cause him to return to [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").
- When accompanying you as a follower, Erik may be inexplicably attacked by members of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") if visiting [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- Dismissing Erik as a follower after he's been recruited as a Blade still plays dialogue saying he's returning to Rorikstead even though this is not where he'll be going.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- Despite normal behavior, if made a [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), Erik will charge you to travel with you, every time.
- The dialogue option to become a steward[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") may never appear.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- If made a steward[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), the steward dialogue options may not appear.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
  - Leaving the area for 24 in-game hours and returning may resolve this.
- ([DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"))Erik may use [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon")'s follower dialogue.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.2, fixes this bug.
- He may attack you on sight after you have liberated the Reach for the Stormcloaks. After Solitude has been conquered and the civil war has ended, he will revert back to his normal behavior. **?**

# Skyrim:Erik the Slayer

## Overview

| Erik the Slayer (RefID: 000350B8, 000656E2) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000350B8 000656E2 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000350A7 00065657 |
