Erik at Frostfruit Inn

Erik sitting for a drink

**Erik** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [barbarian](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbarian "Skyrim:Barbarian") living in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). He is the son of [Mralki](/wiki/Skyrim:Mralki "Skyrim:Mralki"), innkeeper of the [Frostfruit Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn"). Erik's mother died when he was little. Erik is bored of his life as a farmer and yearns to leave the town and taste adventure. However, Mralki, a caring and overprotective father, won't let his son do anything even remotely dangerous. Erik asks you to [convince his father](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik_the_Slayer_(quest) "Skyrim:Erik the Slayer (quest)") to change his mind. If successful, he will change his name to **Erik the Slayer**.

After completing his quest it is possible to [hire](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") Erik the Slayer for 500 gold when returning at a later date. Erik is a melee/bow class that favors two-handed weapons and light armor (he has semi-decent Block skill). He has a cheerful disposition and comments about how little regret he has about becoming an adventurer. He can also be [recruited](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") into the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

He sleeps from 10pm to 6am, waking up to head outside and tend the crops. He ends his workday at 6pm and returns to Frostfruit Inn for a one-hour evening meal. He then spends the rest of the day inside the inn until his bedtime. When he becomes a mercenary, however, he will quit his job as a farmer and instead will just stay at the inn.

He wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1d9 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"), and wields an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). He carries a spare [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and [a selection of middle-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). As a mercenary, he will be clad in a more appropriate apparel: a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), and a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). He will keep his iron sword, but will discard his other items.

## Related Quests

- **[Erik the Slayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik_the_Slayer_(quest) "Skyrim:Erik the Slayer (quest)")**: Help [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik") become an adventurer.
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

### Erik the Slayer

When you approach him, he may tell you about his father:

:   *"My father, Mralki, manages the inn. He used to be a soldier, but he left that life behind."*

If you have not solved his problem, he may also remark:

:   *"You look like you've seen your share of adventure. I envy you that. In fact, maybe you can help me with something."*

Similarly, if you have refused to help him earlier, talking to him again will prompt him to ask you:

:   *"Did you reconsider? Will you talk to my father?"*

You may mention that his crops seem to be thriving, and Erik will agree:

:   **Your crops seem to be thriving**
:   *"It's true. For as long as I can remember our crops have always done well. I'm not sure whether it's the soil, the climate or the favor of the Divines, but we've never had a poor harvest."*
:   **Have you lived here all your life?**
:   *"Born and raised right here in Rorikstead. My father was a soldier. He fought in the great war and when it was over, he retired here to raise a family. My mother passed away when I was just a babe, so he did his best to raise me on his own. It's not the most exciting place in the world, but the people here work hard and don't cause trouble for anyone."*
:   **What is it that you need?**
:   *"I want to be an adventurer like you, but my father says I can't. He says that he needs me to stay here and work the farm, and even if he did let me be an adventurer, we couldn't afford to buy armor. His name's Mralki, and he's the innkeeper here. I hope you can change his mind."*
:   **I'll see what I can do.**

    :   *"Thank you. I can't stand the thought of being trapped in this village for the rest of my days."*
:   **You should probably stick to farming.**

    :   *"Well, if you change your mind, I'd still like your help."*

If you agree to help him, he may leave you with these words as you bid him farewell:

:   *"I hope you can change my father's mind. He can be a little stubborn."*

Mralki insists on protecting Erik, as is evident in his dialogue:

:   *"That fool son of mine, Erik, wants to be an adventurer. He*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *a good-natured lad, but he's got no idea how dangerous the world really is."*
:   *"Some folk here will tell you I'm sheltering my boy too much, but I ask you, isn't it a father's duty to keep his children safe?"*

Talk to him about his son, and he will again show concern:

:   *"My son? Erik? What about him? Did something happen? Is he alright?"*

When you tell him that Erik wants to be an adventurer, Mralki will reason that he does not have enough septims to buy his son some armor. To solve this, you can either bribe, persuade, or intimidate him.

When you return to Erik, he may ask you:

:   *"Did you have any luck talking to my father?"*
:   **I haven't spoken to him yet.**

    :   *"Can't blame you for having better things to do than help some farmer you don't know."*
:   **Your father changed his mind.**

    :   *"I can't thank you enough, friend. I'll hope you'll come back to Rorikstead soon and pay me a visit. Maybe we can swap stories about our adventures over a mug of ale at the inn!"*

## Dialogue

After some time, visit Rorikstead and Erik will don his new set of armor and adopt a new schedule. His dialogue will also change: you cannot ask him about his life in Rorikstead anymore. He will greet you cheerfully:

:   *"Good to see you again! How would you like to hire a brave, if untested, mercenary?"*

He may comment on his new life:

:   *"It just feels right somehow, having this new life as an adventurer. It's what I was meant to do."*
:   *"At first I thought I'd miss farming. I guess I've had my fill of it, because I don't miss it at all."*
:   *"This new armor fits me like a glove."*

He may also tell you about his plans for the future:

:   *"If I can make enough money here in Skyrim, I think I'll travel to Hammerfell and see what work I can get there."*

If you have previously hired him, he may also say:

:   *"You're back! Great! Are we going on another adventure?"*

:   *"It's great to see you again! It's been too quiet without you around."*
:   **Erik the Slayer, huh? Sounds fearsome.**

    :   *"Father says I should pick a name that describes what I really am, but nobody's going to hire Erik Greenthumb or Erik Hoe-pusher. No, I need a name that will put some fear in the hearts of my enemies. When I have some enemies, that is."*
:   **You decided to become a mercenary?**

    :   *"Seemed like the best way to see the world and make some coin. Sure I'm a little green, but what I lack in experience, I make up for in courage."*

Upon hiring him, he will enthusiastically say:

:   *"Lead the way!"*

When you say that you need him to do something, he will ask:

:   *"What do you need?"*

Tell him to wait and he will reply:

:   *"I'll be right here. Be careful now!"*

When you ask him to follow you again, Erik will exclaim:

:   *"Great! Let's go!"*

If asked to trade items, he will say:

:   *"No problem! How can I help?"*

Dismissing him will have him tell you:

:   *"Well, it's been fun. I guess I'll head back to Rorikstead."*

If you have hired Erik the Slayer before, he will say the following as you approach:

:   *"I could really use some more experience in the field. I'd be happy to join you again, and it won't cost a thing."*

Accepting his offer and he'll respond:

:   *"I'm ready to go!"*

## Conversations

Before Erik becomes a mercenary, he can be seen conversing with other residents of Rorikstead. [Jouane Manette](/wiki/Skyrim:Jouane_Manette "Skyrim:Jouane Manette") asks Erik if he needs anything from the merchants in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"):

:   **Jouane Manette:** *"Anything I can pick up for you on my next trip into the city, Erik?"*
:   **Erik:** *"Thanks for the offer, Jouane, but I'm saving up for a new sword."*

Erik asks [Lemkil](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil "Skyrim:Lemkil") about his daughters:

:   **Erik:** *"I'm not saying it's my business, but I have to ask. Why are you so cruel to your little girls?"*
:   **Lemkil:** *"You're right, it's none of your business. How about you keep your nose out of it?"*
:   **Erik:** *"You keep on like you are, you'll end up with two daughters who hate you."*
:   **Lemkil:** *"Hah! And what would a witless oaf like you know about raising children?"*

Erik also engages in small talk with [Rorik](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik "Skyrim:Rorik"):

:   **Rorik:** *"Ah, there's nothing like fresh air and honest labor to bolster the spirit."*
:   **Erik:** *"True enough, but there's nothing wrong with a little adventure now and then. Not much excitement in working the soil every day."*

Erik can have two conversations with his father:

:   **Erik:** *"Father, how old were you when you left home?"*
:   **Mralki:** *"I know where this is going, son. As I've said many a time. the world is a dangerous place. You're much safer here at the farm, with me."*
:   **Erik:** *"But I don't want to be safe! I'm not afraid of the dangers out there. The only thing I'm afraid of is wasting my life on this farm."*
:   **Mralki:** *"Yes, that's your mother's side of the family talking. Just stay on for one more season, that's all I ask."*

:   **Mralki:** *"I heard you sneaking around downstairs last night. Were you trying to break into my chest again, son? I've told you to leave it alone."*
:   **Erik:** *"I just wanted to try on your old armor, from back when you were a soldier. I thought I might be old enough to wear it."*
:   **Mralki:** *"I've told you a hundred times, I lock that chest for a reason. I don't want you getting a head full of ideas about adventure and glory."*
:   **Erik:** *"I'm old enough to decide how to live my life, and I'd be honored to wear your armor, if you'd just let me. I'm strong enough to handle it."*
:   **Mralki:** *"Strong, yes, but how clever are you? I'll tell you what, if you can open the lock on my chest, you can have everything in it."*
:   **Erik:** *"I'll take your challenge, but if I win I get to start a new life as an adventurer, and with no objections from you."*

## Notes

.jpg)

Erik West aka "Immok the Slayer", whom Erik the Slayer was named after

- He is [based on](/wiki/Skyrim:Easter_Eggs#Erik_the_Slayer "Skyrim:Easter Eggs") [Erik West](/wiki/General:Erik_West "General:Erik West"), who was known as "ImmoktheSlayer" on the forums and was given an opportunity to play Skyrim at Bethesda’s studio during its development thanks to the Make-a-Wish foundation. He died of cancer in May 2011, six months before Skyrim’s official release.
- Before changing his name to Erik the Slayer, his RefID is `000350B8` and his BaseID is `000350A7`.
- He should put on his new armor immediately after your fast travel away and back. If that doesn't happen, try entering `setstage RoriksteadFreeform 20` and talking to Erik again. Then move away and come back.
- Although his default gear is governed by the Heavy Armor skill, Erik is actually more proficient in Light Armor. Additionally, he is by default equipped with a one-handed weapon and shield, though he is more proficient in Two-Handed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. His class was changed to [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H").
- He has unused lines for when you tell him to wait (*"You sure? All right. I'll keep guard here."*) and when you tell him to follow you (*"Good. I'm ready for anything."*), but due to a scripting oversight, you cannot normally hear them.

## Bugs

- Erik may occasionally be found beside the road close to [Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument") for unknown reasons.
  - Hiring and dismissing Erik on these occasions will cause him to return to [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").
- When accompanying you as a follower, Erik may be inexplicably attacked by members of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") if visiting [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- Dismissing Erik as a follower after he's been recruited as a Blade still plays dialogue saying he's returning to Rorikstead even though this is not where he'll be going.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- Despite normal behavior, if made a [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), Erik will charge you to travel with you, every time.
- The dialogue option to become a steward[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") may never appear.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- If made a steward[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), the steward dialogue options may not appear.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
  - Leaving the area for 24 in-game hours and returning may resolve this.
- ([DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"))Erik may use [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon")'s follower dialogue.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.2, fixes this bug.
- He may attack you on sight after you have liberated the Reach for the Stormcloaks. After Solitude has been conquered and the civil war has ended, he will revert back to his normal behavior. **?**

Erikur's House

**Erikur's House** is a large mansion lying just northwest of the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

It is the last building on the right before the Blue Palace and across from the Bards College and Bryling's house.

## Related Quests

- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur")  [Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli "Skyrim:Gisli")  [Melaran](/wiki/Skyrim:Melaran "Skyrim:Melaran")  [Kraldar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kraldar "Skyrim:Kraldar") \*  [Thonjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonjolf "Skyrim:Thonjolf") \* |

\* Will be exiled here should [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") be given to the [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and subsequently retaken for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

### Exterior

There are two entrances to Erikur's House, with a third door leading out onto a small balcony that can be used as an exit. On the ledge southwest of the balcony, there is a [Potion of Plentiful Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"). There are five barrels lying down to the right of the main entrance to this house and once you have completed the Thieves Guild special "reputation" job in Solitude there will be a sixth barrel standing upright to the right of these with the [thief cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") shadowmark "Cache") Cache carved into the side of it. There is also a [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)")  "Protected") Protected to the left of both entrances and painted on a barrel by the second entrance.

### Erikur's House

Upon entering through the main door you are on the ground floor, there is a wooden bench to the left of you and a smaller wardrobe on your right holding a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") and two [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). Moving forward, on your left is a storage area and a second entrance. Against the northeast wall are a set of shelves holding several mead barrels, two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). To the right of this is a cupboard holding a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") and an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"). Opposite these is a pen holding twenty-one [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") barrels, with several sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") around it. Against an interior wall to the northwest is another cupboard this one holding various cheese wheels and wedges, with an unlocked safe to the left that is easy to miss. Continuing along the main corridor there is another wooden bench on the left with a small set of shelves opposite holding a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") and a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") on top. At the end of the corridor is an urn with tundra cotton sticking out the top and stairs leading upstairs.

On the second floor, there is a bedroom on your left, it is the living quarters of [Melaran](/wiki/Skyrim:Melaran "Skyrim:Melaran") and contains an owned single bed in the southern corner, with an end table with a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") on next to it. Beside this is an open box containing a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"). To the right of this, in the western corner is a wooden bench and small wardrobe holding a candlestick and a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")*. In the northern corner is a seating area consisting of a wooden bench and chair arranged around a low table holding a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") with [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese, a goblet and a copy of *[The Cake and The Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*, there is also a small table in the corner with a lit candle on. Above this are two wall shelves holding a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), two goblets and a [cup](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"). There are two decorative urns in the room with tundra cotton in them.

Erikur on his enchanter

Opposite the door to the bedroom in the corridor is a small wardrobe with an open box on top holding four [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower, a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"). Past this the corridor opens out into a room, on your right is the third entrance with a small wardrobe against the southwestern wall with two deathbell flowers on top and a basket containing two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") beside it. Opposite it is an urn with tundra cotton on a small round table. Coming out from the northeastern wall are bookshelves containing a [potion of ultimate magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Magicka"), a [potion of vigorous stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Stamina"), a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"), a [weak stamina poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Stamina_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Stamina Poison"), an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem") and several common books. Next to this is a long open box containing a bunch of lavender, a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), a [potion of plentiful magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and two empty lesser soul gems. There is also a [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") on a stand. In the northern corner is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). Against the bedroom wall, to the southwest is a wooden bench and an open box containing a potion of strength, two soul gem fragments, two blue and one [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") and a deathbell flower.

To the northeast is a fireplace with a cooking pot in front of it on a stand, under the pot is a portion of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") and to the right is a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") in a cast iron pot. On the mantle above the fire is a bottle of [frostbite vemon](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), two goblets and a bowl. On the left is a small round table holding a goblet and bottle of wine. To the right is an intimate eating area with a small square table and two chairs. On the table are two plates of [seared slaughterfish steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two goblets and bread and cheese. Over this is a wall shelf holding a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a bunch of tundra cotton and a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Finally against the northeastern wall is a narrow table holding a goblet and plate with three [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak").

Erikur's bedroom

Climbing to the top floor you reach a balcony that goes all the way around the building, but still allows views down to the center of the house. Turning left at the top you pass a small table and wooden bench. In the western corner are two bookshelves, a low table and chair. On the table is a goblet and a copy of *[Shezarr and the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shezarr_and_the_Divines "Skyrim:Shezarr and the Divines")*. The bookshelves contain eleven common books, a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength") and a [potion of extreme stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina"). Continuing around the balcony you come to Erikur's bedroom which contains an owned four poster double bed. There is a long chest at the end of it, a small wardrobe to the left of it has an open box on it containing a bunch of tundra cotton and a red mountain flower. There is a tall wardrobe against the southwest wall and a set of shelves to the left, behind the open door. These hold two [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), two bottles of frostbite venom, a deathbell flower, a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") and a basket containing two bunches of lavender. On the right side of the bed is another low wardrobe. Against the northeast wall is a low wardrobe with a goblet on top, to the right of this is a wash basin on a stand and a basket containing a small coin purse. Beside these is yet another wardrobe with two goblets and a jug on top. Against the southeast wall is a narrow table with a bowl of bread, a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") on a plate and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and above this is a wall shelf holding a bunch of lavender.

Back out onto the balcony and continuing to travel clockwise you pass a narrow table with a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") holding two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and two [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat")  on and an urn with tundra cotton beside it. Above is a wall shelf holding a bunch of lavender and a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"). In the north corner is a wooden bench. Along the northeastern wall is a cupboard and in the eastern corner another wooden bench beside two small tables holding a goblet and bottle of wine, a plate of bread, cheese and a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") and copies of *[The Seed](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Seed "Skyrim:The Seed")* and *[The Windhelm Letters](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Windhelm_Letters "Skyrim:The Windhelm Letters")*. Along the southeastern wall is a bench and then further along are two small cupboard with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a goblet and a jug on top of them.

## Notes

- If you help Erikur during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), he will consider you a friend afterwards, making low-value items here free to take.

## Bugs

- There is a "Protected" shadowmark to the left of both doors and on a barrel by the side door. Despite this however, the house can still be the target of a Thieves Guild special jobs quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, addresses this issue. The house is no longer a valid quest target.
- Some of the items are marked as owned by the MarkarthHagsCureFaction, making them free to take if you help [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela"). **?**
- Erikur's House has its ownership set to SolitudeEvetteSansHouseFaction. Its lock list is also set to SolitudeEvetteSansHouseLockList.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

Erikur

**Erikur**, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), is a [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). He oversees the local businesses and imports low quality weaponry from [Black Marsh](/wiki/Lore:Black_Marsh "Lore:Black Marsh") to sell to the [Imperial army](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") for a high price. However, his loyalty is flexible and can even be bought by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). As an influential and wealthy citizen of Skyrim, he is one of the party guests at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity"), where he may serve as a distraction. He is also the older brother of [Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli "Skyrim:Gisli"), who despises him for his pompous and questionable tendencies.

He sleeps from midnight to 8am, then heads to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") to [attend court](#Conversations) straight away. At 1pm, he enjoys a two-hour lunch at the palace. He then resumes his duties until 8pm, when he spends the night relaxing at [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House") before going to bed at midnight. However, during Diplomatic Immunity, he will be found at the Thalmor Embassy until the quest ends.

Erikur wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#000f8713 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") along with a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#00086993 "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). He wields a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Keys#Key_to_Erikur.27s_House "Skyrim:Keys") to [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur%27s_House "Skyrim:Erikur's House"), a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and a selection of [upper-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload")**: Frame a [ship's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") captain to get revenge for a jilted merchant.
- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").

## Dialogue

He will often talk about politics and business:

:   *"The Imperials are good for business, and business is good for Skyrim."*
:   *"I understand what's best for Solitude... and Jarl [Elisif](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") knows it."*
:   *"Half of the businesses in town owe me money, and I own most of the rest. I practically run Solitude already."*
:   *"[Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling")'s obsession with honor and tradition is quaint, but politically irrelevant."*

Should you speak to him directly you can ask him some questions:

:   **What's your place in the court?**

    :   *"I'm a Thane. In the future, you may want to gain that information before talking with someone. Risk of looking like an idiot, and all that."*
:   **Do all the Thanes support Elisif?**

    :   *"Oh, most certainly. At least, when Elisif herself asks.
        If you're inquiring whether we have concerns about her age and inexperience, well, let me put it this way...
        The Thanes have every confidence in [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius")'s leadership."*

However, if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capture Solitude, his answer will instead be:

:   *"I don't suppose it matters much anymore.
    As long as Ulfric wishes Elisif to remain Jarl, remain Jarl she will. And the Thanes will continue to follow her orders.
    As long as those orders came from Ulfric."*

### Diplomatic Immunity

Erikur will appear as a guest to [Elenwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Elenwen "Skyrim:Elenwen")'s party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"). If approached, he'll remark on either the war or the festivities. You can tell him that he sounds like quite the businessman, striking up a conversation with the merchant. If you ask him who he is, he'll tell you just how important his contributions are. He'll continue sanctimoniously, and end in a more jovial tone; commenting that his work brings in loads of gold.

:   *"Elenwen always throws quite a party. I never miss one if I can help it."*

:   *"For the man who knows how to make money, war can be a most profitable venture."*

:   *"The [Great War](/wiki/Lore:Great_War "Lore:Great War") is long past. It's time the Empire and the Aldmeri Dominion put aside their differences. Prosperity is good for everyone."*
:   **You sound like quite the businessman.**
:   *"Not every Nord is obsessed with strength, honor and skill at arms.
    A rare few are born with a gift for making money. My investments are my strength and my wealth is my weapon.
    As for honor, well, there are some luxuries even I can't afford."*
:   **What brings you to this party?**
:   *"You must be new to Skyrim, or you'd already know who I am. I have a stake in most anything of importance in Solitude.
    I feel that it's time to put aside the grievances of the past, and let peace and prosperity flourish between the Empire and the Aldmeri Dominion.
    I try to do my little part. Besides, just between you and me, it's making me pots of money, hahaha."*

During the party, he may be seen with a [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") maid named [Brelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelas "Skyrim:Brelas").

:   **Erikur:** *"There's a likely-looking filly. Even if she is an elf. You there! Serving girl! What's your name, dear?"*
:   **Brelas:** *"Uh, Brelas, sir. Did you need a drink? Something to eat?"*
:   **Erikur:** *"No, no, that's not what I'm interested in right now. I just wanted to get a better look at you. I like what I see, my dear. And believe me, I don't say that to everyone. I'm very discriminating when it comes to the female form."*
:   **Brelas:** *"Um, thank you. Sir. Was there anything else I can do for you?"'*
:   **Erikur:** *"Oh... not at the moment. Maybe later. Don't go far."*
:   **Brelas:** *"Yes, sir."*

When he is approached, he may ask you:

:   *"Did you see that serving girl? I hear elf women are insatiable..."*
:   **I saw you eyeing that serving girl.**
:   *"Mmm, yes... Brelas, is that the one? I hope you're not thinking of cutting me out, are you? Haha.
    I'm warning you, when I get my heart set on something I'm not easily put off."*
:   **Don't worry. She's all yours.**

    :   *"Ha. We'll see. I do have my eye on her, but she seemed a bit cold when I spoke to her earlier. Maybe just playing hard to get, eh?"*
:   **Maybe I can talk to her for you. See if she's interested.**

    :   *"Really? Yes, maybe that would be just the thing. She seemed to be playing hard to get when I spoke to her earlier. Go on. See what she says. Now you've gone and gotten my hopes up again."*

If you've agreed to talk to Brelas, you will see just how interested she is in him: *"Ugh. Erikur, right? He was talking to me earlier. I could tell what he was after. I hate working these parties. Some of the guests are nice, but there's always a few like Erikur."* She will end by pleading you, *"Please tell him to leave me alone. Politely. I'm sure you'll have better luck getting through to him than I would."*

You can use this to cause a distraction at the party.

Return to Erikur, who will ask you if you've spoken to her. You have three possible replies to choose from.

:   *"Have you talked to Brelas yet? I'm not a patient man, you know."*
:   **Not yet. These things can't be rushed.**

    :   *"Ha. Don't toy with me. I may just have to seize my opportunity with both hands, ha ha ha. But we'll play it your way for now."*
:   **Yes. She said she can sneak you up to her quarters right now.**

    :   *"Haha. I knew it! No woman yet born has been able to resist my charms for long. Thank you, my friend. I owe you one."*
:   **Yes. She wants you to leave her alone.**

    :   *"What? That little tease! Leading me on and turning cold at the last minute. I don't think so."*

Erikur will walk up to Brelas and proposition her again. Their conversation will depend on what you told him earlier:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Lie** | **Truth** |
| **Erikur:** *"Hello, my dear. I got your message. Where shall we go?"*  **Brelas:** *"What? I'm sorry, sir, but you must have misunderstood. I'm not permitted to leave the party."*  **Erikur:** *"Oh, I don't think so. I think I understand perfectly. Don't worry, my dear, I will make any necessary excuses to your employer."* | **Erikur:** *"So you think you can toy with me, is that it? No, my dear. I have my heart set on you, and I always get what I want."*  **Brelas:** *"I'm sorry, sir. I didn't mean to give you the wrong impression earlier. I meant no disrespect."*  **Erikur:** *"Don't worry, I'll let you make it up to me. Now, where can we go for a little privacy, hmm?"* |

Either way, it will end disastrously, creating a distraction at the party:

:   **Brelas:** *"No, I'm sorry, but I can't go anywhere with you. I won't. Please, I must get back to my duties."*
:   **Erikur:** *"Don't you dare walk away from me, you slut! Do you know who I am?"*
:   **Brelas:** *"Please, sir, leave me alone!"*
:   **Erikur:** *"Now you're going to be sorry you crossed me. Elenwen! This servant girl has been throwing herself at me in a most disgusting manner."*
:   **Elenwen:** *"Is that so, Erikur? And you with such delicate sensibilities. It must have been most upsetting."*
:   **Erikur:** *"I demand that you have this wench removed from my presence at once!"*
:   **Elenwen:** *"Well. Whatever the truth of it, I'm sure a few words with Master [Rulindil](/wiki/Skyrim:Rulindil "Skyrim:Rulindil") will have a salutary effect. Take her downstairs."*
:   **Brelas:** *"No!"*
:   **Guard:** *"Yes, Madame Ambassador."*
:   **Brelas:** *"Mistress Elenwen, it's not true! I did nothing! Sir, you must tell her! You don't know what they'll do to me! Please!"*
:   **Erikur:** *"Well, I'm glad that little unpleasantness is over."*

Whether you lie to him or tell him the truth, you will increase Erikur's [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you, even if you rescue Brelas later in the quest.

### The Dainty Sload

If you have completed enough [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") jobs in Solitude, asking [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") about a special job will have him tell you, *"I need you to make your way to Solitude and talk to Erikur. He's lookin' to run some kind of a shill job. Now, he's not exactly goin' to welcome you with open arms, but keep your cool. Do this job right and we've just made an important friend out there."*

Now approach Erikur and tell him about how Delvin Mallory said he has work for you. If you claim Delvin sent you because you're the best, he'll air a hint of doubt, but if you get straight to the point, he'll be more enthusiastic. Regardless of how you answer him, Erikur will elaborate on his predicament.

:   **Delvin Mallory said you have work for me.**
:   *"It's about time you got here.
    I'm not accustomed to dealing with people who are unreliable. That's why I asked Delvin to send me his best."*
:   **That's why he sent me.**

    :   *"Hmph. That remains to be seen."*
:   **Let's just get to work.**

    :   *"That's more like it."*
:   *"Nothing raises my ire more than having an agreement broken. It's bad for business and it wastes time.
    Captain Volf of the [Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") has decided to test my patience on this matter by neglecting to honor a trade agreement we had established."*
:   **I assume this is where I enter the picture.**
:   *"I need you to help me show him the error of his ways by sneaking on board the Sload and planting some contraband."*
:   **What sort of contraband?**
:   *"You'll need to get your hands on some [Balmora Blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Balmora_Blue "Skyrim:Potions") from [Sabine Nyette](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabine_Nytte "Skyrim:Sabine Nytte") down by the docks. She's the first mate on another ship, the [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave").
    Once you get your hands on it, I want you to plant it in Captain Volf's footlocker. I'll take care of the rest."*
:   **Consider it done.**
:   *"Captain Volf is ashore right now and I want the authorities waiting for him when he gets back.
    Now get going... I don't want to see your face until the job's done."*

Before you get to work, you may inquire about the Red Wave and Balmora Blue.

:   **You have any information on the Red Wave?**

    :   *"There's pirates and then there's the crew of the Red Wave. They're in a class by themselves.
        They usually make runs along the coast shipping all sorts of contraband to and from [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind").
        Rumor has it they can get you anything for the right price."*
:   **What exactly is Balmora Blue?**

    :   *"Not sure. I know that it starts with [Moon Sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar"), but all sorts of other ingredients are added to increase its potency.
        Used to be a lucrative underworld commodity when [Balmora](/wiki/Lore:Balmora "Lore:Balmora") was still standing. Now the stuff is beyond valuable.
        It's also very illegal. Anyone caught with Balmora Blue looks forward to rotting in jail for a very long time."*

Once you've completed the dirty work for Erikur, give him the good news. He will reward you with a random [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes").

:   **I've planted the contraband on the Dainty Sload.**
:   *"Yes, I know. In fact, by now, Captain Volf should be on his way to the prisons.
    Our contract is complete. Here's a token of my gratitude for your efforts.
    Oh, convey my compliments to Delvin for me. Tell him I'll be happy to reopen whatever doors he needs in Solitude."*

Return to Delvin, who will be pleased as well: *"Erikur assures me that Captain Volf will spend pretty much the rest of his life clapped in irons. Best of all, he's also pledged to open doors for us in Solitude and to get things rollin' again."*

## Conversations

As long as [Viarmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Viarmo "Skyrim:Viarmo") is not at the Blue Palace to [perform](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") Olaf's Verse, you may hear Erikur speak with other court attendants:

:   **Erikur**: *"I've heard the Empire plans to levy a tax on our trading ships. Falk, you've got to do something about this."*
:   **Falk**: *"General Tullius needs more money for the war effort. We need the funds to arm and provision more troops."*
:   **Erikur**: *"Then let's increase the taxes on the farms and merchants. We can't afford to lose the loyalty of the ship captains."*
:   **Falk**: *"We know full well about your investment in shipping ventures, Erikur. I've also heard troubling rumors about dealings between you and the crew of that pirate ship, the Red Wave. Thankfully, Jarl Elisif cares far less about your lost profits than she does about winning the war!"*
:   **Erikur**: *"The Jarl would be wise to remember that it is her thanes - and my profits - that are paying for this war."*

:   **Elisif**: *"Steward Falk, I have a task for you. I want to begin stockpiling food and water in the event we come under siege, and I would like you to oversee this work personally."*
:   **Falk**: *"A wise course of action, my Jarl. However, we have little food or water to spare."*
:   **Erikur**: *"General Tullius will never allow that. He's ordered all surplus food to be given over for the war effort."*
:   **Falk**: *"General Tullius does not run this city, Thane Erikur. Or have you forgotten your oaths of fealty?"*
:   **Erikur**: *"My apologies, Jarl Elisif. I was thinking only of the importance of the war effort."*
:   **Elisif**: *"There's no need for an apology, and you're right about the war. Perhaps this is a matter best discussed with the general in person."*
:   **Falk**: *"I will make the arrangements, my Jarl."*

:   **Elisif**: *"As you know, Solitude's coffers are much depleted by the war efforts. Thane Erikur, you have a strong head for business. What do you suggest?"*
:   **Erikur**: *"This is an unfortunate but unavoidable ebb in revenue. But as long as we continue to support the Empire, our sacrifices will be well rewarded."*
:   **Bryling**: *"Listen to you, speaking of sacrifice. You've never gone hungry a day in your life, Erikur!"*
:   **Elisif**: *"And what would my impetuous Thane Bryling suggest, instead?"*
:   **Bryling**: *"Simple. Let the Empire fight its own war, with its own funds, and without hijacking our supplies and soldiers. Let Haafingar rebuild."*
:   **Erikur**: *"My lady... Surely you're not that naive. Such foolishness would only leave us defenseless. The rebels would storm the palace in an afternoon."*
:   **Bryling**: *"The Stormcloaks only rebel because the Empire uses Skyrim as its personal larder. The more they take, the more support the rebels gain!"*
:   **Elisif**: *"That is quite enough. Perhaps I will raise these issues when I have an audience with General Tullius."*

:   **Elisif**: *"Thane Bryling, what do you have to report about the state of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar")'s defenses?"*
:   **Bryling**: *"The news is the same as it's been for the rest of the war, your grace. Our borders are secure, but at the cost of the guards for our towns and roads."*
:   **Erikur**: *"I don't see any reason why we'd need them. As long as those dogs stay outside of our borders, we're fine."*
:   **Bryling**: *"The Stormcloaks are far from the only threat to the hold. The roads are beset by bandits and beasts... and now there's even talk of bloody dragons."*
:   **Erikur**: *"My dear Bryling. Barring any... fancy and folly... the good people of Haafingar are surely capable of dealing with the odd highwayman or stray dog."*
:   **Bryling**: *"Trouble on the roads and cities means less commerce. Less commerce means less money and more starving people. And that means more crime."*
:   **Erikur**: *"Humph. That's only a problem for people who can't afford to hire their own security."*
:   **Elisif**: *"That may well be our only answer. I will empower my Steward to seek out capable individuals to secure Haafingar. Thank you, my Thanes."*

He will discuss business with [Melaran](/wiki/Skyrim:Melaran "Skyrim:Melaran"):

:   **Erikur**: *"Melaran, you lazy milk drinker, have you finished studying the imports from [Black Marsh](/wiki/Lore:Black_Marsh "Lore:Black Marsh")?"*
:   **Melaran**: *"Indeed I have, sir. [Elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") weapons for their armies, sir. Elven material, but poor workmanship, like most of what we get from them."*
:   **Erikur**: *"Scary, thinking of those boots with an army of Elven weapons at their command. Let's be thankful they're half a world away, eh?"*
:   **Melaran**: *"Even a fine weapon is only as good as its wielder, sir. But they should fetch a high price from the Imperial army."*
:   **Erikur**: *"Right you are, elf! Or even from the rebels, if they've got enough money to make a competitive offer."*
:   **Melaran**: *"As always, lord, your loyalty is a shining example to us all."*

At other times, he will talk with Gisli:

:   **Erikur**: *"Sister, how is my fortune coming along?"*
:   **Gisli**: *"Profits continue to rise. The warehouse continues to bring in good revenues, and rent on your stores in the Well is acceptable."*
:   **Erikur**: *"I'm afraid 'acceptable' just isn't acceptable anymore. I'm sure they can spare a few more coins in monthly rent."*
:   **Gisli**: *"Yes, brother. I'm sure they'll agree it's a fair price to pay in order to avoid interacting with you on a daily basis."*
:   **Erikur**: *"Fair or not, they'll pay it, and that's all I need to care about. Bear that in mind, sister."*

:   **Erikur**: *"That clumsy maid at the palace spilled wine on my best suit. Sister, I believe it's time for a replacement."*
:   **Gisli**: *"I can commission one from the Radiant Raiment. It won't be cheap, but if you want the best, they're the only choice."*
:   **Erikur**: *"I swear, those scheming elves charge us twice what anyone else would pay."*
:   **Gisli**: *"Of course they do, brother. You keep raising their rent."*

## Unused Dialogue

An unfinished quest, [Boethiah's Bidding](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests#Boethiah.27s_Bidding "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"), featured [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") as the target of an assassination. Unused dialogue indicates that Erikur would have taken her place as [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Solitude:

:   **Are you doing well, serving as Jarl?**
:   *"Ahhh. Quite fine my friend. Quite fine. So sad what happened to young Elisif. Tragic really. Such a young and pretty girl. Was in over her head, I'm afraid. But we should be done with murders in the Blue Palace. I've stepped up security around here."*

The dialogue notes strongly imply that he was involved with her murder.

:   **I'm having some difficulties with the guards. Can you take care of that?**
:   *"Hmm... Yes, I've heard about all that fuss. I myself know it's all a terrible, terrible misunderstanding. I'm quite sure you're innocent in all this. This one time only, I'll grant you special immunity for any past transgressions, real or perceived. But going forward, I'm sure you realize that your fate is in your own hands. And the law can not be bent for personal friendships."*

Imperial Solitude [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Guards "Skyrim:Guards") will worry about Erikur's safety as jarl:

:   *"First Torygg and now Elisif. Damn those Stormcloaks. Let's hope that Erikur fares better than they did."*
:   *"We'll protect Erikur as best we're able, but I fear the throne of Solitude is cursed."*

Some scenes would also play out a bit differently:

[Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak")'s speech scene to the troops after the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") won the war would've gone like this:

:   **Galmar**: *"And now, I present to you, Ulfric Stormcloak, hero of the people, liberator and High King of Skyrim!"*
:   **Ulfric**: *"I am indeed Ulfric Stormcloak, and at my side the man/woman we know as Stormblade, and the world knows as the Dragonborn. And indeed, there are many that call us heroes. But it is all of you who are the true heroes! It was you who fought a dying Empire who sunk its claws into our land, trying to drag us down with it. It was you who fought the Thalmor and their puppets who would have us deny our gods and our heritage. It was you who fought your kin who didn't understand our cause, who weren't willing to pay the price of our freedom. But more than that, it was you who fought for Skyrim, for our right to fight our own battles... To return to our glory and traditions, to determine our own future!"*
:   **Soldiers**: *"Huzzah!"*
:   **Ulfric**: *"And it is for these reasons that I cannot accept the mantle of "High King." Not until the Moot declares that title should adorn my shoulders will I accept it."*
:   **Soldier**: *"And what about Jarl Erikur?"*
:   **Ulfric**: *"Yes, what about Jarl Erikur? Will he cast aside the Imperial coin falling into his coffers? Will he acknowledge that we Nords deserve to determine our own future? Will he swear fealty to me, that all may know we are at peace, and a new day has dawned?"*
:   **Erikur**: *"I do!"*
:   **Ulfric**: *"Then it is settled. The Jarl will continue to rule Solitude, I will garrison armies here to ward off Imperial attempts to reclaim the city. And in due time, the Moot will meet, and settle the claim to High King once and for all. There is much to do, and I need every able bodied man and woman committed to rebuilding Skyrim. A great darkness is growing, and soon we will be called to fight it, on these shores or abroad. The Aldmeri Dominion may have defeated the Empire, but it has not defeated Skyrim!"*
:   **Soldiers**: [cheering]

One of the scenes between Bryling and Falk Firebeard would get a new line acknowledging Erikur's new status as well:

:   **Bryling:** *"Falk, you shouldn't have come. You know what'd happen if people found out about us."*
:   **Falk:** *"I know, my lady. I just needed to see you outside of court, away from all of the politics."*
:   **Bryling:** *"I'm serious. If Erikur knew about us, he'd force you to resign from your position. And without you helping the Jarl, Solitude would be weaker."*
:   **Falk:** *"You're right, of course. But when this war is over, I'll gladly resign and we can stop sneaking around like this."*
:   **Bryling:** *"One more reason to pray for the fighting to end then, my love."*

The opening scene of [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown") would now also mention him by name:

:   **Tullius:** *"Tell me again, why I'm wasting men chasing after a fairy tale."*
:   **Rikke:** *"If Ulfric gets his hand on that crown, it won't be a fairy tale. It'll be a problem."*
:   **Tullius:** *"Don't you Nords put any stock in your own traditions? I thought the Moot chose the king. We're backing Erikur. When the Moot meets, they'll do the sensible thing."*
:   **Rikke:** *"Not everyone's agreed to the Moot. You've been here long enough to know that Nords aren't always sensible. We follow our hearts."*
:   **Tullius:** *"So what - Ulfric gets this crown and then suddenly he's High King?"*
:   **Rikke:** *"No, it's not as simple as that, but the Jagged Crown would be a potent symbol for his cause to rally around. But, if we found it first..."*
:   **Tullius:** *"And we gave it to Erikur?"*
:   **Rikke:** *"In the absence of the Moot, it would further legitimize his claim."*
:   **Tullius:** *"Perhaps... I'm entrusting you with what resources I can spare. But I'm warning you, if this turns out to be a waste of time and men..."*
:   **Rikke:** *"It won't be a waste."*
:   **Tullius:** *"Make sure you take the Auxiliary here. You can send him/her back when you get there and find nothing but old bones and cobwebs."*
:   **Rikke:** *"The Stonefist's no fool. He's found the Crown. But we'll get to it first."*

## Notes

- During [The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload"), his inflection changes, noticeably sounding quite unlike the usual MaleSlyCynical voice.
- He is under the protection of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). His house is marked several times with the "protected" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)"). Despite this, he may still be the target of a Thieves Guild [special jobs quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Special_Job_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), even if the reputation quest The Dainty Sload has been completed.
- Erikur does not have a unique facial model, he instead uses the default male Nord face. He shares this quirk with numerous other NPCs, including [Briehl](/wiki/Skyrim:Briehl "Skyrim:Briehl"), [Sond](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(bandit) "Skyrim:Sond (bandit)"), [Lynoit](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynoit "Skyrim:Lynoit"), [Barknar](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Barknar (Dawnguard)"), and many other generic NPCs.
- A scene with Gisli implies that Erikur owns the building Radiant Raiment is located in, and the sisters pay him rent. However, a scene Bryling has with [Irnskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand") implies that *she* owns the building and the sisters pay *her* rent, instead.

## Bugs

- When Melaran speaks to Erikur about importing weapons from Black Marsh, his spoken dialogue does not match the subtitles.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Erikur may not appear on the map, making the quest The Dainty Sload impossible. He appears on the main map screen as being situated in the ocean, northeast of the Katariah, however the game directs you from Skyrim to the Blue Palace, and from there no direct path to Erikur can be found.
  - If this bug occurs, Erikur can be found underneath Solitude at the location of the map marker.
  -  Erikur can be moved from the middle of the ocean during The Dainty Sload if you use the following console commands: `prid 000198A9` and `moveto player` .

Eris in the Red Wave

**Eris** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [witchblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchblade "Skyrim:Witchblade") and a pirate aboard the [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave"), under the command of [Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia").

Eris wears [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), a leveled piece of jewelry, a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and an additional small amount of gold. She wields a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), which can be up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") in quality and knows the following spells: [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"), [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), and [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia")**: Kill a [pirate captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") on her own [ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave").

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

:   *"My father was all the family I ever had. I felt so lost when he died. But the crew of the Red Wave's my family now."*
:   *"I've seen some truly wondrous sights since I took to the seas. I had no idea a man could die in so many ways..."*
:   *"Just yesterday, I saw a musician in the street playing a flute. It was... beautiful. I want that flute."*
:   *"[Dorian](/wiki/Skyrim:Dorian "Skyrim:Dorian") is helping me perfect my fencing, but I don't think I'll ever be as good as he is."*

Erith

**Erith**, a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Children "Skyrim:Children"), is the daughter of [Daighre](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre "Skyrim:Daighre"). She can be found in [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine"), just outside [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), and is usually in the company of her faithful companion [Torom](/wiki/Skyrim:Torom "Skyrim:Torom").

She wears [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Daighre%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Daighre's House") to [Daighre's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre%27s_House "Skyrim:Daighre's House"), a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

## Dialogue

When approached she can say:

:   *"Why is everyone so upset? If there's [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), the Jarl will take care of them, right?*"
:   *"Hope [Pavo](/wiki/Skyrim:Pavo_Attius "Skyrim:Pavo Attius") will be able to go back to his mine soon. Everyone needs a home."*
:   *"What'cha doing in Left Hand? Do you dig up rocks too, like my mom?"*
:   *"Why do they call it Left Hand Mine? Can the miners use their right hands too?"*
:   *"Have you met [Torom](/wiki/Skyrim:Torom "Skyrim:Torom")? He's the best dog in the Reach."*

## Conversations

:   **Daighre**: *"[Skaggi](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi_Scar-Face "Skyrim:Skaggi Scar-Face") tells me that you were bothering him today. Can't you and Torom just play by yourselves?"*
:   **Erith**: *"But mom, it's so boring with just me and Torom. I was just asking Skaggi some questions."*
:   **Daighre**: *"You leave him alone. I don't want to hear Skaggi telling me you've been bothering him again!"*
:   **Erith**: *"Yes, ma'am."*

:   **Erith**: *"Mama, can we talk. You know, about papa?"*
:   **Daighre**: *"Of course, sweetie. What'd you like to know?"*
:   **Erith**: *"I don't know. What'd he look like?"*
:   **Daighre**: *"He had your soft face, and that silly grin you get when you've done something wrong. That's his, too."*

## Notes

- Should you choose to adopt Erith, you will see Torom in your house every so often since his AI will have him seek out Erith, regardless of her location.

## Bugs

- Erith's bed isn't a child's bed, so she stays up all night.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Erj

## Overview

| Erj (RefID: 00093857) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Nchuand-Zel Armory](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel_Armory "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel Armory") | | |
| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer_(class) "Skyrim:Conjurer (class)") |

Erj

**Erj** is a dead [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") found in the [Nchuand-Zel Armory](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel_Armory "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel Armory"). His [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Erj%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Erj's Notes") can be found next to him.

## Related Quests

- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").

## Notes

- Reanimating Erj's corpse will also reanimate Erj's Familiar, a ghost wolf.

Erlendr in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)")

**Erlendr**, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), is one of the souls in the [Hall of Valor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Valor "Skyrim:Hall of Valor"). He was turned to stone by the wizard [Grimkell](/wiki/Lore:Grimkell "Lore:Grimkell"), along with [Hunroor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunroor "Skyrim:Hunroor") and [Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas "Skyrim:Nikulas"), while on a quest to find [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").

## Related Quests

- **[Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)")**: Seek out [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") within [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").

## Notes

- Erlendr is first mentioned in the quest [Betrayal at Brodir Grove](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Betrayal_at_Brodir_Grove "Bloodmoon:Betrayal at Brodir Grove") in [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon").

Ernanthil

**Ernanthil** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who offers the player a [rogue's job](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogue%27s_Job_Offer "Skyrim:Rogue's Job Offer"), when [the cup of Fortune](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortunate_Son#The_Cup_of_Fortune "Skyrim:Fortunate Son") is chosen at the [Roadside Ruins.](/wiki/Skyrim:Roadside_Ruins "Skyrim:Roadside Ruins") All interactions with him are by dead-drop letters until he finally appears in Eslaf's room in [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") during your battle with his brother [Cuinanthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Cuinanthil "Skyrim:Cuinanthil"), the course of which he watches.

He wears typical thieves guild garb that cannot be looted. He wields a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and carries [a journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ernanthil%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ernanthil's Journal"), leveled [rich items](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich_Pocket_Contents "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") and a copy of the skill book *[Thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(book) "Skyrim:Thief (book)")*.

## Related Quests

- **[Fortunate Son](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortunate_Son "Skyrim:Fortunate Son")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Claim a fortune.

## Quest-Related Dialogue

After killing [Cuinanthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Cuinanthil "Skyrim:Cuinanthil"):

:   *"I'm surprised you succeeded. Please accept this as payment."*

:   :   **It was a pleasure working with you.**
    :   *"Yes, yes, thank you and all that. But enough of this. Such things are best forgotten."*

:   :   **I still have questions.**
    :   *"Not my problem. But enough of this. Such things are best forgotten."*

:   :   **I think I'll just kill you and take it all.**
    :   *"What in the world..."* **(Turns hostile)**

:   :   **This isn't enough. You barely did any work and just showed up at the end.**
    :   *"It can't be helped. But enough of this. Such things are best forgotten."*

If you attempt to speak to him again he will brush you off:

:   *"Yes, yes, thank you and all that. But enough of this. Such things are best forgotten."*

Erwan

Erwan is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") hedge wizard encountered at [Traitor's Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Traitor%27s_Post "Skyrim:Traitor's Post") during the related quest. She and her bandit companions are hostile and will attack on sight.

Erwan is a former member of the [Crimson Dirks](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Dirks "Skyrim:Crimson Dirks") and appears to be quite mentally disturbed; she has killed the merchant [Gunther](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunther "Skyrim:Gunther") and now considers his corpse to be her "best friend". Gunther had been sent her way by her brother Edward as a "gift", along with a copy of *[The Crimson Dirks, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v5 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v5")* which describes her earlier life.

She wears [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots") and wields an [elven war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_War_Axe "Skyrim:Elven War Axe"). She also carried a [Dwarven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), and eight [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), as well as her [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Erwan%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Erwan's Journal") and a [letter from Edward](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Edward "Skyrim:Letter from Edward"). She utilizes [frost damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") spells in combat such as [Frost Cloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Cloak "Skyrim:Frost Cloak"). You will be required to kill her and read her journal as part of the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
