Evette San

Evette at the Burning of King Olaf festival

**Evette San** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [food vendor](/wiki/Skyrim:Food_Vendor "Skyrim:Food Vendor") who has a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Evette San's House") and a market stall in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). She deals in a variety of [wines](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") and other beverages. Her latest shipment of spiced wine has been halted by the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") and she needs someone to convince them to release it.

Her business very much depends on the annual Festival held by the Bards College, but since [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg")'s death at the hands of [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), and with the widowed [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair") declaring the Festival as 'poor taste', Evette sees no real future for her unique spiced wine.

She owns a house in Solitude, right across the street from [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor"), and sleeps there every night between midnight and 6am. After waking up she heads directly to the market stalls and spends fourteen hours offering her various beverages, including her trademark [Spiced Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine"), based on an old family recipe created by her father, infamous town drunk [Octieve San](/wiki/Skyrim:Octieve_San "Skyrim:Octieve San"). At 8pm she heads back to the house and spends the rest of the evening there, either eating, wandering or relaxing. There are two exceptions to her daily routine. When you arrive in Solitude for the first time, she will be amidst the crowd witnessing the execution of [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir"). During the Burning of King Olaf Festival, near the conclusion of the quest [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames"), she will sell her goods near the entrance to the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College") and will even hand you a few bottles of spiced wine, as a reward for saving the festival.

Selling her wine hasn't made her rich and her attire reflects that, a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of cheap [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261bd "Skyrim:Clothing"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries her [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Evette_San%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Evette San's House"), a spare [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Spiced Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:The Spiced Wine")**: Convince [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") to hand over some spices.

## Dialogue

When she is at her stall, she will often try and attract customers by yelling:

:   *"Spiced Wine to warm the blood!"*
:   *"Keep the cold at bay with our spiced wine!"*
:   *"Spiced wine, the taste of home and hearth!"*

When you get near her, she will try to sell her produce even harder:

:   *"Spiced wine for ya? It's a family recipe."*
:   *"Wanderer like you needs a little fire in the veins. Some spiced wine?"*
:   *"I swear, I left another bottle right here..."*
:   *"If you see my father Octieve around, stay clear. He'll only ask you for money or mead."*

When spoken to:

:   **Is your spiced wine made from a secret recipe?**
:   *"Oh, yes. A secret family recipe. The only good thing my father Octieve ever did. In fact, it's so good, no one else in Skyrim even tries to make any."*

When finishing conversation, she will remark:

:   *"Good luck out there. It seems like a tough time to be wandering Skyrim."*
:   *"Stay warm and keep sober. It's the two things I know for sure will make life better."*

When asked about her business, before starting the quest [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")

:   **How are your sales?**
:   *"They're... adequate. Honestly, I rely on the business brought in by the Burning of King Olaf, and that's not likely to happen this year."*
:   **What's the Burning of King Olaf?**
:   *"It's a great big festival put on by the bards, every year. They burn an effigy of old King Olaf. It's quite a bit of fun. The bards give out spiced wine during the festival, so they put in a big order. And then, for weeks after, demand is so high, I can barely keep up. But with the death of High King Torygg, the Festival has been declared "in poor taste." So it looks like it won't happen this year."*

After Tending the Flames is complete:

:   **How are your sales?**
:   *"Oh, very brisk. When the snow sets in, even the hardiest Nord needs some spiced wine to warm the blood."*

### Festival Dialogue

However, once you save the Festival, Evette will be overly excited and can be found near the Bards College during the festivities, offering her spiced wine as always:

:   *"Spiced Wine here. First cup is paid for by the college."*
:   *"Get some Spiced Wine. A Festival Favorite."*

Not surprisingly, she will treat you with the utmost respect and hand you a few bottles with the words:

:   *"Just one bottle per customer. Except for the man who saved the festival. Here's a couple bottles for you."*

### The Spiced Wine

In addition to her problems with the festival, Evette also faces huge problems with the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") as they have been holding back supplies. If you have yet to start the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death"), Evette will greet you with:

:   *"You wouldn't have a few minutes to run down to the docks would you?"*
:   **What do you need from the docks?**
:   *"I've got a shipment of Spices the East Empire Company is holding up. I need someone to convince them to release it."*

:   :   **I'm not really heading that way.**
    :   *"Ah well. I'll keep looking for someone. Thanks anyway."*

:   :   **Shouldn't be a problem.**
    :   *"Great. Get back to me when you're done and I'll give you something for your time."*

When you return from [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici"), Evette will be pleased to see her shipment released:

:   **The East Empire Company is sending up your spices.**
:   *"Thank you so much. I swear it's a fight with them every shipment. Here's something for your troubles."*

## Conversations

When working at the market, Evette will quite often engage in conversations with the townsfolk:

:   **[Aia](/wiki/Skyrim:Aia_Arria "Skyrim:Aia Arria")**: *"You know, my father collected exotic alcohols."*
:   **Evette**: *"Really?"*
:   **Aia**: *"Rum from [Hammerfell](/wiki/Lore:Hammerfell "Lore:Hammerfell"), mulled wine from [Daggerfall](/wiki/Lore:Daggerfall "Lore:Daggerfall") and the like."* **or**
:   *"None of what he collected tasted as good as your Spiced Wine, Evette."* **or**
:   *"I'm still finding your Spiced Wine to be the best drink I've ever tasted."*
:   **Evette**: *"Thanks, Aia. That means a lot."* **or**
:   *"Glad to hear it, Aia."*

:   **Evette**: *"Spiced Wine for the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever")?"*
:   **[Sorex](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius")**: *"Actually just a bottle for me today. I'm thinking of giving it to [Vivienne](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis")."*
:   **Evette**: *"Sure, Sorex. Just like you did the last one."*
:   **Sorex**: *"The last one was a warm up."*

:   **[Silana](/wiki/Skyrim:Silana_Petreia "Skyrim:Silana Petreia")**: *"Are your sales going well?"* **or** *"I hope the Divines have been keeping you well."*
:   **Evette**: *"Not too bad. A few of the guests from the upcoming wedding have placed orders."* **or** *"They seem to when you're around Silana."*
:   **Silana**: *"It should be quite the affair. Nice to have something happy in the midst of the war."* **or** *"Vittoria is practically glowing."*

:   **Evette**: *"A bit of warming wine, [Illdi](/wiki/Skyrim:Illdi "Skyrim:Illdi").*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *You know you can't resist."*
:   **Illdi**: *"Not fair. You're well aware I can't seem to get warm here."* **or** *"Do you know I look forward to Burning of King Olaf each year just because of the fire?"*

:   **[Rorlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorlund "Skyrim:Rorlund")**: *"Ah a few bottles of Spiced Wine should hit the spot."*
:   **Evette**: *"Of course. And I'm sure it's mostly for ceremonial purposes."*

:   **[Ataf](/wiki/Skyrim:Ataf "Skyrim:Ataf")**: *"I'll take a bottle of spiced wine."*
:   **Evette**: *"I haven't known you to drink before, Ataf."* **or** *"A bottle of spiced wine for ya, Ataf?"*
:   **Ataf**: *"Viarmo is trying to get Elisif to allow the Burning of King Olaf. I don't want to look like I don't know how to drink in front of the other bards."* **or** *"No thank you. I'm still feeling sick from the festival."*

:   **[Jawanan](/wiki/Skyrim:Jawanan "Skyrim:Jawanan")**: *"I think I may wait until the Burning of King Olaf to have and*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *Spiced Wine."*
:   **Evette**: *"You and everyone else. Word is it may not happen this year though."*

Back at home, she and her father may chat:

:   **Evette**: *"Father, could you clean up the house a little while I'm away?"*
:   **Octieve**: *"Maybe. I'll see if I feel like it."*
:   **Evette**: *"I'm on my feet all day. Can you please do this one thing for me?"*
:   **Octieve**: *"Sure, whatever."*

:   **Octieve**: *"Where've you been all day?"*
:   **Evette**: *"At the market, father."*
:   **Octieve**: *"Well, did you bring back any mead?"*
:   **Evette**: *"I barely make enough for us to eat as it is, father. You can't just drink it all away."*
:   **Octieve**: *"Humph. Some daughter you are."*

## Notes

- If you [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") [Octieve San](/wiki/Skyrim:Octieve_San "Skyrim:Octieve San"), Evette will technically become your stepdaughter.
- Evette and her spiced wine are mentioned in *[The Elder Scrolls: The Official Cookbook](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls:_The_Official_Cookbook "Books:The Elder Scrolls: The Official Cookbook")*.

## Bugs

- Evette may stop giving out free Spiced Wine to female players.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. It was due to a previous script added by the USKP that later went missing.

# Skyrim:Evil in Waiting

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Seal away an [ancient evil](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume") |
| Reward: | [Hevnoraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(item) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (item)"), [Hevnoraak's Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak%27s_Staff "Skyrim:Hevnoraak's Staff"),  Word for the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") shout. |
| ID: | dunValthumeQST |
| Suggested Level: | 24 |

[Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter [Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume") and speak to the ghost named [Valdar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdar "Skyrim:Valdar").
2. Collect the [vessels](/wiki/Skyrim:Opaque_Vessel "Skyrim:Opaque Vessel") from each of Hevnoraak's [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") minions.
3. Kill the [Dragon Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Hevnoraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)").

### The Forgotten Ruin

*"Leave, stranger. Evil stirs in this place."*

The [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") of [Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume") lies southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") at the end of the path that leads southeast from [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"). No citizens will ever mention the ruin, although the Greybeards may detect a "whisper of a [word](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power")" from the location, as there is a [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") in the ruin. They can point you in the right direction.

When you arrive there will be no enemies guarding the exterior door leading into the side of the great mountain, but there is a possibility of a troll encounter, so be on guard. Enter [Valthume Vestibule](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume_Vestibule "Skyrim:Valthume Vestibule") and you will immediately be sought out by a ghost named [Valdar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdar "Skyrim:Valdar") who will provide a warning: *"Leave, stranger. Evil stirs in this place. I fear for the security of the very land if it should break free."* If you ask for more details, the ghost will elaborate on the danger that lurks within: *"We stand at the tomb of Hevnoraak, who has been dead for many generations. I fear, however, that his return may be at hand."*

Valdar reveals that he stayed behind to constrain the power of the [Dragon Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Hevnoraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)"), but that his own strength is fading away. Due to this weakness, he needs a champion to find three vessels scattered around the large ruin; their combined power can help vanquish Hevnoraak, thus saving the land of Skyrim from his vengeance. Accept the challenge and Valdar will open a gate in the back of the vestibule leading to the real ruin of Valthume. He will then sit down on his throne atop his own skeleton, and you can gather some more information on the threat waiting to break out of his prison: *"Hevnoraak planned his resurrection obsessively before dying. My duty in life and in death is to make sure he stays in this tomb for eternity."* Apparently, Valthume was a former den of dragon worshippers, with Hevnoraak as their leader: *"He had a way of enthralling people and built up a loyal army of followers. Good men fell under his spell and were forever twisted. Made... evil. After that, fear was enough to keep them in line. He could torture and humiliate them and they would not rebel. Even in death, they serve him still."*

### Valthume

*"Even in death, they serve him still."*

While the exterior of the ruin only consists of a single door, the ruin of Valthume is incredibly large and far from linear; make sure to keep an eye on the map markers and prepare for a fairly long trek to gather all three vessels. The first chamber is huge, with no enemies in sight. Hevnoraak's sarcophagus stands in the middle of the room, sealed shut, with his throne strategically placed in the background. You can do nothing here now, so locate the southern stairway and jump over the [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") to avoid the corresponding [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") around the corner. Proceed forward and dispose of the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") enemies. The door to the south is sealed shut from the other side, so go through the tunnel to the east.

Before long, you will stand in a huge chamber, clearly an area for offerings, which is inhabited by two leveled draugr. The overhanging ledges provide an opportunity for ranged attacks. Claim some loot in a hidden room above the altar, by jumping to the side balcony, then jump again to the corner balcony, and then jump yet again to reach the altar. then jump down and open the chest on the floor. There is a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") that will net you a fight against four [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and a draugr carrying the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Valthume Cellar Key") to escape the trap, but little else. Instead, take the southern tunnel and open the door to your right for the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill book *[Withershins](/wiki/Skyrim:Withershins "Skyrim:Withershins")*. You will pass a tantalizing expert-locked door, however it leads only to the aforementioned pit containing the spiders.

Return to the tunnel and make your way through several fire traps and beware of the four pressure plates triggering [darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"). The room contains two exits, both of them closed, so pull the handle near the eastern stone wall and watch it lower. Behind you, the metal gate will disappear as well, but ignore it for now and choose the eastern path. Before long, you will be attacked by a boss-leveled draugr protecting the first of the [opaque vessels](/wiki/Skyrim:Opaque_Vessel "Skyrim:Opaque Vessel"). After the battle, claim the vessel and the quest will update with a new map marker.

Backtrack to the previous room and follow the path unveiled behind the metal gate. The next chamber is divided into two levels, and several draugr will welcome you with open hostility as you enter. Dispose of them, cross the bridge and [unlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") the door on the other side for some minor loot and useful potions. The room to the northeast on the lower level contains a handle that opens a tunnel leading to a room you glimpsed earlier filled with some minor loot. Return to the two-leveled chamber and locate the eastern door, leading to the next zone, Valthume Catacombs.

### The Catacombs

The Catacombs

The first chamber of the catacombs features a chest in plain sight; when you open it, the attached [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") will cause a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider") to be released from above, along with several regular arachnids. Locate the eastern gate, pull the handle, and approach the catacomb area. Battle your way through the undead enemies and watch out for the pressure plate on the floor. Locate the gate in the northwestern part of the area and pull the chain in the alcove behind you. Face another leveled draugr and claim the second [vessel](/wiki/Skyrim:Opaque_Vessel "Skyrim:Opaque Vessel") from the pedestal. Before leaving, get rid of the [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") on the small pedestals, for an easier exploration later.

Locate the other exit from the catacombs and pass by the holes in the wall, now peaceful without the trapped soul gems. More catacombs await in the following area, guarded by even more draugr enemies, be also sure to watch out for a pressure plate and [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Traps") trap. Make your way to the gate and pull the chain. As you explore the next huge chamber, more enemies will burst out of their sarcophagi, so fight them, then find the stairs and walk down to the level below. Continue through the western path to an iron door, open it, and fight three frostbite spiders guarding the [iron claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Claw "Skyrim:Iron Claw"). As you lift the claw from the pedestal, the four [flamethrower statues](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") will all shoot at you, so head to the [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Traps") and turn the rings as depicted on the iron claw: **Dragon—Hawk—Wolf**. Activate the keyhole and the gate will open, allowing access to the final room.

The vessel is guarded by a boss-leveled draugr along with several leveled draugr, so prepare for the tough battle and claim the last [opaque vessel](/wiki/Skyrim:Opaque_Vessel "Skyrim:Opaque Vessel"). When you take it, the nearby iron gate will open and provide access to a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") with a word for the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") shout, along with a boss-leveled chest. It is time to return the three vessels to [Valdar](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdar "Skyrim:Valdar"), so find the western gate for a quick shortcut back to Valthume. Raise the door bar and you will find Valdar waiting for you in the throne room.

### Hevnoraak

*"Fools! You will not hold me here any longer, Valdar!"*

When you return to Valdar with the three vessels, Valdar will congratulate you and explain their original purpose. The dragon priest used them to extract his blood, his goal being to resurrect himself after death to become an exceedingly powerful lich. Your task is to empty the vessels, thus making it impossible for the priest to regain his formidable powers. The ghost will point you towards the sconce in front of the throne, so head up there and fill the sconce with the blood from the vessels. The ritual also requires you to sit in the throne, so take a seat and witness Valdar's resurrection of the weakened Hevnoraak.

As the ritual is completed, the dragon priest will burst out of his coffin and yell: *"Fools! You will not hold me here any longer, Valdar!"* Valdar will immediately seek shelter, and it is up to you to fight the powerful dragon priest. He will use [his staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak%27s_Staff "Skyrim:Hevnoraak's Staff") to cast walls of lightning towards you, which create a lasting [shock damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Shock_Damage "Skyrim:Shock Damage") effect. Dodge the powerful attack and corner the priest, then dispose of him as quickly as possible. When all is said and done, claim his staff and loot his [dragon priest mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(item) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (item)") and a huge amount of gold from his remains. Valdar will thank you wholeheartedly, not only for saving Skyrim, but also for freeing him from his eternal duty as guardian inside Valthume. The ghost will then disappear and the quest will end.

## Notes

- The bars in front of the word wall are removed as a result of you "reaching over" the *pedestal* of the third vessel to pick it up, not the acquisition of the vessel itself. As a result, if the vessel is sent flying during combat the word wall will seem to be unreachable and bugged. To fix it and lower the spikes, just jump over the pedestal.
- All the chains and handles for doors are right next to or just before them. You should be able to locate them easily.
- As you approach the area around [Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume"), you will experience short, strong earthquakes. These earthquakes are not related to the quest, but are rather attributable to the ruins of [Arkngthamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Arkngthamz "Skyrim:Arkngthamz") in the mountains nearby. The earthquakes will stop once you've entered the Dwemer ruin and begin the quest [Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages").
- Valthume has a large number of filled urns and burial jars, which makes it worthwhile to complete the [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned") quest before going there.

## Bugs

- If the dragon claw door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- The spikes blocking the word wall may be reactivated by dragon shouts or objects hitting the opaque vessel's pedestal. This can leave you trapped.
  - Use a ranged shout like Unrelenting Force on the pedestal holding the opaque vessel.
- In some cases, an opaque vessel may be forced through a wall, such as by blasts or shouts. This can leave the vessel unobtainable. **?**
  - Call the console commands "player.removeitem 8d770 1" then "player.removeitem 3e6bb 1" then "player.removeitem 3e6bc 1" to remove all existing vessels since it's hard to find which one(s) you're missing.
  - Call the console commands "player.additem 8d770 1" then "player.additem 3e6bb 1" then "player.additem 3e6bc 1" to add each vessel to your inventory.
  - Call the console command "setstage dunValthumeQST 10" to advance the quest. Valdar will now accept your progress and prepare for the ritual.
- If the opaque vessel is knocked down from the pedestal, the spikes blocking the word wall can be activated by placing an item on it if jumping over does not work.
- Walking just west of Valthume the game will freeze. Noted about were the juniper tree is located on the western road.
- Hevnoraak may not emerge from his coffin on completing the ritual. **?**
  - Call the console commands "prid 4CF61" and then "enable".
  - He can be forced out with a rune spell (like Fire Rune) or a Shout (like Unrelenting Force or Marked For Death) cast at his coffin.
- After defeating Hevnoraak, the quest may not disappear from your quest list.
- When Hevnoraak emerges from his coffin, his hitbox may be faulty; arrows fly through his torso as if nothing was there. Aiming at his knees and lower legs may result in a hit, but arrows can phase through these parts of his body occasionally, too. Area-of-effect magic (such as Fireball) and melee attacks don't seem to be affected.
- Sometimes the ghost of Valdar will not approach the player upon entering the tomb. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Evil in Waiting (dunValthumeQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 3 |  | A spirit known as Valdar has asked me to collect three vessels in Valthume to defeat the Dragon Priest Hevnoraak. *Objective 5:* Collect the Vessels (<Global=dunValthumeVesselCollectedCount>/3) |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Perform the ritual with Valdar |
| 15 |  | Valdar has asked me to collect three vessels in Valthume to defeat the Dragon Priest Hevnoraak. I brought the vessels to Valdar who told me the vessels contained the blood of Hevnoraak. I am to use this blood in a ritual to defeat him. |
| 40 |  | *Objective 15:* Defeat Hevnoraak |
| 50 |  | Valdar has asked me to collect three vessels in Valthume to defeat the Dragon Priest Hevnoraak. I brought the vessels to Valdar who told me the vessels contained the blood of Hevnoraak. I used the blood to weaken and awaken Hevnoraak, and defeated him. |
| 60 | ☑ | Vader *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* has asked me to collect three vessels in Valthume to defeat the Dragon Priest Hevnoraak. I brought the vessels to Valdar who told me the vessels contained the blood of Hevnoraak. I used the blood to weaken and awaken Hevnoraak, and defeated him. Valdar told me to take his iron mask and faded away. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 2, 5, 20, 30.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunValthumeQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunValthumeQST`.

Evul Seloth

**Evul Seloth** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who lives in [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") after it is reopened. He wears [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"), and he carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

He shares dialogue with his fellow miners:

:   *"It's good to get back to mining after all these years."*
:   *"This mine's amazing! Have you ever seen so much ebony in your life?"*
:   *"I've been out of the business so long, I almost forgot how to swing a pickaxe."*
:   *"Good to know that the mine's safe again. I heard a lot of strange things happened here."*
:   *"Getting your hands dirty, outlander?"*
:   *"Help yourself to as much ore as you like... you've earned it."*
:   *"I haven't set foot in these mines for ages. It's strange being back after so long."*
:   *"There's nothing quite like the sound of metal striking rock."*
:   *"Nice to be making some coin again."*
:   *"Thanks to House Redoran getting these mines reopened, I can provide for my family again."*
:   *"Welcome to Raven Rock Mine, outlander."*

## Notes

- He shares a surname with [Malur Seloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Malur_Seloth "Skyrim:Malur Seloth"), who lives in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), but there is no indication that they are related.

# Skyrim:Experimental Subject (A)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [75.166.104.64](/wiki/Special:Contributions/75.166.104.64 "Special:Contributions/75.166.104.64"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Likelolwhat](/wiki/User:Likelolwhat "User:Likelolwhat"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

For the alternate version, see [Experimental Subject (B)](/wiki/Skyrim:Experimental_Subject_(B) "Skyrim:Experimental Subject (B)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Help [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") by being a test subject in his experiment.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | 250 gold |
| ID: | DLC2TTR4a |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** Any time after speaking to Neloth during [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") except when finding him a new steward | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Any time after speaking to Neloth during [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward") except when finding him a new steward | | |

*"You won't feel a thing. But if you do, try not to scream too loudly. My ears are sensitive."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
2. Allow him to cast an [experimental spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth%27s_Health_Boost "Skyrim:Neloth's Health Boost") on you.
3. Enter the water at any point in gameplay.
4. Return to Neloth to report the side effects of his spell.

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") will request you help him with an experiment. Agree and he will cast an [experimental spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth%27s_Health_Boost "Skyrim:Neloth's Health Boost") on you, instructing you to report to him any side effects. The spell will endow you with 25 additional points of health. You can observe the status of the effect through the Active Effects section of your magic menu. The effect is permanent until you submerge yourself up to arm's length in water. Doing so will then cause a 25 point decrease to health permanently until you return to Neloth. Streams running through caves, and other shallow water regions should not affect this, nor should wading in shallow water for any period of time. It is therefore possible by carefully avoiding deep water to maintain this bonus for a significant period. By obtaining [Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Boots_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking") during [Unearthed](/wiki/Skyrim:Unearthed "Skyrim:Unearthed") this bonus can theoretically be maintained indefinitely, provided you manage to stay out of the rain (some players have reported that rain induces the negative effects).
Returning to Neloth and reporting the negative effects will result in him removing the spell, which will set you back to normal. He will then reward you 250 gold regardless of your level.

## Notes

- Any body of liquid, such as the acid in [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") or the lava in [The Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge"), counts as water for the purposes of this quest.

## Bugs

- When Neloth asks if you are willing to be an experimental subject, the dialogue may end without presenting the option "What kind of experiment". This means the quest cannot be started.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  - It may also break the Research quest chain. Completing another quest for Neloth may restore the proper dialogue functions.

## Quest Stages

| Experimental Subject (DLC2TTR4a) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | I let Neloth cast an experimental spell on me. If I discover any side effects, I should tell him right away. *Objective 100:* Watch for side effects |
| 200 |  | I let Neloth cast an experimental spell on me. I've discovered a potentially dangerous side effect. Normally it boosts my health, but if I am in the rain or swim, it reduces my health. *Objective 200:* Talk to Neloth |
| 300 | ☑ |  |
| 400 | ☒ | Neloth asked me to be a test subject for one of his experiments. I refused. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR4a stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR4a`.

# Skyrim:Experimental Subject (B)

## Overview

For the alternate version, see [Experimental Subject (A)](/wiki/Skyrim:Experimental_Subject_(A) "Skyrim:Experimental Subject (A)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") by being a test subject in his experiment.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | 250 gold |
| ID: | DLC2TTR4b |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** [Azra's Staffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Azra%27s_Staffs "Skyrim:Azra's Staffs") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | [Azra's Staffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Azra%27s_Staffs "Skyrim:Azra's Staffs") | | |

*"You won't feel a thing. But if you do, try not to scream too loudly. My ears are sensitive."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
2. Allow him to cast a [new silence spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells#Silence "Skyrim:Spells") on you.
3. Demand repayment for the spell's failure.

### The Eighth Silence

[Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") is excited about his new research. Offer to help and he will explain that he is working on a new silence spell. If you agree to help Neloth will reply, *"Excellent. If this works, I'll prepare a version that you can cast yourself, if you ever wish to inflict... er, study silence."* He will then prepare and cast the spell.

### Tentacle Things

You will be rendered blind for a short time, and your stamina will drain. In the dark, Neloth will speak to you, while a panicked [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") interjects:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Talvas:** | *"Master Neloth! What have you done to him/her? What are those things growing out of his/her eyes?"* |
| **Neloth:** | *"Well that's unexpected. I presume you are blind, given the state of your eyes. It's nothing that can't be fixed. The spell that is. I think I can fix the spell. It should only take a couple more years. But first, I need some data. Try wiggling them. No, don't shake your fist. Wiggle the tentacle things where your eyes used to be."* |
| **Talvas:** | *"I think I'm going to be sick."* |
| **Neloth:** | *"Hmm. From the way they are waving about, I'm assuming they aren't under your control. And I see now that your tongue is also...well, it's probably best if I don't say. Don't bother trying to scream though."* |
| **Talvas:** | *(Vomits)* |
| **Talvas:** | *"Is it over yet? Does he/she have eyes again?"* |
| **Neloth:** | *"It looks like it's beginning to wear off. Hmm. Your eyes appear to be completely back to normal. Interesting."* |

### Compensation

Your sight will automatically be restored at this point. You can ask Neloth for compensation:

:   **I think you owe me for that spell.**
:   *"I suppose I do. It's too bad it wore off so quickly though. Unfortunately you don't appear to be suffering from any side effects. Anyway, take this for your time."*

He will give you 250 gold.

## Bugs

- After the conversation is completed your screen may remain black. UI elements will be visible, but the environment will not.
  - One way to solve the blindsight is to open a black book. **?**

## Quest Stages

| 300 | ☒ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR4b stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR4b`.

# Skyrim:Extracting an Argonian

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Rescue [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") from his [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") captors.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing"), [Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass") |
| Reward: | [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") as a potential [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | +1 ([Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus")) |
| ID: | DarkwaterCrossingDerkeethusRescueQuest |
| Suggested Spells: | [Muffle](/wiki/Skyrim:Muffle_(spell) "Skyrim:Muffle (spell)"), [Fire Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") |
| Suggested Level: | 9+ |

Derkeethus, trapped in the cave where you find him

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to the residents of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing").
2. Travel to [Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass").
3. Search the cave for [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus").
4. Free Derkeethus from his prison.
5. Escort Derkeethus out of the cave.

### Darkwater Crossing

If you talk to the residents of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") (for example [Sondas Drenim](/wiki/Skyrim:Sondas_Drenim "Skyrim:Sondas Drenim"), a miner in nearby [Goldenrock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenrock_Mine "Skyrim:Goldenrock Mine")), you will soon hear of an Argonian named [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") who recently went to explore the pools around Darkwater - and who hasn't been seen in a long time. The residents will not be able to say for sure where Derkeethus is, but he has actually run into trouble inside [Darkwater Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pass "Skyrim:Darkwater Pass").

Locating Darkwater Pass can be difficult. The easiest route from Darkwater Crossing is to cross the bridge that spans the river to the southwest of the settlement. At the crossing, take the right path. Just before you reach the second bridge and [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol"), a stone marker to the left of the road will indicate a dusty path heading west up the mountainside. Follow the path as it curves sharply south, and onward through the trees along the cliff's edge. Eventually you will come to a large pool fed by three large waterfalls. Drop into the pool and turn directly around to the north - an iron door in the cliff wall in front of you leads to Darkwater Pass.

### Darkwater Pass

Follow the low tunnel past an unlocked chest, and you will reach a small cavern. Watch out - a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") will drop out of a [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") in the wall immediately to your right as you enter. Follow the path up into a larger cavern. A Falmer waits immediately ahead outside a tent, and yet another may drop from a hive above and to the left. In the north wall is an opening into a pillared chamber where three [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") reside. Head past this chamber and up the stairs to reach a small room with a trap door in the center. Look down through the bars to see [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") pacing about in his cell below. Be mindful of the Falmer in the adjoining room with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") (step in here and two more Falmer will drop from the hives up near the ceiling).

Northeast from the center of the trap door, there is a lever on the wall. Pulling this lever lowers a section of wall, revealing a spiral staircase heading down. A corridor in the west wall leads south to a small circular room called Darkwater Pit. As soon as you approach, Derkeethus will engage you in conversation and ask you to help him escape. The [Darkwater Pit Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Pit_Key "Skyrim:Darkwater Pit Key") is in the left [Burial Urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") just inside the gate, but the gate is the standard barred prison cell door with sufficient gaps to allow you to reach through and take the key from the burial urn. If he has lockpicks in his inventory, Derkeethus may have already escaped his cell and be waiting somewhere in the corridor. If this has happened, it may alert the Falmer in the arcane enchanter room.

Although there is still more of Darkwater Pass to explore, the easiest way to get Derkeethus out is to head straight back the way you came - particularly as he will not crouch into a sneaking stance when you do during this quest, and there are some nasty traps and Falmer further up the cave.

Once you have led Derkeethus to safety, he will thank you for saving him. You can now recruit him as a follower if you wish. If not, you can recruit him at any time from Darkwater Crossing.

## Notes

- Derkeethus will only continue to follow you if you remain close to him. If you move too far away he will turn around and return to the pit he started in.
- On rare occasions Derkeethus may appear on the trail between the upper and lower entrances to Darkwater Pass, begging for help escaping the cave. Just lead him to the lower entrance. He will thank you and promptly vanish. He may then be found at Darkwater Crossing.
- This quest can sometimes clash with a [Companions quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") where an NPC needs to be rescued, potentially giving you two temporary followers.

## Bugs

- Residents may only talk about Derkeethus going missing and give no quest or objectives. Locating his cage in Darkwater Pass should bring you to quest stage 20.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=10616))
- Derkeethus may not follow you once freed from his prison. Attempt normal resolutions - waiting, talking, leaving and returning, or reloading the game.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12066)).

## Quest Stages

| Extracting an Argonian (DarkwaterCrossingDerkeethusRescueQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |

| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Get Derkeethus out of the cave. |
| 200 | ☑ | I rescued Derkeethus from the Falmer of Darkwater Pass, and he's returned to his home in Darkwater Crossing. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 205.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DarkwaterCrossingDerkeethusRescueQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DarkwaterCrossingDerkeethusRescueQuest`.

## Overview

Eydis

**Eydis** is a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:EncClassBanditMelee "Skyrim:EncClassBanditMelee") who can be found in [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz"). She wears a [Skaal coat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Coat "Skyrim:Skaal Coat") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Boots "Skyrim:Skaal Boots") and [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Hat "Skyrim:Skaal Hat"). She carries an enchanted [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") and her [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eydis's Journal"), and may also carry a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a small amount of gold. Reading her journal will reveal that she came to Fahlbtharz with [Ulyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulyn "Skyrim:Ulyn") to help him search for the [Visage of Mzund](/wiki/Skyrim:Visage_of_Mzund "Skyrim:Visage of Mzund"), an enchanted Dwarven helmet. She and Ulyn were forced to defend themselves against [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider"), and [Ulyn's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulyn%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ulyn's Journal") indicates that he went further into the ruin while she stayed back to hold them off—to her obvious misfortune.

# Skyrim:Eydis

## Overview

This article is about the Nord in the base game. For the Bandit added by Dragonborn, see [Eydis (Dragonborn)](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Eydis (Dragonborn)").

Eydis at the [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn")

**Eydis** is the owner and publican of the [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn"). She works there with her son [Skuli](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuli "Skyrim:Skuli") and [Leontius Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius"). Skuli's father has gone missing and Eydis can be overheard lying to her son about his whereabouts. She will relate some of the inn's history—especially the story of the time [Tiber Septim](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim") stayed there after leading the invasion of Old Hrol'dan. The room she rents is the very room that he slept in.

Eydis will spend all of her time tending to her inn, never sleeping or taking a break from her duties as publican.

She wears a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0005b6a1 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Shoes") befitting a barkeeper. Eydis is armed with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") to defend herself from potential threats. Additionally, she carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Key to Old Hroldan Inn") to her home as well as a variety of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

Her greetings:

:   *"Don't underestimate my son, Skuli. He may look young, but he can handle any drunks we get."*
:   *"Skuli's father is off fighting for the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")/[Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). I'm sure he's just fine."*
:   *"Old Hroldan is the stone that the Empire's history is built on."*
:   *"Ah, a visitor. Old Hroldan Inn has hundreds of years of history, friend."*

## Quest-Related Events

The first time you approach Eydis she will greet you by presuming you will want to stay in Tiber Septim's old room:

:   *"You'll be looking to rent Tiber Septim's room I take it?"*
:   **Tiber Septim's room?**
:   *"That's right. In the Second Era, Tiber Septim himself led the army that conquered Old Hroldan from the barbarians of the Reach. Septim would later found the Empire that united [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"), but his first known battle and victory was right here. And this inn has the very bed the great general slept in on his first night as Old Hroldan's liberator. As good as it was hundreds of years ago."*
:   **I'll rent Tiber Septim's room. (10 gold)**
:   *"Have a good rest. It's the big room with the double bed."*

Sleeping in the rented bed will lead to you being awakened to the sound of Eydis screaming, leading to the beginning of her [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan"). A [ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") has appeared in the inn, terrifying the hostess. Approaching her will have her speculate on who the phantom was:

:   *"Do you think the ghost is one of... Tiber Septim's dead men?"*

Speaking to her will have her say:

:   *"[Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara") have mercy that gave me a fright."*
:   **I heard screaming.**
:   *"There's a... ghost. Just wandering around my inn like it owned the place."*
:   **You said you saw a ghost?**
:   *"Yes. I've heard stories that Old Hroldan was haunted, but no ones*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *seen a ghost here since the [Great War](/wiki/Lore:Great_War "Lore:Great War"). He's from the battle, I just know it. He's one of Tiber Septim's soldiers... back from the dead."*

Speaking to the ghost will have it call you 'Hjalti' and tell you he is looking for [Hjalti's Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjalti%27s_Sword "Skyrim:Hjalti's Sword"). Returning to Eydis and asking her about Hjalti:

:   **The ghost mentioned a "Hjalti."**
:   *"Hjalti? I've never heard of anyone named Hjalti. Tiber Septim had many names. Maybe that's one of them?"*

:   **The ghost is looking for his sword.**
:   *"A sword? I remember a legend that Tiber Septim had attacked one of the enemy camps before he came to Old Hroldan. It could be there. I'll mark it down on your map."*

After returning to the inn with the sword, and delivering it to the spirit, the ghost will disappear. This will cause Eydis to have further remarks about its sudden departure: *"All of a sudden, the ghost disappeared. What happened to it?"* She will wonder if the shade will return: *"Do you think that ghost is coming back? It seems to have vanished."* She will also claim she was just adjusting to the ghost's presence before it left: *"I was just getting used to that ghost being here, and poof, now he's gone."*

## Conversations

Eydis with her son, Skuli

Eydis will have a couple of conversations with her child, Skuli. One is about Skuli's missing father:

:   **Skuli**: *"Mama, where did papa go?"*
:   **Eydis**: *"He's off fighting the war, dear. For the Stormcloaks."*
:   **Skuli**: *"Last time you said he was fighting for the Empire."*
:   **Eydis**: *"Yes. I'm sure he's doing well there."*

They will also have a brief dialogue in which Eydis questions him about the current status of one of his chores:

:   **Eydis**: *"Did you clean the linens, yet?*
:   **Skuli**: *"I did. Those mead stains are always tricky."*

## Notes

- A [torn note](/wiki/Skyrim:Torn_Note "Skyrim:Torn Note") addressed to an "Eydis" can be found in [Chillwind Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillwind_Depths "Skyrim:Chillwind Depths") by the body of [Firir](/wiki/Skyrim:Firir "Skyrim:Firir"). Bringing it to Eydis has no effect, and Firir appears to have been a caravan guard, not a soldier as Eydis claims her husband is.
- After [The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan") is finished, Eydis will comment on the ghost's disappearance.
- If Eydis is slain, Skuli will inherit the inn and Leontius Salvius will take over as publican.

## Bugs

- Eydis may still behave as though she has seen the ghost even if [The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan") has been completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Despite the "Say Once" flag, Eydis may repeat her initial line about being frightened by the ghost even after the situation has been resolved.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Eydvina Shield-Hearth

## Overview

| Eydvina Shield-Hearth (RefID: FE[xxx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID#Creation_Club "Skyrim:Form ID")C88) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Added by | [Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim "Skyrim:Hendraheim") | | |

| Level | PC×1 (range=6-60) | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | FE[xxx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID#Creation_Club "Skyrim:Form ID")C88 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | FE[xxx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID#Creation_Club "Skyrim:Form ID")C55 |

Eydvina Shield-Hearth

Eydvina armored up

Eydvina Shield-Hearth is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") warrior who owns the ancient hall of [Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)"). She sends you a [warrior's challenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:Warrior's Challenge") for ownership of the house, seeking an honorable death due to actions she took during the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). She can be found sweeping at the stables of the home.

When you speak to her, no matter what option is chosen she will walk over to a nearby tree and pick up a Nordic Sword of Scorching, Scaled Horn Helmet, and Hide Shield and engage combat. She always carries an Iron Sword, lockpick, ring of major stamina, belted tunic, ale, *[Eydvina's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydvina%27s_Note "Skyrim:Eydvina's Note")* and wears Scaled Horn Armor, Boots, and Bracers.

During combat, she uses her Nordic Sword and Hide Shield to fight. You can attack her before she picks up the equipment, leaving her to fight with less armor and a weaker iron sword. Provoking her before speaking to her (such as pickpocketing, stealing, or assaulting her) will cause her to enter combat and fail one of the quest stages. However, no matter what option is taken she will always drop the [Key to Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Hendraheim "Skyrim:Key to Hendraheim") upon death which will allow you to gain ownership of the house and complete the quest.

She will despawn as soon as you enter the house, so be sure to loot anything you think you need from her before going inside.

## Related Quests

- **[Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(quest) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim "Skyrim:Hendraheim"): Earn the deed to an [ancient Nordic hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)").

## Dialogue

When you first see her, she will comment with generic dialogue. When you speak to her:

:   :   **I received your letter.**
    :   *"I understand."*

:   :   **I've come to accept your challenge.**
    :   *"I understand."*

:   :   **Are you the fool who challenged me?**
    :   *"That is so."*

When entering combat:

:   *"Fight, or die well."*

## Bugs

- Her pathfinding after ending dialogue may first cause her to walk to the shovel at the stables before picking up her helmet. **?**
- If she ragdolls, there is a chance her body will become unlootable and cannot even be targeted by spells such as Reanimate Corpse, leaving the key unobtainable. **?**
- If you steal her shield, sword and/or helmet before she can pick them up, there's a chance she will hire a group of thugs to go after you even after her death. **?**

# Skyrim:Factions

## Overview

Almost all [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:People "Skyrim:People") and [creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") in Skyrim belong to one or more **factions** (or **guilds**). These faction memberships control the [combat reaction](#Group_Combat_Reaction) of all NPCs and creatures, both towards you and towards one another. You can be a member of more than one faction at a time.

## Joinable Factions

There are four primary factions that you can join.

- **[Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions")** — A guild of mercenaries, dedicated to combat, based in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). They are similar to the [Fighters Guild](/wiki/Lore:Fighters_Guild "Lore:Fighters Guild") in previous games.
  - *[The Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle")* — The most trusted and accomplished members of the Companions.
- **[College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)")** — A guild dedicated to the study and practice of magic based in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). They are similar to the [Mages Guild](/wiki/Lore:Mages_Guild "Lore:Mages Guild") of previous games.
- **[Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)")** — A secret guild dedicated to professional thievery, based in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
  - *[Nightingales](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales "Skyrim:Nightingales")* — A cabal of the Thieves Guild's top members that serves [Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Nocturnal "Skyrim:Nocturnal") and protects her shrines in Skyrim.
- **[Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood")** — A secret guild made up of professional assassins, the same as from previous games.

You may also take part in the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") by joining one of these two factions.

- **[Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")** — The military power of the empire, they seek to maintain Imperial control of Skyrim from their base in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
- **[Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")** — The main organization of rebels in Skyrim's civil war, they seek Skyrim's independence from the Empire. They are based in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

You can join these factions, although they only have a short quest chain.

- **[Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College")** — A guild of musicians, vocalists and story tellers based in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). They have a single quest to join and a few side quests for members.
- **[Tribunal Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal")** — A [Dark Elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") cult that still worships the old gods of the [Tribunal](/wiki/Lore:Tribunal "Lore:Tribunal"). You can choose to side with them while completing the related quest chain.

Two new factions become available with the [Dawnguard add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").

- **[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)")** — An order of [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") hunters.
- **[Volkihar Vampire Clan](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan")** — A clan of vampires trying to blot out the sun.

## Noteworthy NPC Factions

- **[Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder")** — A group of bandits based out of [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto").
- **[Blackwater Brigands](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackwater_Brigands "Skyrim:Blackwater Brigands")** — A gang of wannabe pirates found at [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear").[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread")
- **[Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades")** — An order of warriors that once served the Emperor before being disbanded and nearly exterminated by the Thalmor.
- **[Blood Horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker")** — A group of pirates based out of [Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly").
- **[Crimson Dirks](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Dirks "Skyrim:Crimson Dirks")** — A former bandit crew from Cyrodiil.[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")
- **[Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist "Skyrim:Cultist")** — Worshippers of the fallen [Dragon Priest](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Priest "Lore:Dragon Priest") [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)"), also known as the First Dragonborn.
- **[Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn")** — [Bretons](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") native to [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") who want to overthrow the region's Nord rulers.
- **[Frostmoon Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf#Frostmoon_Pack "Skyrim:Werewolf")** — A pack of [werewolves](/wiki/Lore:Werewolf "Lore:Werewolf") based at [Frostmoon Crag](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmoon_Crag "Skyrim:Frostmoon Crag").
- **[Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards")** — A monastic order dedicated to studying and preserving the Way of the Voice.
- **[Morag Tong](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong "Skyrim:Morag Tong")** — A professional guild of [assassins](/wiki/Skyrim:Morag_Tong_Assassin "Skyrim:Morag Tong Assassin") lawfully sanctioned in [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind").
- **[Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus")** — An Imperial espionage organization responsible for protecting the Emperor; it rose to prominence after the disbandment of the Blades.
- **[Pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate "Skyrim:Pirate")** — Criminals who prowl the shores of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").
- **[Psijic Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Psijic_Order "Skyrim:Psijic Order")** — An ancient and mysterious monastic order from the Summerset Isles known to practice an arcane form of magic known as Mysticism.
- **[Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand")** — Werewolf hunters that oppose the Companions.
- **[Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village_People "Skyrim:Skaal Village People")** — An offshoot tribe of [Nords](/wiki/Lore:Nord "Lore:Nord") who inhabit [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
- **[Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows")** — A group of thieves based in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") that steal valuables from the corpses of the dead.
- **[Synod](/wiki/Skyrim:Synod "Skyrim:Synod")** — One of two competing mage organizations in [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") which formed when the [Mages Guild](/wiki/Lore:Mages_Guild "Lore:Mages Guild") splintered.
- **[Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor")** — The ruling faction of the [Aldmeri Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion"), it seeks to establish elven supremacy over the race of men.
- **[Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall_People "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall People")** — A group of former Skaal based out of [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").
- **[Vigil of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigil of Stendarr")** — A militant holy order of [Stendarr](/wiki/Lore:Stendarr "Lore:Stendarr") adherents founded after the [Oblivion Crisis](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion_Crisis "Lore:Oblivion Crisis"), its members are dedicated to hunting [Daedra](/wiki/Lore:Daedra "Lore:Daedra").

## Group Combat Reaction

The combat reaction value together with the [aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") and [assistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Assistance "Skyrim:Assistance") values of an NPC determine how members of a faction behave in combat[*verification needed*]. See the [CK Wiki](https://ck.uesp.net/wiki/Faction) for more.

## Complete Factions List

A full list of all (including those not available to you), along with their members and interrelationships, can be found at the pages below:

# Skyrim:Faendal's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Faendal's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Faendal%27s+House)) | | |

Faendal's House

**Faendal's House** is a small home in the southern part of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), located behind [Sven and Hilde's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven_and_Hilde%27s_House "Skyrim:Sven and Hilde's House") and across from [Hod and Gerdur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod_and_Gerdur%27s_House "Skyrim:Hod and Gerdur's House").

It is the home of [Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal"), a local hunter and lumber mill worker. It consists of one zone, *[Faendal's House](#Faendal.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")\* [Trainer (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Common)")[Archery (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Archery (Common)") |

\* Becomes a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") only if the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter") is completed in his favor

## Related Quests

- **[A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter")**: Use a forged letter to resolve a love triangle.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Exterior

| Crops | Other |
| --- | --- |
| 4 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  3 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  4 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 1 [Stone Quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") |

## Faendal's House

Faendal's House, interior

There is only one room to the house and it is crammed with items. Starting to the right and moving counter-clockwise, there is a small dining table with two chairs, followed by a single bed, a non-respawning end table and a non-respawning cupboard, and then the fireplace. Next is a food table with a bench, then a respawning food barrel and an armor table, and finally another non-respawning cupboard. To the right of the bed is a respawning chest and there is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") by the fire, and a small non-respawning chest under the armor table. In addition to the standard stag's head above most fireplaces in Skyrim's homes, Faendal has a deer's head above his small dining table, and a slaughterfish mounted on either side of his bed.

There is a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull") by the bed, a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") by the fire, and on the armor table, a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), two [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), and a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"). There is a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") on the non-respawning cupboard beside this table, behind some books on the shelf with the [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and the [potion of true shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"). On the shelf above that are two [sabre cat pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt"), and four loose iron arrows. The books on the cupboard next to the door include *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*, *[Scourge of the Gray Quarter](/wiki/Skyrim:Scourge_of_the_Gray_Quarter "Skyrim:Scourge of the Gray Quarter")*, *[Pension of the Ancestor Moth](/wiki/Skyrim:Pension_of_the_Ancestor_Moth "Skyrim:Pension of the Ancestor Moth")*, and *[Ode To The Tundrastriders](/wiki/Skyrim:Ode_To_The_Tundrastriders "Skyrim:Ode To The Tundrastriders")*. The end table beside the bed holds a copy of *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")*.

There are a few [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and a good deal of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") about the house. Above the fire is a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), and hanging above the food table and the cupboard by the bed are four portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), three portions of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids. There are four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging above the food table, which is set with two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), two loaves and one piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), one serving each of [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), one serving each of [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), and a varied selection of cheese: [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"). Three more bottles each of wine and alto wine can be found, one of each on the armor table, end table, and small dining table. The small dining table also holds an additional loaf of bread.

## Notes

- The front door has an apprentice-level lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Faendal%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Faendal's House") to which is carried by Faendal. The key can be freely taken from him if he becomes your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").
- After completing the quest [A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter") in Faendal's favor, all low value items become free to take, and the bed becomes usable.
- Directly behind the southwest corner of the house is a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone"), if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.
- A respawning food barrel sits on the east side of the porch, and another respawning food barrel can be found just north of the potato plants in the garden.
- The chest under the armor table is safe storage, but none of the other containers are safe.
