Faendal at the Riverwood mill

Faendal attempts to woo Camilla

**Faendal** is a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerMarksmanJourneyman "Skyrim:TrainerMarksmanJourneyman") living in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). He is the common level [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") for [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"). He is involved in [a love triangle](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter") with [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven") and [Camilla Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Camilla_Valerius "Skyrim:Camilla Valerius"). Should you end the love triangle in his favor, he can become a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), and later be [recruited](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades") to the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"). He may also be recruited as a [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") if the [Hearthfire DLC](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.

He is the local hunter who provides Riverwood's basic needs for meat and pelts; additionally, he works at the local lumber mill, under the watchful eye of his employer [Gerdur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerdur "Skyrim:Gerdur"). His workday starts every morning at 7am and lasts for twelve hours. He will either chop wood, work at the table, or simply relax by looking at the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") while leaning against the fence. Three times a day, at 7am, 11am, and 3pm, he will spend two hours carrying chopped wood to unload near [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor")'s forge. When the clock strikes 7pm, he heads back home and strolls around until 10pm when he takes a late one-hour dinner before going to bed. After only five hours of sleep, he gets out of bed again at 4am and heads up the mountain for a bit of hunting before his workday starts again. The only exception to this routine occurs upon completion of [The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw"), where Faendal will skip the first two hours of his workday and instead visit Camilla Valerius inside the [Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader").

He wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1d9 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Faendal%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Faendal's House") to his house. He wields a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") with twelve [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Related Quests

- **[A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter")**: Use a forged letter to resolve a love triangle.
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").
- **[Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling")**: Become [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah")'s new champion.

## Dialogue

:   *"Did I see you talking to Sven? Maybe not. Maybe...nevermind. But I would stay away from him if I were you."*
:   *"Greetings, sister/brother Elf. Good to see a familiar face so far from home."*
:   *"Riverwood's agreeable enough, I suppose. For a Nord village."*
:   *"There's beauty here unmatched in all of Skyrim, to be sure."*
:   *"Maybe you've already met Camilla Valerius?"*
:   *"If only Camilla shared my affections. Or even knew about them."*
:   *"Are you a hunter, by chance? The hills surrounding the village are ripe*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *with game."*
:   *"I work at the lumber mill, but I escape into the forest whenever possible."*
:   *"I miss [Valenwood](/wiki/Lore:Valenwood "Lore:Valenwood"), but the wilds here are... serviceable."*
:   *"I don't like to brag, but I once took down a bear at three hundred yards. In a blizzard."*

### A Lovely Letter

If you ask him what his problem is with Sven, he will reveal his secret crush on Camilla and his frustrations:

:   **What's your problem with Sven?**
:   *"He's a bard, so he says. Occasionally he finds time to do his job here at the mill. Thinks his ballads and sonnets are going to convince Camilla Valerius to marry him. As if she would say 'yes.' An intelligent, beautiful woman like her wouldn't fall for that nonsense... I hope."*

You can reply in two different ways:

:   **You 'hope'? You don't sound very sure...**
:   *"I've been thinking... maybe Camilla needs a little help seeing Sven for what he is. Could you... could you give her this letter, and say it's from Sven? I think I've matched that Nord's lack of cleverness perfectly."*

:   **You're right. When have words ever inspired feelings of love?**
:   *"I don't need your jokes right now, but maybe you have a point. Maybe Camilla needs some help seeing Sven for what he is. Could you... could you give her this letter, and say it's from Sven? I think I've matched that Nord's lack of cleverness perfectly."*

He will then hand you a [fake letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal%27s_Fake_Letter_from_Sven "Skyrim:Faendal's Fake Letter from Sven") and remind you of your task:

:   *"Tell me as soon as you've given Camilla the letter."*

You can also show it to Sven, who will write another fake letter to make Faendal look racist. You can tell Faendal that Sven wanted you to deliver this letter to Camilla, saying it was from him, and he will be quite surprised:

:   *"What is that blowhard up to now? So, he thinks he can turn Camilla against me? Two can play at this. Here. Give this letter to Camilla and tell her it's from Sven. Let's see what she thinks of him after reading that."*

If you hand Camilla the fake letter from Faendal and lie to her, she will be shocked by how chauvinistic Sven apparently is. When you return to Faendal to tell him that you don't think Camilla will be spending any more time with Sven, he will be happy and hand you a small amount of gold, with his thanks:

:   **I don't think Camilla will be spending any more time with Sven.**
:   *"I appreciate your help. Please, take this. Some gold I've saved up from working at the mill."*

## Notes

- Faendal is the only male Wood Elf [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") in the game.
- When an active follower, Faendal will not attack you when you turn into a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf").
- Because Faendal can become a follower, it is possible to train up to level 50 in Archery with him for no cost. Simply ask him to train you, and then trade items with him to get back the gold you spend on training.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- Faendal's mood is set to disgusted, which is why his facial expression tends to show this.
- Faendal also [appears](/wiki/Castles:Faendal "Castles:Faendal") in [*Castles*](/wiki/Castles:Castles "Castles:Castles").

## Bugs

- Faendal is set to follow [Camilla Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Camilla_Valerius "Skyrim:Camilla Valerius"), so if you marry Camilla, Faendal will sometimes either be found in your house or just outside. This can also lead to him being killed at the hands of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") or [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") if Camilla is picked for radiant quests such as [Rescue](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue "Skyrim:Rescue")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") or [Rescue Mission](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") from the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Faendal may still talk about how he works at the lumber mill in Riverwood if he's hired as a steward for one of the Hearthfire homesteads.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.
- Sometimes Archery skill and level progress will not increase when training with Faendal; however the money will be taken for all five training steps.
- Sometimes the option to train in Archery will not show up after selecting, *"Can you train me to be better at archery?"* when speaking to him.

Fahlbtharz

**Fahlbtharz** is a large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") east of the [Water Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Water_Stone "Skyrim:Water Stone") containing [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"), [albino spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider"), [oil spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Oil Spider (creature)"), and [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"). It contains four zones: *[Fahlbtharz](#Fahlbtharz_.28zone.29)*, *[Fahlbtharz Corridor](#Fahlbtharz_Corridor)*, *[Fahlbtharz Boilery](#Fahlbtharz_Boilery)*, and *[Fahlbtharz Grand Hall](#Fahlbtharz_Grand_Hall)*. A fifth zone, *[Fahlbtharz Forge](#Fahlbtharz_Forge)*, is found if the [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed.

## Related Quests

- **[Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Decide the fate of a [heretical cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple").
- **[Trueflame](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame_(quest) "Skyrim:Trueflame (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Restore power to the Dwarven Forge in Fahlbtharz to restore a [powerful artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame "Skyrim:Trueflame").
- **[The Kagrumez Gauntlet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Kagrumez_Gauntlet "Skyrim:The Kagrumez Gauntlet")**: Survive the [Kagrumez](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez "Skyrim:Kagrumez") trials to claim a unique [prize](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Black_Bow_of_Fate "Skyrim:Dwarven Black Bow of Fate").

### Exterior

You will be ambushed by three rieklings near the entrance, one of which will be mounted on a bristleback. The Dwarven structures are partially destroyed and situated on a slope. There are also a few riekling structures, comprising a [hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Hut "Skyrim:Riekling Hut") and a bridge leading to a Dwemer tower with a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a copy of the rare book *[Nchunak's Fire and Faith](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchunak%27s_Fire_and_Faith "Skyrim:Nchunak's Fire and Faith")* beside it.

### Fahlbtharz

The main chamber

Due to its placement on a hill, the entry hallway is tilted. Go straight ahead and face a couple rieklings inhabiting this area. There is a fire behind some fencing with two pieces of charred skeever meat on top, and in and beside a tent opposite are three books, including a copy of *[Where were you when the Dragon Broke?](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_were_you_when_the_Dragon_Broke "Skyrim:Where were you when the Dragon Broke")*. The hallway to the west then descends to the south and west, passing another tent and two more huts. Proceed south through several broken pipes and piles of rubble until you reach an open door and two dead rieklings pierced with [Dwarven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"). Avoid the two pressure plates that activate the [slicer](/wiki/Skyrim:Slicer "Skyrim:Slicer") trap just before the door, and head inside.

Follow the passage to fight a leveled [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"), then enter a room with a 10-button control panel on the right and a novice-locked door with a Dwarven chest behind it on the left. The buttons, numbered from left to right and top to bottom, trigger the following:

Control panel

| 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Opens/closes the gate on the west side of the room, through which you first enter the room. | Spawns a leveled [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") from its port. (**once**) | Toggles a stationary [spinning blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades"). | Spawns a leveled [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") from its port. (**once**) | Spawns a leveled [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") from its port. (**once**) |
| 6 | 7 | 8 | 9 | 10 |
| Spews flames on the left side of the control panel. | Opens/closes the novice-locked door on the north side of the room. | Toggles a stationary [spinning blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades"). | Opens/closes the gate on the southeast side of the room. | Does nothing (see [bugs](#Bugs)). |

Mushroom garden

To progress, activate the second button from the right in the bottom row (**9**). The gate that has now been opened leads to a hallway with a caved-in room on the left containing an adept-locked chest. With the [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, the caved-in portion with the adept-locked chest will be replaced by a door to *Fahlbtharz Forge*. At the end of the hallway is a room containing a [kinetic resonator](/wiki/Skyrim:Kinetic_Resonator "Skyrim:Kinetic Resonator"), with an expert-locked chest to the left of it (on the wall, not the ground). Hit the resonator to open the nearby gate to the east, and make your way through a web-covered section of the dungeon housing several [oil spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Oil Spider (creature)"), also passing several albino spider eggs and several different fungi. Eventually you will reach a closed gate, which can be opened by hitting the resonator hidden behind the destructible spider web to the left of the gate. Beyond the gate, downstairs, is a room with a mushroom garden containing three [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), two [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), two [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), two [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), and a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungi. You will need to deal with two [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") and a sphere in the two adjacent rooms. The first room through the doorway beside the mushroom farm is a bedroom containing four stone beds around a central table, with an unlocked Dwarven chest near the east wall. Enter the room to the west with a pile of rubble in the center that has broken another table in half, and go through the door at the end of the hall to the left.

You will end up in an expansive chamber full of tall pillars, bearing platforms and walkways at their higher levels, and many giant spinning gears on the lower levels shortly above a large pool of water. Three [Dwarven ballistae](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwarven Ballista") will be guarding the higher levels. Jump down onto one of the spinning gears from under the small Dwemer tower to your right. Navigate southwest over the gears, some of which hide Dwarven spiders, and you will find the entrance to *[Fahlbtharz Corridor](#Fahlbtharz_Corridor)*.

### Fahlbtharz Forge

Fahlbtharz Forge

Fahlbtharz Forge is a small room, as you enter, you will hear a ghost is saying *"Ah"* when killed by [Hand Kenro Hlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro_Hlan "Skyrim:Hand Kenro Hlan"), if you're on the quest [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)"), you need kill Hand Kenro Hlan and progress the quest. There's a forge with 4 [Fahlbtharz Forge Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_Items#Fahlbtharz_Forge_Gem "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal Items") sockets, it's quest related.

### Fahlbtharz Corridor

Fahlbtharz Corridor

There are two pressure plates near the entrance that trigger a [ballista](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwemer Ballista"). On the way upstairs, there is a pressure plate connected to a [slicer](/wiki/Skyrim:Slicer "Skyrim:Slicer") trap. A single [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") will be spawned if you activate any of these three pressure plates. Upstairs to the left is an adept-locked gate, behind which are various Dwemer items including seven pieces of smeltable scrap metal and a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dwarven War Axe"), and a chest. To the right is a door leading to a higher level of the main chamber, back to the zone *[Fahlbtharz](#Fahlbtharz)*.

Back in the main zone, turn left and go upstairs, and you will find yourself in a small alcove with a valve and a lever. The valve lowers the bridge in front of you leading to the water level of the chamber. Pulling the lever will rotate the nearby tower and extend a bridge to it. Cross the bridge and proceed straight ahead as far you can, then jump down onto the spinning gears. One of the gears has two large coin purses and a random enchanted shield in the center. Cross the gears and jump onto the platform ahead. Go upstairs, where you will find the corpse of [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Eydis (Dragonborn)"), an explorer presumably killed by Dwarven automatons. You can loot her body for a set of [Skaal armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Coat "Skyrim:Skaal Coat") (excluding the [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Hat "Skyrim:Skaal Hat")) and [her journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eydis's Journal"). There is a door on the left leading to *[Fahlbtharz Boilery](#Fahlbtharz_Boilery)*, and a valve ahead which lowers two ramps down to the water level of the chamber.

### Fahlbtharz Boilery

Fahlbtharz Boilery

As you enter, you will notice there is an inaccessible gate to your right and a [kinetic resonator](/wiki/Skyrim:Kinetic_Resonator "Skyrim:Kinetic Resonator") behind it. Past the gate, fight a [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") on your way downstairs to find yourself in a long room full of vent pipes and gears. There will be a shelf ahead with a [Dwarven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Bow "Skyrim:Dwarven Bow") and four quivers, each containing 12 [Dwarven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"). A single [Dwarven ballista](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwarven Ballista") stands guard at the end of the room.

Intact boiler

Overcharged boiler

Your progress will be blocked by a closed gate controlled by a steam-powered Dwarven mechanism. Get on the platform above, either by riding the two pistons up at this end, or by walking to the far end and climbing the stairs. There is a small alcove underneath the upper platform containing a table and chairs along with four unlocked Dwarven chests. In the center of the upper platform above the alcove lies the corpse of another unlucky explorer, [Ulyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulyn "Skyrim:Ulyn"), which can be looted for [his journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulyn%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ulyn's Journal") providing a few hints on how to solve the puzzle. Nearby rests a leveled enchanted bow and a quiver of 25 random arrows of up to ebony quality. You will also see a boiler consisting of a large Dwemer gear with twenty steam meters around it, and six resonators: three to the left, and three to the right. Each resonator represents a value (see [puzzle values](#Puzzle_Values)), which equals the number of steam meters that will be powered when that resonator is hit, or the number that will be reset when the resonator is hit again. Steam meters are powered progressively and clockwise, whereby each steam meter glows blue when powered, and orange when overpowered.

#### Puzzle Values

- Values of #1 and #6 are hinted in [Ulyn's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulyn%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ulyn's Journal").

| Resonator | #1 | #2 | #3 | #4 | #5 | #6 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Value | **3** | **4** | 6 | 9 | **13** | 18 |

The puzzle is solved when all twenty steam meters are powered, and none are overpowered. This can be achieved by shooting resonators #1, #2, and #5, numbered 1-6 from left to right as you face them. However, if the resonators are hit incorrectly, the boiler will be overcharged, venting out steam and spawning hostile Dwarven automatons. Failing more than twice will result in three moving [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") being activated instead.

Go upstairs through the gate that has been opened, and you will find the resonator that opens the previously inaccessible nearby gate. Destroy the nearby spider, then open the door straight ahead leading to a higher level of the main chamber, back to the zone *[Fahlbtharz](#Fahlbtharz)*.

Back in the main zone, an essential lever that is easily overlooked will be on a wall directly to the right. The walkways will then align in a way which, after some further gear-navigating and resonator manipulation, will lead to *[Fahlbtharz Grand Hall](#Fahlbtharz_Grand_Hall)*. A lootable skeleton with a random enchanted bow and a quiver containing 15 arrows of leveled quality nearby can be found in the tower with the resonator. The opposite tower holds a large Dwarven chest. To the left of the entrance to the Grand Hall, on top of a nearby tall rock formation below, is a lootable skeleton holding a small expert-locked Dwarven chest, as well as an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") with three lockpicks next to it.

### Fahlbtharz Grand Hall

Fahlbtharz Grand Hall

Treasure room

You will find that the entire hall is covered with spider webs, so prepare to fight several [albino](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider") and [oil spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Oil Spider (creature)"). Two [Dwarven Centurion Guardians](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") can be found sleeping in the corners ahead, but will not awaken unless attacked or otherwise interacted with. As you move away from the entrance, two [Dwarven ballistae](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwarven Ballista") will ambush you from above.

Within the hall is a round platform with three Dynamo Actuators that must be filled by [centurion dynamo cores](/wiki/Skyrim:Centurion_Dynamo_Core "Skyrim:Centurion Dynamo Core"), dropped by the centurions nearby, to progress. Fortunately, the middle actuator is already filled. The actuators, from left to right as you face them, trigger the final gate, the staircase to it, and the bars before the gate, respectively.

After filling the Dynamo Actuators, you will be able to access the treasure room, which contains five [piles of gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold#Pile_of_Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a treasure chest, a leveled battleaxe up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") quality, a single [Kagrumez resonance gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez_Resonance_Gem "Skyrim:Kagrumez Resonance Gem"), and the unique Dwarven helmet [Visage of Mzund](/wiki/Skyrim:Visage_of_Mzund "Skyrim:Visage of Mzund"). Activate the lever on the left to lift yourself back to surface, directly north of the [Abandoned Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Lodge "Skyrim:Abandoned Lodge"). This means leaving three valuable centurion dynamo cores behind; the alternative is to take them and make the long trek back to the surface the way you came.

Fahlbtharz lift

## Notes

- Moving across the spinning gears and into the nearby towers can be frustrating. A carefully targeted Whirlwind Sprint can sometimes get you where you want to go; save the game before trying.
- It is possible to get into the treasure room and retain two dynamo cores by removing the center one that controls the stairs, then placing it in the activator that opens the swinging gates. Once you have that set, jump onto the right activator that controls the bars, place a core into it, then remove it and quickly use Whirlwind Sprint as you line your sight with the opening to the control room. It is very tight timing, but it can be done. Note: Your follower will catch up to you when you leave the room.
- It is possible to loot some items from the treasure room without any extra dynamo cores by using [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") to pull items through the bars.

- It is possible to completely bypass the boiler room puzzle by standing right up against the gate near the entrance and casting spells/powers (see "Working Methods" below) or shouting through it, thus hitting the resonator.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Working Methods  - **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic**   - Most shock spells   - Rune spells (indirectly)   - [Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Blizzard "Skyrim:Blizzard")   - [Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Fire Storm") - **[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") magic**   - [Circle of Protection](/wiki/Skyrim:Circle_of_Protection "Skyrim:Circle of Protection") - **[Powers](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers "Skyrim:Powers")**   - [Battle Cry](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_Cry "Skyrim:Battle Cry")   - [North Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Wind "Skyrim:North Wind") - **[Shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Shouts "Skyrim:Shouts")**   - [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force")  |  | | --- | |  | |

- If you want the treasure from the final room (including the Visage and the resonance gem) but don't want to bother with the puzzles of the entire ruin, you can use a wooden plate or platter to glitch through the locked gate of the Fahlbtharz Lift, use the lift to go down, and then claim the treasure. Note that you can't "backtrack" to the entrance this way, as the door leading to it is barred by the puzzle.

## Bugs

- The button at the bottom right corner of the control panel was intended to activate the flamethrower on the right side of the panel, but doesn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- There are some Dwarven chests that are double placed, and thus lootable twice.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you sneak attack the centurions in the Grand Hall before they activate, you may not be able to loot their corpses, and will either need to have brought two centurion dynamo cores with you to progress, or exit Fahlbtharz before clearing it.
- If you carry no Centurion dynamo cores and keep interacting with an empty actuator, one will eventually be added to your inventory. That way you may fill all the actuators, despite starting with zero cores.
- Sometimes you'll have to *remove* the right dynamo core after adding it in order to clear the bars.
- When you enter the Grand Hall, there is a map glitch where albino/oil spiders and any items will fall through. **?**
- The body of Eydis can disappear. Attempts to use `player.moveto` will just move you to where the body should have been. **?**
- The Dwarven Ballista in the Boilery is sometimes not hostile **?**

## Maps

Fahlbtharz

**Fahlbtharz** is a large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") east of the [Water Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Water_Stone "Skyrim:Water Stone") containing [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"), [albino spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider"), [oil spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Oil Spider (creature)"), and [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"). It contains four zones: *[Fahlbtharz](#Fahlbtharz_.28zone.29)*, *[Fahlbtharz Corridor](#Fahlbtharz_Corridor)*, *[Fahlbtharz Boilery](#Fahlbtharz_Boilery)*, and *[Fahlbtharz Grand Hall](#Fahlbtharz_Grand_Hall)*. A fifth zone, *[Fahlbtharz Forge](#Fahlbtharz_Forge)*, is found if the [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed.

## Related Quests

- **[Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Decide the fate of a [heretical cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple").
- **[Trueflame](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame_(quest) "Skyrim:Trueflame (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Restore power to the Dwarven Forge in Fahlbtharz to restore a [powerful artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame "Skyrim:Trueflame").
- **[The Kagrumez Gauntlet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Kagrumez_Gauntlet "Skyrim:The Kagrumez Gauntlet")**: Survive the [Kagrumez](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez "Skyrim:Kagrumez") trials to claim a unique [prize](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Black_Bow_of_Fate "Skyrim:Dwarven Black Bow of Fate").

### Exterior

You will be ambushed by three rieklings near the entrance, one of which will be mounted on a bristleback. The Dwarven structures are partially destroyed and situated on a slope. There are also a few riekling structures, comprising a [hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Hut "Skyrim:Riekling Hut") and a bridge leading to a Dwemer tower with a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a copy of the rare book *[Nchunak's Fire and Faith](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchunak%27s_Fire_and_Faith "Skyrim:Nchunak's Fire and Faith")* beside it.

### Fahlbtharz

The main chamber

Due to its placement on a hill, the entry hallway is tilted. Go straight ahead and face a couple rieklings inhabiting this area. There is a fire behind some fencing with two pieces of charred skeever meat on top, and in and beside a tent opposite are three books, including a copy of *[Where were you when the Dragon Broke?](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_were_you_when_the_Dragon_Broke "Skyrim:Where were you when the Dragon Broke")*. The hallway to the west then descends to the south and west, passing another tent and two more huts. Proceed south through several broken pipes and piles of rubble until you reach an open door and two dead rieklings pierced with [Dwarven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"). Avoid the two pressure plates that activate the [slicer](/wiki/Skyrim:Slicer "Skyrim:Slicer") trap just before the door, and head inside.

Follow the passage to fight a leveled [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"), then enter a room with a 10-button control panel on the right and a novice-locked door with a Dwarven chest behind it on the left. The buttons, numbered from left to right and top to bottom, trigger the following:

Control panel

| 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Opens/closes the gate on the west side of the room, through which you first enter the room. | Spawns a leveled [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") from its port. (**once**) | Toggles a stationary [spinning blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades"). | Spawns a leveled [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") from its port. (**once**) | Spawns a leveled [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") from its port. (**once**) |
| 6 | 7 | 8 | 9 | 10 |
| Spews flames on the left side of the control panel. | Opens/closes the novice-locked door on the north side of the room. | Toggles a stationary [spinning blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades"). | Opens/closes the gate on the southeast side of the room. | Does nothing (see [bugs](#Bugs)). |

Mushroom garden

To progress, activate the second button from the right in the bottom row (**9**). The gate that has now been opened leads to a hallway with a caved-in room on the left containing an adept-locked chest. With the [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, the caved-in portion with the adept-locked chest will be replaced by a door to *Fahlbtharz Forge*. At the end of the hallway is a room containing a [kinetic resonator](/wiki/Skyrim:Kinetic_Resonator "Skyrim:Kinetic Resonator"), with an expert-locked chest to the left of it (on the wall, not the ground). Hit the resonator to open the nearby gate to the east, and make your way through a web-covered section of the dungeon housing several [oil spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Oil Spider (creature)"), also passing several albino spider eggs and several different fungi. Eventually you will reach a closed gate, which can be opened by hitting the resonator hidden behind the destructible spider web to the left of the gate. Beyond the gate, downstairs, is a room with a mushroom garden containing three [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), two [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), two [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), two [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), and a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungi. You will need to deal with two [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") and a sphere in the two adjacent rooms. The first room through the doorway beside the mushroom farm is a bedroom containing four stone beds around a central table, with an unlocked Dwarven chest near the east wall. Enter the room to the west with a pile of rubble in the center that has broken another table in half, and go through the door at the end of the hall to the left.

You will end up in an expansive chamber full of tall pillars, bearing platforms and walkways at their higher levels, and many giant spinning gears on the lower levels shortly above a large pool of water. Three [Dwarven ballistae](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwarven Ballista") will be guarding the higher levels. Jump down onto one of the spinning gears from under the small Dwemer tower to your right. Navigate southwest over the gears, some of which hide Dwarven spiders, and you will find the entrance to *[Fahlbtharz Corridor](#Fahlbtharz_Corridor)*.

### Fahlbtharz Forge

Fahlbtharz Forge

Fahlbtharz Forge is a small room, as you enter, you will hear a ghost is saying *"Ah"* when killed by [Hand Kenro Hlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro_Hlan "Skyrim:Hand Kenro Hlan"), if you're on the quest [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)"), you need kill Hand Kenro Hlan and progress the quest. There's a forge with 4 [Fahlbtharz Forge Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_Items#Fahlbtharz_Forge_Gem "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal Items") sockets, it's quest related.

### Fahlbtharz Corridor

Fahlbtharz Corridor

There are two pressure plates near the entrance that trigger a [ballista](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwemer Ballista"). On the way upstairs, there is a pressure plate connected to a [slicer](/wiki/Skyrim:Slicer "Skyrim:Slicer") trap. A single [Dwarven sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") will be spawned if you activate any of these three pressure plates. Upstairs to the left is an adept-locked gate, behind which are various Dwemer items including seven pieces of smeltable scrap metal and a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dwarven War Axe"), and a chest. To the right is a door leading to a higher level of the main chamber, back to the zone *[Fahlbtharz](#Fahlbtharz)*.

Back in the main zone, turn left and go upstairs, and you will find yourself in a small alcove with a valve and a lever. The valve lowers the bridge in front of you leading to the water level of the chamber. Pulling the lever will rotate the nearby tower and extend a bridge to it. Cross the bridge and proceed straight ahead as far you can, then jump down onto the spinning gears. One of the gears has two large coin purses and a random enchanted shield in the center. Cross the gears and jump onto the platform ahead. Go upstairs, where you will find the corpse of [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Eydis (Dragonborn)"), an explorer presumably killed by Dwarven automatons. You can loot her body for a set of [Skaal armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Coat "Skyrim:Skaal Coat") (excluding the [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Hat "Skyrim:Skaal Hat")) and [her journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eydis's Journal"). There is a door on the left leading to *[Fahlbtharz Boilery](#Fahlbtharz_Boilery)*, and a valve ahead which lowers two ramps down to the water level of the chamber.

### Fahlbtharz Boilery

Fahlbtharz Boilery

As you enter, you will notice there is an inaccessible gate to your right and a [kinetic resonator](/wiki/Skyrim:Kinetic_Resonator "Skyrim:Kinetic Resonator") behind it. Past the gate, fight a [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") on your way downstairs to find yourself in a long room full of vent pipes and gears. There will be a shelf ahead with a [Dwarven bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Bow "Skyrim:Dwarven Bow") and four quivers, each containing 12 [Dwarven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"). A single [Dwarven ballista](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwarven Ballista") stands guard at the end of the room.

Intact boiler

Overcharged boiler

Your progress will be blocked by a closed gate controlled by a steam-powered Dwarven mechanism. Get on the platform above, either by riding the two pistons up at this end, or by walking to the far end and climbing the stairs. There is a small alcove underneath the upper platform containing a table and chairs along with four unlocked Dwarven chests. In the center of the upper platform above the alcove lies the corpse of another unlucky explorer, [Ulyn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulyn "Skyrim:Ulyn"), which can be looted for [his journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulyn%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ulyn's Journal") providing a few hints on how to solve the puzzle. Nearby rests a leveled enchanted bow and a quiver of 25 random arrows of up to ebony quality. You will also see a boiler consisting of a large Dwemer gear with twenty steam meters around it, and six resonators: three to the left, and three to the right. Each resonator represents a value (see [puzzle values](#Puzzle_Values)), which equals the number of steam meters that will be powered when that resonator is hit, or the number that will be reset when the resonator is hit again. Steam meters are powered progressively and clockwise, whereby each steam meter glows blue when powered, and orange when overpowered.

#### Puzzle Values

- Values of #1 and #6 are hinted in [Ulyn's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulyn%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ulyn's Journal").

| Resonator | #1 | #2 | #3 | #4 | #5 | #6 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Value | **3** | **4** | 6 | 9 | **13** | 18 |

The puzzle is solved when all twenty steam meters are powered, and none are overpowered. This can be achieved by shooting resonators #1, #2, and #5, numbered 1-6 from left to right as you face them. However, if the resonators are hit incorrectly, the boiler will be overcharged, venting out steam and spawning hostile Dwarven automatons. Failing more than twice will result in three moving [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") being activated instead.

Go upstairs through the gate that has been opened, and you will find the resonator that opens the previously inaccessible nearby gate. Destroy the nearby spider, then open the door straight ahead leading to a higher level of the main chamber, back to the zone *[Fahlbtharz](#Fahlbtharz)*.

Back in the main zone, an essential lever that is easily overlooked will be on a wall directly to the right. The walkways will then align in a way which, after some further gear-navigating and resonator manipulation, will lead to *[Fahlbtharz Grand Hall](#Fahlbtharz_Grand_Hall)*. A lootable skeleton with a random enchanted bow and a quiver containing 15 arrows of leveled quality nearby can be found in the tower with the resonator. The opposite tower holds a large Dwarven chest. To the left of the entrance to the Grand Hall, on top of a nearby tall rock formation below, is a lootable skeleton holding a small expert-locked Dwarven chest, as well as an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") with three lockpicks next to it.

### Fahlbtharz Grand Hall

Fahlbtharz Grand Hall

Treasure room

You will find that the entire hall is covered with spider webs, so prepare to fight several [albino](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider") and [oil spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Oil Spider (creature)"). Two [Dwarven Centurion Guardians](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") can be found sleeping in the corners ahead, but will not awaken unless attacked or otherwise interacted with. As you move away from the entrance, two [Dwarven ballistae](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ballista "Skyrim:Dwarven Ballista") will ambush you from above.

Within the hall is a round platform with three Dynamo Actuators that must be filled by [centurion dynamo cores](/wiki/Skyrim:Centurion_Dynamo_Core "Skyrim:Centurion Dynamo Core"), dropped by the centurions nearby, to progress. Fortunately, the middle actuator is already filled. The actuators, from left to right as you face them, trigger the final gate, the staircase to it, and the bars before the gate, respectively.

After filling the Dynamo Actuators, you will be able to access the treasure room, which contains five [piles of gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold#Pile_of_Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a treasure chest, a leveled battleaxe up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") quality, a single [Kagrumez resonance gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez_Resonance_Gem "Skyrim:Kagrumez Resonance Gem"), and the unique Dwarven helmet [Visage of Mzund](/wiki/Skyrim:Visage_of_Mzund "Skyrim:Visage of Mzund"). Activate the lever on the left to lift yourself back to surface, directly north of the [Abandoned Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Lodge "Skyrim:Abandoned Lodge"). This means leaving three valuable centurion dynamo cores behind; the alternative is to take them and make the long trek back to the surface the way you came.

Fahlbtharz lift

## Notes

- Moving across the spinning gears and into the nearby towers can be frustrating. A carefully targeted Whirlwind Sprint can sometimes get you where you want to go; save the game before trying.
- It is possible to get into the treasure room and retain two dynamo cores by removing the center one that controls the stairs, then placing it in the activator that opens the swinging gates. Once you have that set, jump onto the right activator that controls the bars, place a core into it, then remove it and quickly use Whirlwind Sprint as you line your sight with the opening to the control room. It is very tight timing, but it can be done. Note: Your follower will catch up to you when you leave the room.
- It is possible to loot some items from the treasure room without any extra dynamo cores by using [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") to pull items through the bars.

- It is possible to completely bypass the boiler room puzzle by standing right up against the gate near the entrance and casting spells/powers (see "Working Methods" below) or shouting through it, thus hitting the resonator.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Working Methods  - **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic**   - Most shock spells   - Rune spells (indirectly)   - [Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Blizzard "Skyrim:Blizzard")   - [Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Fire Storm") - **[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") magic**   - [Circle of Protection](/wiki/Skyrim:Circle_of_Protection "Skyrim:Circle of Protection") - **[Powers](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers "Skyrim:Powers")**   - [Battle Cry](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_Cry "Skyrim:Battle Cry")   - [North Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Wind "Skyrim:North Wind") - **[Shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Shouts "Skyrim:Shouts")**   - [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force")  |  | | --- | |  | |

- If you want the treasure from the final room (including the Visage and the resonance gem) but don't want to bother with the puzzles of the entire ruin, you can use a wooden plate or platter to glitch through the locked gate of the Fahlbtharz Lift, use the lift to go down, and then claim the treasure. Note that you can't "backtrack" to the entrance this way, as the door leading to it is barred by the puzzle.

## Bugs

- The button at the bottom right corner of the control panel was intended to activate the flamethrower on the right side of the panel, but doesn't.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- There are some Dwarven chests that are double placed, and thus lootable twice.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you sneak attack the centurions in the Grand Hall before they activate, you may not be able to loot their corpses, and will either need to have brought two centurion dynamo cores with you to progress, or exit Fahlbtharz before clearing it.
- If you carry no Centurion dynamo cores and keep interacting with an empty actuator, one will eventually be added to your inventory. That way you may fill all the actuators, despite starting with zero cores.
- Sometimes you'll have to *remove* the right dynamo core after adding it in order to clear the bars.
- When you enter the Grand Hall, there is a map glitch where albino/oil spiders and any items will fall through. **?**
- The body of Eydis can disappear. Attempts to use `player.moveto` will just move you to where the body should have been. **?**
- The Dwarven Ballista in the Boilery is sometimes not hostile **?**

## Maps

- 

  Fahlbtharz
- 

  Fahlbtharz Corridor
- 

  Fahlbtharz Boilery
- 

  Fahlbtharz Grand Hall

# Skyrim:Faida

## Overview

| Faida (RefID: 00019A29) | | | |

Faida at work in the tavern

**Faida** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [food vendor](/wiki/Skyrim:Food_Vendor "Skyrim:Food Vendor") and the innkeeper of the [Four Shields Tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Shields_Tavern "Skyrim:Four Shields Tavern") in the small village of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). She stays behind the inn's counter all day. During the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)"), she will direct you towards the [Imperial Courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Courier "Skyrim:Imperial Courier").

Faida wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") along with some [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloves#000261c1 "Skyrim:Gloves") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries some [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)")**: Find and deliver some forged documents to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").

## Quest-Related Events

At the start of Breaching Security, you will find Faida outside the [Penitus Oculatus Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Outpost "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Outpost") alongside her lover [Gaius Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") and his [father](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro"). Before starting his security inspections, Gaius shares a heartfelt goodbye with his father, and will then have a short moment with Faida:

:   **Faida**: *"Well, this is it, then. Look after yourself, Gaius. You're doing your duty, and I'm proud of you. But you'd better come back to me. You hear?"*
:   **Gaius**: *"Oh, Faida. I may travel alone, but you know I carry you always in my heart. I'll see you soon."*

After this, Gaius departs and Faida will head back to work at the inn.

## Dialogue

Faida can greet you by saying:

:   *"Faida's the name. I keep the inn."*
:   *"Something different about you, I can tell. Hope you ain't here to cause trouble."*
:   *"The meals I serve ain't what I'd call a Jarl's feast, but they'll fill your belly."*
:   *"Seen a lot of travelers lately. Mostly soldier*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, nowadays."*
:   *"You met the [Lylvieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family%27s_House "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House")? Quiet family, but they're the heart of Dragon Bridge."*
:   *"Poor [Horgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir "Skyrim:Horgeir"). Everyone in town knows about his [wife](/wiki/Skyrim:Olda "Skyrim:Olda")'s [affair](/wiki/Skyrim:Lodvar "Skyrim:Lodvar") but him. Probably better if he doesn't know."* (As long as no member of [Horgeir's family](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Horgeir's House") is around)
:   *"I think the dragons are here to test us, and make sure we're still true Nords."*
:   *"I was a barmaid at the [Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever") when I met my husband, rest his soul. Wasn't for him, I'd still be working there!"*

:   **Where can I learn more about magic?**
:   *"Nords don't care much for magic. The [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") is about the only place it's not looked down on. Otherwise you could talk to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair")'s [pet wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") in Solitude."*

## Conversations

[Julienne Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve") is currently learning about the innkeeper trade from Faida. They can be found having the following conversations:

:   **Julienne**: *"Miss Faida, may I ask you a question?"*
:   **Faida**: *"Of course, Julienne. What's on your mind?"*
:   **Julienne**: *"What do you do when a customer can't afford to pay for a meal or a drink?"*
:   **Faida**: *"Since my customers are mostly local, I just knock on their front doors the next day."*

:   **Faida**: *"Mind you don't forget to sweep up, Julienne. The floor's looking a bit dusty."*
:   **Julienne**: *"I won't forget. I'll do it after I get the dishes cleaned."*
:   **Faida**: *"You've been working hard lately. You'll make a fine innkeeper someday."*
:   **Julienne**: *"If the [Nine](/wiki/Lore:Nine_Divines "Lore:Nine Divines") are willing!"*

## Rumors

Back in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Minette Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Minette_Vinius "Skyrim:Minette Vinius") may mention her in response to her father saying that running a bar isn't a lady's job:

:   *"What about 'Auntie Faida' in Dragon Bridge? She runs a bar, and you said she's one of your favorite girls!"*

## Notes

- According to relationship data as seen in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), she's the cousin of [Corpulus Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpulus_Vinius "Skyrim:Corpulus Vinius"). Minette Vinius also refers to this fact in a scene.
- It seems that Faida was once meant to be a part of a love triangle with Julienne and removed Dragon Bridge resident, [Tasius Tragus](/wiki/Skyrim:Tasius_Tragus "Skyrim:Tasius Tragus"). Tasius and Faida are marked as lovers in the Creation Kit, with Julienne being marked as a secret lover.
  - Tasius' role was seemingly given to a man named Voltus Agallon, who in turn got replaced by both [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") and [Gaius Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro"). Like Tasius, Gaius is also shown to be in a relationship with Faida, although they aren't marked as such in the files.

## Bugs

- [Julienne Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve") was meant to be Faida's backup for the Four Shields Tavern, but isn't because there is no backup alias.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Falas Selvayn

## Overview

Falas Selvayn

**Falas Selvayn** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") trader who can be found at the [Ramshackle Trading Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramshackle_Trading_Post "Skyrim:Ramshackle Trading Post") between the hours of midnight and 5am.

He wears [ebony armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Armor "Skyrim:Ebony Armor") with [steel plate boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Plate Boots"), [steel plate gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Plate Gauntlets"), and a [Pale guard's helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Guard%27s_Helmet "Skyrim:Pale Guard's Helmet").

He also carries the unique bow [Glass Bow of the Stag Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow_of_the_Stag_Prince "Skyrim:Glass Bow of the Stag Prince"). It cannot be bought from him, nor obtained by killing him as he is [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") but it can be pickpocketed from him if you have the [Misdirection](/wiki/Skyrim:Misdirection "Skyrim:Misdirection") perk. If you lack the Misdirection perk, an alternative is reverse-pickpocketing a dagger (or other melee weapon) into his inventory, then getting him to equip it in combat (attacking and drawing the nearby spriggan towards him works, or simply attack him and then use the Bend Will shout on him). This will allow you to pickpocket the bow without the perk as well as to buy it from him, as his bow would no longer be equipped.

## Dialogue

:   **Who are you?**
:   *"Who am I? Who are you? Buy something or keep moving."*

:   **Where do you get your goods?**
:   *"Sometimes things fall off the back of a cart. I find them, clean them up and resell them."*

:   **What have you got for sale?**

## Notes

- He will not appear if you arrive at, or even near, the trading post before midnight. You must enter the area between midnight and 5am, or else he will not spawn. If you're having trouble, go to Raven Rock, wait until midnight, then walk from there. If he still does not appear, you can fix this on PC by using the console and typing `prid [RefId]` followed by `enable` in the console. (For more details on what constitutes "near", see the [OnCellAttach talk page](https://ck.uesp.net/wiki/Talk:OnCellAttach_-_ObjectReference "ckwiki:Talk:OnCellAttach - ObjectReference") on the Creation Kit wiki.)
- Falas shares the last name with [Fadase Selvayn](/wiki/Morrowind:Fadase_Selvayn "Morrowind:Fadase Selvayn").
