Faldar's Tooth

**Faldar's Tooth** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). It contains only one zone, *[Faldar's Tooth](#Faldar.27s_Tooth)*.

The bandits force the wolves to fight in a central pit for the entertainment of Nords who come to watch and bet on the outcome of the fights.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval")**: Journey to a random location to retrieve a fragment of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst_(quest) "Skyrim:Bloodthirst (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Find a cursed blood-drinking sword.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Faldar's Tooth

As soon as you approach this fort, even if you haven't been detected, you can hear one of the bandits say *"Give them the dogs boys!"* At this point the outer wooden gate slowly descends, releasing two pit wolves. There are five bandits on guard around the walls of the fort, including one standing outside the fort wall on the northwest side of the tallest tower. The others can generally be found as follows: one on the east wall, one on the middle level near some tents, and the final two on the higher level—one inside and one outside of a large tent. The walls of the fort are crumbling and have been shored up and patched with wooden palisades and platforms in places. The corner tower to the southwest has collapsed and there is a point between this and a wooden platform where, with careful climbing and jumping, it is possible to enter the fort's exterior without having to pass through one of the two entrances. The two entrances are to the east and south, with the former being past the two wolves that are released, and the other through an adept-locked gate. They both lead into small courtyards and give access to the main part of the fort's interior. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found on the dock to the south. Fish from [Temperate Lakes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") can be caught here.

Guard wolves

The entrance to the east past the wolves leads to a separate courtyard with two doors to the interior; however, one of these is blocked by rubble. Beyond the locked gate to the south, the courtyard contains a wooden door leading to the interior on your right and an empty gated area, where the gate can not be interacted with, against the south wall to the left of the gate. The adept-locked front gate can be opened using a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth_Key "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth Key") found in a tent on a higher level of the exterior. Opposite the empty gated area is a flight of stone stairs leading up to the middle level of the exterior, which contains three small tents—one against the north wall, one near the stairs, and the third near the west wall. All have bedrolls in them, and the third has a campfire in front of it. To the south there are a ramp and bridge leading up to a platform. From there, across another bridge to the highest level, there is a large tent near a lit campfire and the tallest tower; inside is a bedroll and table. On the table are eight loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and the key to the southern entrance gate and tower to the east, while under the table is an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest").

#### Entry Tower

The interior is arranged in a circuit. Only the western entrance allows you to choose to travel in either direction around the interior, due to a wooden gate with only a chain on that side. The interior of the fort seems to have suffered a lot of damage over the years and contains a lot of [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") throughout and several [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus growing in the damp environment.

Bandit working

Beyond this door is a narrow corridor with a level-locked cage on the right, which contains a bedroll. After a couple of turns the corridor opens into a small room with a couple of small cages that are normally found hanging and a couple of torture racks, with a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") on your right.

#### Forge

There is a doorway opposite that leads out to the top of a curved staircase with a [falling boulder trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") and a lever to activate it to the left. Partway down the stairs there is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that will also trigger this trap. At the bottom of the curved stairs there is a wooden door on the west wall and a wooden gate with a chain to the right that lowers it. Behind the door a flight of narrow stairs leads up. At the top there are many thick roots coming through from above in front of you. Off to the left is a bandit using a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") or [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). The forge is in the southern corner with the grindstone to the right. Against the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding seven pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore"), and a novice-locked chest. Behind the grindstone is a second set of shelves holding a quiver of [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), with a workbench and sideboard that have been crushed by falling masonry and an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") on the ground to the right of this. To the east around a central pillar is the path onward and a small campfire at the top of a flight of stairs that descend to the northwest.

At the bottom is a shallowly flooded room with a wooden slatted path and several [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"). There is a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in this room that may be already dead from being caught in a trap. The doorway out of this room is to the southwest and is trapped with a tripwire that triggers a [skull ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull_Ram "Skyrim:Skull Ram"). It comes from northwest and travels across the front of the doorway inside the room, so passing in this direction it is safe to trigger it.

Beyond the doorway are two patches of fly amanita fungus next to a caved-in section on the left. To the right there is a bandit archer near three stalls separated by stone walls, each area having a stool and bucket. On the separating walls are three common books, a [potion of the warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Warrior "Skyrim:Potion of the Warrior"), and a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"). Opposite to the south-southwest is a set of shelves holding three minor [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions")—one of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), one of [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and one of [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka")—along with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). On a second set of shelves to the right are a couple more common books, a bottle of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"), and a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"). The corridor continues around the corner to the northeast and passes an open door to an alcove containing a set of shelves that hold twenty-one bottles of Nord mead, a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a potion of minor healing, and a potion of minor magicka. Opposite, attached to the southeast wall, there is a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall"); the [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers it is in the center of the corridor, just past the alcove door. It is simple to see and avoid.

Bandits drinking

Beyond the pressure plate is a doorway into an L-shaped room with a closed wooden door opposite, and a doorway on the left and a couple of sets of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling in the middle of the room. Around the corner, to the left is the rest of the room with two bandits sitting at a table with four chairs. On the table is a large amount of loose coins with a few more under the table. Above this table is an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging from the ceiling. Behind this table are two sets of shelves holding a random healing potion and a random magicka potion. There is a small wooden table immediately to the left of the closed door holding a mead barrel and a long wooden table against the south wall holding a random enchanted [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), and a random stamina potion. Any fighting in the first room will alert two more bandits from the room beyond the door to join in the fight.

#### Kitchen and Dormitory

The room through the doorway on the left is small and has a large pile of firewood and a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") against the southwest wall. Opposite is a chest with an apprentice-leveled [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that triggers [poison darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") to shoot from the left across in front of the chest. To the right is a round wooden table holding three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") and a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Marksmanship Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Marksmanship_Lesson "Skyrim:The Marksmanship Lesson")*.

Dormitory

Through the door to the northeast is a semi-circular room that appears to be being used as a dormitory, with a cave-in near the bottom of a flight of stairs on your left. Among the rubble in the corners are a bottle of alto wine and a random potion. Opposite the door, against the inner wall is a set of shelves holding three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), five loose coins, a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), and two common books. To the right of this is a sideboard holding two potions of minor healing and a potion of minor magicka, with a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") to the right. Against the outer wall is a long wooden table holding a potion of minor healing, with a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") underneath. There are two dressers at this end of the room holding a bottle of Nord mead and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), seven beds and a bedroll along the walls with a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet"), another pair of leather boots and another pair of iron boots all next to separate beds. At the far end of the room, beyond a doorway into a circular room on the left are two cupboards holding nothing much of interest.

The circular room appears to be a dining hall with two long wooden tables and benches in the center and several round wooden tables and chairs arrayed around these. There are many portions of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat") around this room and on the floor by a closed wooden door to the northeast four portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") among several wooden bowls and plates. They are explained in a [cook's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Cook%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Cook's Journal") found later. The door leads to a kitchen area with a bandit found working and a fireplace complete with [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in a corner to the northwest. To the left of this is a set of shelves full of clutter. Against the southeast wall is a set of shelves filled with dog meat and seven [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). To the left of this is a sideboard with a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")* on top, and hanging above are three bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), and two bunches of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam").

To the northeast is another doorway into a corridor, with a firewood pile on the left with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against it, and a long wooden table on the right with a cook's journal that explains the grilled leeks on the floor, a small coin purse, and six loose coins. To the left is a set of shelves holding only common [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing") and footwear. Beyond this the corridor turns to the southeast and there is a bedroll by the wall. In front, this corridor is badly damaged with rubble heaped along both walls. There is a closed wooden door at the end of the corridor with a chain to the right.

#### Waterlogged Chamber

Waterlogged chamber

Upon opening the door there is a closed wooden gate behind, which is operated by the chain. There is a balcony beyond the gate with several barrels of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") on either side, a dead wolf in front, and stairs leading down to a lower level that is partially flooded. Opposite is another balcony with flights of stairs against the walls on either side. On this second balcony are two skeevers. In the eastern corner is an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") on top of a barrel, along the balcony are more barrels of food along with a pullbar on a stone pillar that overlooks the room, and in the southern corner on a crate is a random enchanted [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"). In the middle at the front is a pullbar that also operates the wooden gate opposite, if you have decided to work the other way around the interior. Under the first balcony is an area that can be reached from the lower level at either end, and in the middle of the southeast wall, under the water, is an unlocked chest. The room has many [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plants growing from the ceiling and walls. There is a short corridor to the southeast with a second dead wolf in the water at the start, which ends at a closed wooden door.

Fighting pit

This door leads into an area with a central caged area, which has a novice lock and contains two leveled wolves and benches all around, a table and chairs, a sideboard holding mead barrels, and a master-locked caged counter where the bandits seem to accept bets on the outcomes of the fights. Against the north wall are two cages; the first contains a dead [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Dark Elf (dead)") and has a novice lock, while the second is empty except for a bucket of dog meat and has a master lock. This implies that some of the fights aren't always just between wolves. The central pit area is splattered with blood and quite a bit has splashed the floor outside the cage. There are bales of straw in the eastern corner, on which is a small coin purse. There are several loose coins on the round table.

Cashier's cage

Inside the caged counter area is an unlocked chest with a small coin purse on the floor, and under the counter are seven coin purses of different sizes, a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), two steel arrows, a quiver of iron arrows, some loose coins, and a leveled healing potion. If you have started the quest [Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst_(quest) "Skyrim:Bloodthirst (quest)") [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"), you will also find the [Cage Bandit's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Cage_Bandit%27s_Note "Skyrim:Cage Bandit's Note") under the counter. On the countertop are more loose coins, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). There is a narrow corridor heading west with a few loose coins on the floor, which after a couple turns opens into a room with a bandit standing over a dead wolf on a table in the middle of the room; a second is patrolling between this half of the room and the other half to the left through a central gap. A third bandit is standing in the other part of the room, but will come running along with at least one wolf if alerted by fighting. There are an unlocked cage on your right containing a dead wolf, a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") in the corner to your left, and two long tables in front of you with a dead wolf, three common books, two random empty [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and an iron dagger on top. Behind this is a pressure plate that triggers a spike wall, and if you drop something on it, it enables you to walk behind it into an alcove containing a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer"), an adept-locked chest, and a lever that operates the spike wall. On the north wall is a novice-locked wooden door that opens to reveal a small alcove containing a set of shelves with a potion of minor healing, a potion of minor magicka, two potions of minor stamina, a leveled healing potion, a random potion, a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), and a common book.

Butchering a wolf

The second half of this room to the left contains, at the eastern end, an adept-locked cage containing a wolf, and opposite this are three sets of shelves holding an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), two pairs of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"), two pairs of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), a [leather helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"), three [wolf pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt"), and a woodcutter's axe. There is an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slicks "Skyrim:Oil Slicks") along the middle of the floor. In the middle of the southern wall is a master-locked wooden door, with an alcove behind it containing shelves filled with a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), two [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), and a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower. Two more apprentice-locked cages—one empty, one with a dead [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") inside—are to the right of this door. Opposite these are another two cages both adept-locked and containing wolves. There is a woodcutter's axe resting on a broken pillar in the center of this part of the room, and a partially flooded narrow corridor is found to the west with a couple samples of hanging moss growing from the ceiling. That corridor leads to a curved semi-circular room with the wooden gate you encountered shortly after entering and a sideboard against the wall opposite holding two bottles of wine and several empties. The room continues around to the left with a sideboard and wooden table against the east wall holding a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor") and a Nord mead. Against the west wall are a pair of unlocked cages guarded by a bandit.

To the south are some bales of straw with another woodcutter's axe leaning against them. To the west is a curving flight of stairs leading up, past a stone shelf holding two bottles of Nord mead. On the stairs are two pressure plates that trigger [spear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") that come from the outside wall; two bone chimes are also hanging from the ceiling. At the top of the stairs are a badly damaged landing and the second entrance from the other courtyard.

Once outside again, there is additional wooden door in the eastern tower, it is expert-locked, but opens using the key from the large tent. Passing the door there is a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), and one containing foodstuffs and a novice-locked chest. There are also stairs curving up to the top of the tower, where a campfire burns in the center with two small tents next to it, these do not have bedrolls inside. The path along the top of the wall leads to the west to another door in the bottom of the tallest tower. More curving stairs follow, with a pit wolf guarding them heading up. The top of the tower has had wooden platforms and stairs added; this is where the bandit boss will be located. They have a unique piece of dialogue (see [notes](#Notes)). There are a long wooden table holding a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a dresser on the first level, and more wooden stairs leading to high wooden platforms. On the next level there are a table where the boss is originally sitting and stairs up to the top level, which is roofed over and laid out as a bedroom with a double bed, dresser, cupboard, table and chair, and unlocked boss chest. On the dresser is an enchanted [two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") weapon. The cupboard holds three common books and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") skill book *[The Lunar Lorkhan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lunar_Lorkhan "Skyrim:The Lunar Lorkhan")*, with a pair of random enchanted boots to the right. On the table is a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill book *[Proper Lock Design](/wiki/Skyrim:Proper_Lock_Design "Skyrim:Proper Lock Design")*.

## Notes

- Most of the wolves in the fort are locked in cages, but will attack immediately. However, if you are sneaking and back away upon picking the lock, they will attack the bandits patrolling the interior.
- The bandit chief has a unique line of dialogue: *"So you're the one who's been down there killing all my wolves. You're gonna die for that!"*
- The highest tower can be tricky to find. Once you are in the exterior middle section of the fort (you can jump straight to this level from a pile of rubble outside the east wall), follow the north wall eastward then southward toward the lake down a short set of wooden stairs. At the base of the stairs, turn north, and you'll see a wooden door. The key for this door is on a long wooden table in a large tent near the top of the fort's exterior. A lit campfire is adjacent to the large tent.
- A [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is 210 feet north of the fort's tower, on the far side of the rocky area.
- Faldar's Tooth also [appears](/wiki/Online:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Online:Faldar's Tooth") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The key for the radiant prisoner cage is unobtainable, and the cage does not open with the Faldar's Tooth Key. To open the cage, it must be picked.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3, addresses this issue. The key for the radiant prisoner cage has been added to the alias inventory on the Boss NPC.

## Maps

- 

  Faldar's Tooth

Faldrin

**Faldrin** is a dead [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") fisherman who can be found in the first chamber up the stairs in [Alftand Ruined Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand#Alftand_Ruined_Tower "Skyrim:Alftand"). His [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman%27s_Journal_(Fishing) "Skyrim:Fisherman's Journal (Fishing)") can be found outside of [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave"). Some steps in the corridor behind him lies the body of another fisherman named [Jorid](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorid "Skyrim:Jorid").

## Related Quests

- **[Beneath Bronze Waters](/wiki/Skyrim:Beneath_Bronze_Waters "Skyrim:Beneath Bronze Waters")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Investigate the waters outside [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave").

Faldrus

**Faldrus** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [elemental mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental") who can be [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Dark_Elf_on_Pilgrimage_to_Azura.27s_Shrine "Skyrim:World Interactions") wandering in the wilderness. He is on a pilgrimage to the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura") and may point you to it.

When he arrives at Azura's shrine, he will join [Aranea Ienith](/wiki/Skyrim:Aranea_Ienith "Skyrim:Aranea Ienith") in front of the statue and raise his arms in praise. However, he will no longer provide further dialogue options.

## Related Quests

- **[Visit the Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Visit_the_Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Visit the Shrine of Azura")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").

## Dialogue

When near him, he will greet you with:

:   *"I'm on a pilgrimage to the Shrine of Azura, the Goddess of Twilight. If you'll excuse me."*
:   **Where is this shrine?**
:   *"In the mountains to the northeast. I'll mark it on your map."*

## Notes

- Even when he is at the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura"), he will give the same dialogue responses as he does when originally met and has no further dialogue.
- Faldrus does not have unique facial data. Instead, he uses the default male Dark Elf face, albeit with different hair.

## Bugs

- The location for the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura") may not get marked on your map, despite Faldrus saying that he will do so.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

Faleen

**Faleen** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") and the [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") of [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). She can be found in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"). [Another inhabitant](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") of the keep is romantically interested in her, as revealed in [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love"). If Igmund has been removed as the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Markarth, she can be found with him in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

She wears a full set of [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), including a pair of steel gauntlets ([steel Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets") or [steel Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Imperial_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Imperial Gauntlets") versions) and a pair of steel boots ([steel cuffed](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots") or [steel shin](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shin_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Shin Boots") versions). She is equipped with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") and a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield"), and carries a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") with twelve [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a random selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

When first approaching Jarl Igmund, Faleen will stop you in your tracks and say:

:   *"You. Who are you to approach the Jarl of Markarth?"*

:   **I'm a traveler. I have questions.**

:   **I'm looking for work.**

:   **I was looking to purchase a house in Markarth.**

Whichever option gets chosen, Faleen will reply by saying:

:   *"Very well, you may approach the Mournful Throne, but watch your words."*

However, should you choose to back away before answering, Faleen will instead say:

:   *"Nothing to say. Fine, but I'm watching you."*

When spoken to afterwards, she may say:

:   *"As his housecarl, Igmund's security is my chief concern."*
:   *"Igmund's father was killed by Forsworn. I won't rest until they've paid with their blood."*
:   *"Raerek is far too cautious, but I'll agree with him on any measure that keeps this city safe."*

When ending conversation, she might offer you a warning:

:   *"Keep your eyes open for Forsworn when you're on the roads."*

Should Markarth be taken over by the Stormcloaks, then Igmund and his court, including Faleen, will be exiled to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")'s [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"). Her greetings will become a lot more bitter as a result:

:   *"Igmund is alive, and I'll keep it that way, Jarl or not."*
:   *"You lay one finger on Igmund, and I'll end you Stormcloak."*

### The Book of Love

:   **I want to talk to you about Calcelmo.**
:   *"Calcelmo? What about him?"*

:   **He has feelings for you.**
:   *"What? You're out of your mind. That old coot's more interested in dead dwarves than anybody around here. Don't talk such rot."*

:   :   **It's true. He told me.**
    :   *"Please, stop wasting my time. You're embarrassing yourself."*

:   :   **You're right. I was probably mistaken.**
    :   *"Of course you were. Now stop wasting my time."*

:   **What do you think of him?**
:   *"Think of him? He's an odd little man. Always poking around the ruins and wasting time in his museum. Seems friendly enough. Obviously intelligent. Why do you ask?"*
:   **I was just curious.**
:   *"Well aren't you a strange one."*
:   **I have a poem I'd like you to read.**
:   *"Pardon me?"*
:   **It's from Calcelmo. Please.**
:   *"I'm not sure what this is all about.'*
:   **(Give poem)**
:   *"This is... lovely. Calcelmo wrote this... about me? I never knew he had such feeling in him."*
:   **He cares about you.**
:   *"Clearly. I've never even thought of him in that manner. I wish that I was as skilled with words as he. Here, take him this letter. I may not be as eloquent as he is, but I hope he understands."*

After giving Faleen's letter to Calcelmo, he'll seek her out and the following conversation will take place:

:   **Calcelmo**: *"Faleen... I..."*
:   **Faleen**: *"Sssh. It's all right. You don't need to say anymore. I had no idea you were so... nuanced."*
:   **Calcelmo**: *"I love you."*
:   **Faleen**: *"So I hear. Come here, you."*

### Conversations

She can be overheard discussing many topics with Igmund and Raerek:

:   **Igmund:** *"Raerek, how is The Reach faring against this Forsworn menace?"*
:   **Raerek:** *"Things are bad, Igmund. Our forces are barely able to keep the Forsworn in check. Merchants are reporting the loss of more of their shipments."*
:   **Igmund:** *"This is why I say we take the fight to them. Gather the Legion and drive those blasted beasts out of the Reach for good."*
:   **Faleen:** *"And what do Legion soldiers know about the hills the Reach? And the caves that make up those hills? The Forsworn can hide and ambush every assault."*
:   **Raerek:** *"The safety of the city and our settlements must be our only concern, Igmund. The rest of the Reach is on its own."*
:   **Igmund:** *"Cowards, the both of you. My father would not sit idly back and wait while evil men take over his lands. We're done discussing this for now."*

:   **Raerek:** *"My Jarl, we need to discuss Markarth's collapsing trade with the other Holds."*
:   **Igmund:** *"Of course there's a collapse in trade. The Stormcloaks stalk every road and the Forsworn attack every caravan."*
:   **Faleen:** *"Not to mention the rebels completely control Windhelm and all of Eastmarch hold."*
:   **Igmund:** *"Why do you pester me with battles we can't win? I need my steward to plan for victory, not nag me with every ill account."*
:   **Raerek:** *"Forgive me for worrying about the future of Markarth. The lifeblood of the city is gold, Igmund, and it doesn't stop beating because there's a war on."*
:   **Igmund:** *"Very well. I'll send the request for additional Legionaries to protect trade to the other Imperial holds. Hopefully, Solitude can spare more men."*

:   **Raerek:** *"Igmund, we need to talk about the Silver-Blood family."*
:   **Igmund:** *"What about them? They seem loyal enough."*
:   **Raerek:** *"Loyal? Thongvor supports Ulfric and his Stormcloaks! We should imprison the entire family as a precaution."*
:   **Faleen:** *"I second that, Igmund. Who knows what that family will do for power? They could be working with the Forsworn for all we know."*
:   **Igmund:** *"Enough! We can't imprison the very people who own the jail we would be throwing them into. The Silver-Bloods are to be left alone, am I clear?"*
:   **Raerek:** *"Yes, my Jarl."*
:   **Faleen:** *"Yes, my Jarl."*

## Unused Conversations

Originally, as part of the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") questline, there was going to be a siege of Markarth, very similar to the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)"). Upon reaching the throne room, you would be greeted as follows:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Faleen**: | *"That's close enough."* |
| **Igmund**: | *"He/She wants the city this badly, he/she can fight me for it."* |
| **Faleen**: | *"No, Igmund. It's too dangerous."* |
| **Igmund**: | *"I will not surrender Markarth without raising my own sword in her defense."* |
| **Faleen**: | *"Kill them all. Protect the Jarl at all costs!"* |

## Notes

- Faleen will always refer to you as "Stormcloak" when she's in exile, even if you haven't joined the Stormcloaks, and the city's turnover has been caused by [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). This is due to the dialogue checking whether or not she's in exile, and not the cause of said exile, as specific dialogue for different causes doesn't exist.

## Bugs

- If Faleen is the target of a radiant quest (such as [Hired Muscle](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Muscle "Skyrim:Hired Muscle")), you will be told to go Markarth even if she has relocated to the Blue Palace. However, the quest marker will point to the correct place.

Falion's House

**Falion's House** is the home of the town wizard in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").

The house is the residence and shop for the wizard [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") and his child apprentice [Agni](/wiki/Skyrim:Agni "Skyrim:Agni").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Agni](/wiki/Skyrim:Agni "Skyrim:Agni")  [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") [Spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Spells") [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Conjuration (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Conjuration (Master)") |

### Exterior

The house is located on the edge of the water behind the [Thaumaturgist's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaumaturgist%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Thaumaturgist's Hut"), along the jetty from [Alva's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Alva%27s_House "Skyrim:Alva's House") in Morthal. There is a covered porch along the front of the building and continuing around to the left. There are two wooden benches and a food barrel to the left of the front door. In the area to the left are two more wooden benches, a large pile of firewood and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone").

### Falion's House

Interior

This is a one-room home, from where Falion also sells his services and items. On your left upon entering is a long wooden table with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel beside it. On the table is a sample of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and four [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). Above the table, hanging from the ceiling are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and two bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the right of the table is a basket containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), with a hanging rack above holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)").

In the northwestern corner is a chair and against the north wall is a set of shelves holding copies of *[The Great War](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Great_War "Skyrim:The Great War")*, *[Azura and the Box](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura_and_the_Box "Skyrim:Azura and the Box")* and the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Catalogue of Armor Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Armor_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Armor Enchantments")*, as well as a [Draught of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Draught of Extra Magicka"), a [Potion of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), an [Enchanter's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Enchanter's Potion"), an [Enchanter's Draught](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Draught "Skyrim:Enchanter's Draught"), six bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two filled [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), two filled [common soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") and one empty common soul gem. The [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") become available for purchase from Falion once you have the [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") [skill perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Perks "Skyrim:Skill Perks"). There is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") in the northeastern corner.

Against the east wall is a single owned bed coming out from the wall, with a round wooden table holding two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Rain's Hand, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Rain%27s_Hand,_v4 "Skyrim:2920, Rain's Hand, v4")* to the left of the bed. In the middle of the east wall is a fireplace with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the mantelpiece and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand in front. To the right is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). Against the south wall is a square wooden table and two chairs. On the table are five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). In the southwestern corner, along the west wall is a second single owned bed with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of it.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase.

|  |
| --- |
| - **Potions**: 1 Draught of Extra Magicka, 1 Enchanter's Draught, 1 Enchanter's Potion, 1 Potion of Extra Magicka |

## Notes

- With [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed, if you ask [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") about [curing vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism#Curing_Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism"), she will go here and in a few days she will come back cured from being a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire").

# Skyrim:Falion's Secret

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Investigate [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion")'s curious activities.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") |
| Location(s): | Unmarked summoning circle [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-42888&y=78400&zoom=15&legacy=true) |
| Reward: | 200 gold |
| ID: | FreeformMorthalA |

Falion's mysterious destination

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note:** This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Follow [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") to his destination at 1am.
2. Ask Falion what he is doing at the summoning circle.
3. Report Falion to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").

### The Guardian

Falion is a master in [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"). While he enjoys the town of Morthal enough to set up a home and business, he seems ever wary of a lurking danger. His academic interests include vampirism and the undead; perhaps he is aware of more than he is letting on.

### The Suspicion

If you inquire around [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") about [the wizard in town](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion"), you are told that he seems to be up to something; specifically, that he goes out into the marsh in the middle of the night.
A conversation with [Agni](/wiki/Skyrim:Agni "Skyrim:Agni"), his ward and apprentice, reveals that she had a "bad dream" in which Falion went away and made "monsters" while she slept. Falion dismisses this as only a dream, and insists his talents are needed to "keep the town safe".

### Late Night Wanderings

If you wait near Falion's house until 1am, you can follow him as he heads out of town, past the mill, and northwest into the marshes. He journeys to what appears to be a summoning circle. This is the same summoning circle where you must meet him to cure your vampirism in [Rising at Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn"). Upon confronting him, he will demand that you leave him to his "work" and never speak to anyone about what you observed that night, although he won't reveal precisely what his work is. You can agree to keep quiet, or blackmail him for 200 gold. Regardless of your choice, you may then report him to the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") if you so desire:

| Jarl | **"He's casting spells out in the marsh in the middle of the night."** | **"Never mind. It's not important."** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Idgrod Ravencrone | *"Ah, so it is not just dreams then. I have seen this. I will see that it is dealt with. Thank you for bringing clarity."* | *"I see. If something does happen, you know where I am."* |
| Sorli the Builder | *"Is that so? Well, I'll make sure that's taken care of immediately. It's good that you brought this to my attention."* | *"Either this is some kind of a joke, or you're keeping something from me. Whichever it is, I don't like it."* |

### Reporting to the Jarl

After reporting Falion to the jarl, she will immediately find and confront him, threatening dire consequences for Falion if he continues his actions. (See [Bugs](#Bugs).) The scene differs depending on the current jarl - [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") or [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Idgrod Ravencrone** | **Sorli the Builder** |
| **Idgrod Ravencrone**: *"Falion, I am disappointed."*  **Falion**: *"What is the meaning of this?"*  **Idgrod**: *"You've been exploring places you shouldn't, and you know it."*  **Idgrod**: *"It stops at once, or else there will be consequences of an unpleasant nature. Do you understand?"*  **Falion**: *"I... Yes, I understand."* | **Sorli the Builder**: *"I'm told that you're up to something out in the marsh, Falion."*  **Falion**: *"What is the meaning of this?"*  **Sorli**: *"I don't even want to know what it is you've been doing."*  **Sorli**: *"It doesn't happen again, or else I'll have you thrown in jail. Clear?"*  **Falion**: *"I... Yes, I understand."* |

## Notes

- Despite the warning, Falion will continue to visit the summoning circle each night as usual, and the jarl will remain oblivious to his continued behavior.

## Bugs

- The scene fails to play, and the jarl will instead permanently follow Falion without interacting with him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  -  `setstage freeformmorthala 200` will complete the quest and release the jarl

Falion

**Falion** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerConjurationMaster "Skyrim:TrainerConjurationMaster") and resident wizard of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). He is a master level [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") and also sells magical equipment and spells at [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_House "Skyrim:Falion's House"). If you catch him at [a strange place](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_Secret "Skyrim:Falion's Secret") in the marsh from 1am to 5am, he will be ready to pay you gold to keep his night activity a secret. His curious activities also relate to his study of [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") and the undead, so should you ever require the service, Falion possesses the power to [cure vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn"), if you bring him a filled [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem").

As a scholar of Conjuration, he claims that he traveled the planes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"), and met [Daedra](/wiki/Lore:Daedra "Lore:Daedra") and even [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer"). While he was studying "life-extending magics" he met with several vampires, and contemplated becoming one of them, but in the end chose not to as it would put his apprentice [Agni](/wiki/Skyrim:Agni "Skyrim:Agni") in danger. He briefly taught at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), but left due to his hatred of the place. He moved to Morthal to further his research and to help keep the place safe. He has also been taking care of Agni after the loss of her parents and is training her as his apprentice. While she seems to trust him, most of the villagers are [wary of him](#Rumors) and think he is up to something sinister, though [Jarl Idgrod](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") ignores their complaints and supports his presence. Due to his dislike in town, it's not public knowledge that the local innkeeper at [Moorside Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Moorside_Inn "Skyrim:Moorside Inn") is his sister, [Jonna](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna").

He wakes at 8am to unlock his house and sell magical items and spells, interrupted by a three-hour nap at 3pm. He can be found wandering around the house, cleaning the place, using the arcane enchanter, sitting at a chair or [conversing](#Conversations) with Agni. At 8pm he locks the house and closes his business. He sleeps for one hour at midnight before he travels to a strange place north of Morthal, staying there for four hours. He returns home at 5am and goes to bed.

Falion wears [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0006b46c "Skyrim:Boots"), and is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). He carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Falion%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Falion's House") to his house, as well as a selection of [higher-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Falion's Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion%27s_Secret "Skyrim:Falion's Secret")**: Investigate Falion's curious activities.
- **[Rising at Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn")**: Track down Falion to rid yourself of [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism").

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

- Potions (req. [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk): 1 [Draught of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Draught of Extra Magicka"), 1 [Enchanter's Draught](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Draught "Skyrim:Enchanter's Draught"), 1 [Enchanter's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Enchanter's Potion"), 1 [Potion of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka")

| ~9 | Leveled [Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls") | Max 12 (12@75%) |

## Dialogue

Upon your first time approaching him, he may remark on your arrival:

:   *"You are new to Morthal. We have not spoken before. This is interesting."*

Once you engage in conversation with him, however, he will be less friendly:

:   *"If you stand before me to accuse me of sacrificing children, or eating the hearts of the dead, you may save your breath. Beyond that I seek only to be left alone to pursue my research."*

:   :   **Why would anyone accuse you of that?**
    :   *"The people of Morthal would much rather weave their own horrid tales about my life than simply ask me for the truth. If they choose to fear me in their ignorance, that is their choice. But it will not change what is true."*

:   :   **So then what do you do?**
    :   *"I keep to myself. I offer spells and scrolls to those who need them, and wisdom in Conjuration magic for those who wish to learn. Beyond that I seek only to be left alone to pursue my research."*

When you enter his house he will greet you:

:   *"If you are here to purchase, I have many spells available. Do come in."*
:   *"Welcome. There are many things here that cannot be found elsewhere."*

Normal greetings:

:   *"My talents are much needed here, in order to keep Morthal... safe."*
:   *"Morthal is a troubled place, and it is my duty to see it rest in peace."*
:   *"Please remain indoors at night. It is dangerous to go outside."*
:   *"The changes in Morthal are of little consequence to me. So long as the laws are upheld, I do not care who does the upholding."* (If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") take over Morthal)

Normal topics:

:   **Why set up shop in Morthal?**
:   *"As anyone will tell you, Morthal can be a dangerous place. My... talents... are useful here. I help maintain order, even if it goes unnoticed."*

:   **What can you tell me about the area?**
:   *"The marsh is treacherous. You would do well to not wander at night."*

:   **Can you teach me about Conjuration?**
:   *"You deal with powerful forces. Take care they do not overwhelm you."*

### Falion's Secret

Falion at the strange landmark

Between 1am and 5am, he can be found studying a curious place in the middle of the marsh. During this time, you can confront him by inquiring about what he is doing, though he'll be dismissive:

:   **What are you doing?**
:   *"What I am doing is none of your business! Why are you here? Did you follow me? I demand that you leave at once and never speak of this again."*

:   :   **Why should I keep this a secret?**
    :   *"It is none of your concern, I assure you. Just... Forget that you ever saw me here."*

:   :   **I want to know what it is you're up to.**
    :   *"I am under no obligation to tell you anything. Now, leave me at once and never mention that you saw me."*

Whichever option you chose, you can reply to Falion in two ways. The first one will net you 200 septims:

:   **If you want me to keep quiet, it's going to cost you.**
:   *"Is that so? I should have expected as much. Fine, I shall give you 200 gold, and you shall leave me in peace. Now go, leave me to my work."*

:   **Okay, I'll leave you alone.**
:   *"Thank you. I will not forget this."*

Despite what you've told him, you can still report to the jarl about this. Should you choose to rat out Falion to the jarl, she will permanently follow Falion without interaction, though [leftover dialogue](#Notes) in game data indicates that either jarl was supposed to confront the wizard.

### Rising at Dawn

If you're a vampire, asking innkeepers for rumors may yield the response, *"They say Falion of Morthal has studied vampires, [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and all matter of undead."* If you are a member of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), a group of vampire hunters, they will not be available for conversation and will instead direct you to Falion to cure yourself.

Speak to Falion and mention to him that you've heard he's an expert in vampirism:

:   **I've heard you're an expert in vampirism.**
:   *"I know many things. I have studied things beyond the reach of most humans, traveled the [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion") planes, seen things one should not see. I have met [Daedra](/wiki/Lore:Daedra "Lore:Daedra") and [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") and everything in between and I know enough to see a vampire where others would see a man."*

:   **How can you be so sure I'm a vampire?**
:   *"I met several of your kind during my studies of life-extending magics. I even considered becoming a vampire myself. In the end, vampirism would endanger my ward Agni which would defeat the intended purpose."*

:   **I'm looking for a cure.**
:   *"It is possible. I know of a ritual but I've never performed it. It requires a filled [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"). You will need to kill someone. When you have a gem and have filled it return to me and I will perform the ritual. I will bring life to your dead body, vampire."*
:   **How do I get a black soul gem?**
:   *"They are rare things, I have one I picked up during my research of the Oblivion realms but it is a precious item."*

:   **I want to purchase your black soul gem.**

If you try to purchase his black soul gem and have enough gold, he'll reply, *"I would not sell it to just anyone but I'll make an exception for you. The cost to replace the gem is quite high."* If you don't have enough gold he will refuse, saying, *"I believe this gem is worth more than you are at the moment."*

When you have filled your black soul gem, bring it to him and he will give further instructions:

:   *"Very well. Meet me at the summoning circle in the marsh at dawn. We shall banish the creature you have become."*

If you only have an unfilled black soul gem, he will instead remark:

:   *"Which is utterly useless at the moment. You need to fill it with a soul."*

Meet him at the usual place he travels to late in the night, which as he reveals turns out to be a summoning circle. Upon talking to him there, he will comment,

:   *"Good, you're here."*
:   **Let's get this over with.**
:   *"As you desire. Stand in the center of the circle."*

After standing in the circle:

:   *"I call upon Oblivion realms. The home of those who are not our ancestors. Answer my plea!
    As in death there is new life, in Oblivion there is a beginning for that which has ended.
    I call forth that power! Accept the soul that we offer!
    As the sun ends the night, end the darkness of this soul, return life to the creature you see before you!"*

Your vision will blur and fade to black, but it will return to normal and you will no longer be a vampire. Upon completion of the ritual Falion will tell you:

:   *"The ritual is complete."*

Ask him if you're no longer a vampire and he will confirm, *"You are human again. Like the rest of us."*

## Conversations

*"Have no fear. I believe it is within you to excel in your studies."*

Falion can be seen having random conversations with Agni, as outlined below. Here Falion's dislike for the College of Winterhold shows up again:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Agni**: | *"When I grow up, will I go to the College in Winterhold?"* |
| **Falion**: | *"No, I don't think that will be necessary."* |
| **Agni**: | *"But I'm learning about magic, and that's what they do there. Shouldn't I go?"* |
| **Falion**: | *"The College is not the only place to learn about magic."* |
| **Agni**: | *"But you went there, didn't you? Isn't that where you learned?"* |
| **Falion**: | *"I was there only for a short time. Much of what I have learned has been on my own. And I will teach you. You have no reason to go there."* |
| **Agni**: | *"But..."* |
| **Falion**: | *"That is enough."* |

He can be found explaining to her how concentration is important to casting spells:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Falion**: | *"Have you been working on your concentration?"* |
| **Agni**: | *"Yes sir, I have."* |
| **Falion**: | *"Good. Concentration is paramount when dealing with magical forces."* |
| **Agni**: | *"Why?"* |
| **Falion**: | *"Because an unfocused mind will almost certainly be obliterated. Destroyed by the forces you attempt to control and yield."* |
| **Agni**: | *"Oh."* |
| **Falion**: | *"Have no fear. I believe it is within you to excel in your studies. But you must learn to concentrate!"* |
| **Agni**: | *"Yes, sir."* |

They may talk about other matters as well:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Agni**: | *"I had a bad dream again last night."* | **Agni**: | *"Is it true that you kill deer and eat their hearts?"* |
| **Falion**: | *"Oh?"* | **Falion**: | *"What? Where did you hear such a thing?"* |
| **Agni**: | *"I dreamt that you went away. You made monsters."* | **Agni**: | *"I don't know. Someone in town said it."* |
| **Falion**: | *"It's just a dream, child. Nothing more."* | **Falion**: | *"It's not true, I assure you."* |
| **Agni**: | *"It was scary. It was like it was real!"* | **Agni**: | *"Okay."* |
| **Falion**: | *"Hush now. Think no more of it."* | **Falion**: | *"Don't believe everything you hear, child."* |

## Rumors

Due to his work involving magic and the undead, and the [Nords'](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") general dislike for magic, a few of Morthal's citizens have a low opinion of Falion. Some people even spread rumors about him eating deer hearts, something Agni asks him about. Upon your first time entering the town, you can find three Nords, [Benor](/wiki/Skyrim:Benor "Skyrim:Benor"), [Thonnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonnir "Skyrim:Thonnir"), and [Jorgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorgen "Skyrim:Jorgen") in front of [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall"). They are confronting [Aslfur](/wiki/Skyrim:Aslfur "Skyrim:Aslfur"), the town [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward"):

*"We've no need for wizards in our midst!"*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Jorgen**: | *"What's the Jarl going to do about it?"* |
| **Thonnir**: | *"How are we supposed to feel safe in our own homes?"* |
| **Aslfur**: | *"Please, enough already! I have told Igrod of your concerns. She'll look after you. Please, go back to your business."* |
| **Jorgen**: | *"We've no need for wizards in our midst!"* |
| **Thonnir**: | *"Morthal has enough problems as it is!"* |
| **Jorgen**: | *"Bah, it's no use. Let's get back to it then."* |

If you later speak to Aslfur and tell him that Morthal seems like a quiet little town, he will mention why the citizens seem suspicious of Falion: *"That's what many here wanted. A quiet life in a quiet place, without the noise or the trouble of a city. Now some worry this wizard, Falion, will foul it all up."* Inquiring Jarl Idgrod if there's some kind of trouble in Morthal will have her answer, *"That which is unknown can create unease, even fear. It is to be expected. Some fear our new resident wizard. As they grow to know him, they will accept him. Time will prove me right."*

You can also meet with Jorgen and ask him why he doesn't trust Jarl Idgrod. He will reply, *"How can I? She never speaks with us. She's allowed this wizard, Falion, to live in our midst practicing gods-know-what."* Similarly, Benor can be found saying to you, *"This isn't the time or place for magic, or whatever it is Falion does."* and *"You ask me, we'd be better off without that wizard in town."* Meanwhile, the jarl's son, [Joric](/wiki/Skyrim:Joric "Skyrim:Joric"), will tell you something about him, though very vaguely: *"It's Falion. He...He did it. I don't know what it was, but he did it."* Idgrod and Aslfur can be overheard discussing what Joric said:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Idgrod**: | *"What troubles you, husband?"* |
| **Aslfur**: | *"It's Joric. I fear his condition is worse. He calls out in his sleep sometimes. I've heard Falion's name. What does it mean?"* |
| **Idgrod**: | *"Joric will be what Joric will be. Give it time."* |
| **Aslfur**: | *"Still, I fear there is some connection."* |

They may also have another conversation:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Aslfur**: | *"Have you made a decision about Falion?"* |
| **Idgrod**: | *"What decision is there to be made? I allowed him to live here. I stand by that."* |
| **Aslfur**: | *"Yes, but there are concerns. Rumors that he's up to something."* |
| **Idgrod**: | *"We are all up to something, my dear. All is as it should be."* |

Jonna may also request the steward to help her brother:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Jonna**: | *"When are you gonna do somethin' to help Falion? Stop people sayin' things about him?"* |
| **Aslfur**: | *"You have to understand, his presence here has caused... Well, it's difficult for the people to get used to."* |
| **Jonna**: | *"They got used to Idgrod just fine, didn't they? So what's the difference?"* |
| **Aslfur**: | *"Yes, well. Perhaps you're right."* |

If you are at the College of Winterhold, you have the option to talk to [Phinis Gestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor"), also a Conjurer and one of Falion's former students. Ask him if there are many Conjurers outside the College, and he will say, *"Not within society, no. Many who practice within the school of Conjuration do so on their own, secretly. Falion is the only one I know who is public about what he does. He was once my teacher here, but left the College years ago."* Asking him why Falion left will have him reply, *"He didn't like the [Arch-Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren"). Hated dealing with him, hated having to answer to him. Falion said he hated what this place was becoming. So he just left. Aren found a note on his desk, and that was it. I understand he settled down in [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), and his presence there caused something of a problem."*

## Notes

- Some dialogue in game data indicates that either Jarl Idgrod or Sorli is supposed to confront Falion about his secret activities:

:   **Idgrod**: *"Falion, I am disappointed."*
:   **Falion**: *"What is the meaning of this?"*
:   **Idgrod**: *"You've been exploring places you shouldn't, and you know it. It stops at once, or else there will be consequences of an unpleasant nature. Do you understand?"*
:   **Falion**: *"I... Yes, I understand."*

:   **Sorli**: *"I'm told that you're up to something out in the marsh, Falion."*
:   **Falion**: *"What is the meaning of this?"*
:   **Sorli**: *"I don't even want to know what it is you've been doing. It doesn't happen again, or else I'll have you thrown in jail. Clear?"*
:   **Falion**: *"I... Yes, I understand."*

- In the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, the summary for him reads *"Falion is a Redguard. While his sister Jonna is accepted by the people of Morthal, Falion is looked at with fear and distrust. Falion has delved deep into the mysteries of Magicka and has become a master of the arts. He has settled in Morthal because he felt drawn to the location and wishes to remain relatively close to the College in Winterhold. He spends his time in his workshop and is the only person in the realm who knows how to cure vampirism. "*

- Falion carries a Black Soul Gem in his personal inventory. When carrying this, the merchant option will show 2 Black Soul Gems for sale.

## Bugs

- Despite being a wizard, Falion knows no spells.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.
